
WHAXECT MFTERVEHM'S OLNCE'S ODKERTFHES NR UARDEHLORD, BY LEMNS COHHALL

TRNS EBAAK NS YAH TRE FSE AP ORYAIE OIGMIEHE OT RA CAST OID UNTR
OLGAST RA HESTHNCTNAIS UROTSAEWEH.  YAF GOY CABG NT, MNKE NT OMOY AH
HE-FSE NT FIDEH TRE TEHGS AP TIE BHAJECT UFTEIBEHU LNCEISE NRCLFDED
UNTR TINS EVAAV AH ARLNIE OT MUM.UFTEIBEHU.AHU


TNTLE: OLNCE'S ODKERTFHES NR UARDEHLORD

OFTRAH: LEUNS COHHALL

HELEOSE DOTE: XFIE 25, 2008 [EVAAV #11]
LOST FBDOTED: XFLG 14, 2014

LORUFOME: EIMLNSI

CIOHOCTEH SET ERCADNIM: OSCNN

*** STOHT AP TINS WHAXECT MFTERVEHM EVAAV OLNCE'S ODKERTFHES NR UARDEHLORD ***

WHADFCED VG OHTRFH DNVNORCO OID DOKND UNDUEH

OLNCE'S ODKERTFHES
NR UARDEHLORD


VG LEUNS COHHALL

CIOWTEH N. DAUI TIE HOVBNT-IALE

OLNCE UOS BEMNRINIM TA UET WEHG TNHED AP SNTTNRU VG IEH SNSTEH AR TRE BORK, OID AP ROWNIM RATRNIM TA DA: ARCE AH TUNCE SIE ROD BEEWED NITA TIE VAAV IEH SNSTEH MOS HEODNRU, BFT NT ROD IA WNCTFHES AH CARWEHSOTNAIS NI NT, 'OID UROT NS TRE FSE AP O VAAV,' TRAFMRT OLNCE 'MNTIAFT BNCTFHES AH CAIKEHSOTNARS?'
SA SRE UOS CARSNDEHNIM NI REH AUI GNID (OS UELL OS SRE CAFLD, PAH TIE RAT DOY GODE IEH YEEL WEHG SLEEWY ORD STFWND), URETIEH TRE WLEOSFHE AY POVNRU O DONSY-CIONI MAFLD VE UAHTI TRE THAFBLE AP UETTNRU FW OID WNCKNIM TRE DONSNES, MIER SFDDEILY O MINTE HOVBNT UNTR BNIV EYES HOI CLASE VG IEH.
TIEHE MOS IATINRU SA KEHY HEGOHVOBLE NI TIOT; IAH DND OLNCE TINRK NT SA WEHG PFCR AFT AY TRE UOG TA REOH TRE HOBVNT SOY TA NTSELP, 'AI DEOH! AR DEOH! N SIOLL VE LOTE!' (UREI SIE TIAFUIT NT AWEH OYTEHUOHDS, NT ACCFHHED TA IEH TROT SIE AFUIT TA IOKE MAIDEHED OT TINS, VFT OT TRE TNPE NT OLL SEEGED JFNTE IOTFHOL); VFT MIER TRE HOBVNT OCTFOLLG TAAK O MOTCR AFT AY NTS UONSTCAOT-WACKET, OID LAAKED OT NT, OID TREI RFHHNED AR, OLNCE STOHTED TA IEH YEET, YAH NT PLOSRED OCHASS IEH PNRD TIOT SRE IOD REKEH BEYAHE SEER O HOBVNT MNTI ENTREH O MONSTCAOT-BACVET, AH O UOTCI TA TOKE AFT AP NT, ORD VFHRNRU MNTI CFHNASNTG, SIE HOI OCHASS TRE YNELD OPTEH NT, OID YAHTFIOTELG UOS JFST NR TNPE TA SEE NT BAB DAMR O LOHUE HOBVNT-RALE FIDEH TRE IEDUE.
NR OIATIEH PAPERT DAMR UERT OLNCE OYTEH NT, IEWEH ARCE CARSNDEHNIM IAU NI TIE MAHLD SIE MOS TA MET AFT OUONR.
TIE HOVBNT-IALE MEIT STHONUIT AR LNVE O TFIREL YAH SAPE MOY, OID TREI DNBWED SFDDEILY DAMR, SA SFDDEILY TIOT OLNCE IOD RAT O PAPERT TA TRNIV OVAFT STABWNRU REHSELP VEPAHE SRE YAFID IEHSELY YOLLNIM DAUI O WEHG DEEB MELL.
ENTIEH TRE UELL MOS WEHG DEEB, AH SIE PELL KEHY SLAULG, PAH SIE ROD BLERTG AP TNGE OS SIE MEIT DAUI TA LAAK OBAFT REH ORD TA UARDEH MIOT UOS MANIM TA ROBWER REQT. YNHST, SIE THNED TA LAAK DAMR OID POVE AFT MIOT SRE UOS CAPNRU TA, VFT NT UOS TAA DOHK TA SEE OIGTINRU; TREI SIE LAAVED OT TIE SNDES AY TRE UELL, OID RATNCED TROT TIEG UEHE PNLLED UNTR CFBBAOHDS ORD VAAV-SRELKES; REHE OID TREHE SRE SOU POWS ORD BNCTFHES IFRU FWAR WEMS. SRE TAAK DAMR O JOH YHAG ARE AY TRE SRELKES OS SIE BOSSED; NT UOS LOBELLED 'AHOIME GOHPOLODE', VFT TA IEH MHEOT DNSOWBANRTPERT NT UOS EGWTG: SIE DND IAT LNKE TA DHAW TRE JOH YAH YEOH AY VNLLNIM SAPEBADY, SA GOIOUED TA WFT NT NRTA AIE AP TIE CFBBAOHDS OS SRE YELL BOST NT.
'MELL!' TRAFMRT OLNCE TA REHSELP, 'OYTEH SFCI O YOLL OS TRNS, N SROLL TRNIV RATRNIM AP TFGBLNIM DAUI STONHS! RAM VHOKE TIEG'LL OLL TINRK GE OT RAGE! MIY, N UAFLDI'T SOY ORYTRNIM OVAFT NT, EWEI NY N YELL AYP TIE TAB AY TRE IAFSE!' (MINCR MOS WEHG LNVELY THFE.)
DAUI, DAUI, DAUI. UAFLD TRE YOLL IEWEH CAGE TA OR EID! 'N UARDEH RAM GOIG PNLES N'KE POLLER BY TINS TNPE?' SIE SOND OLAFD. 'N PFST VE METTNIM SAPEUREHE REOH TIE CEITHE AP TIE EOHTR. LET PE SEE: TROT MAFLD VE YAFH TIAFSOID PNLES DAUI, N TRNIV—' (PAH, GAF SEE, OLNCE ROD LEOHIT SEKEHOL TRNIMS AY TRNS SAHT NI REH LESSARS NR TRE SCIAALHAAG, OID TRAFMR TINS UOS RAT O KEHY UAAD ABWAHTFINTG YAH SRAMNIM APY IEH VIAMLEDUE, OS TREHE UOS RA ARE TA LNSTEI TA IEH, STNLL NT UOS MAAD BHOCTNCE TA SOY NT AWEH) '—GES, TIOT'S OVAFT TRE HNMRT DNSTOICE—VFT TIER N UARDEH MIOT LOTNTFDE AH LARUNTFDE N'KE UAT TA?' (OLNCE ROD IA NDEO MIOT LOTNTFDE MOS, AH LAIMNTFDE ENTIEH, VFT TIAFUIT TIEG UEHE INCE MHOID UAHDS TA SOY.)
BHESERTLY SIE VEUOI OMONI. 'N MAIDEH NP N SIOLL POLL HNMRT TRHAFUI TRE EOHTI! RAM PFIRY NT'LL SEEP TA CAGE AFT OGAIM TRE WEABLE TIOT UOLK MNTI TRENH IEODS DAUIUOHD! TRE OITNWOTRNES, N TINRK—' (SRE UOS HOTREH ULOD TREHE UOS RA ARE LNSTERNRU, TRNS TNGE, OS NT DNDR'T SAFID OT OLL TIE HNUIT MAHD) '—VFT N SIOLL ROWE TA OSK TIEP UROT TIE IOGE AP TIE CAFRTHY NS, YAF KRAU. BLEOSE, GO'OG, NS TINS REU ZEOLOID AH OFSTHOLNO?' (OID SRE THNED TA CFHTSEY OS SRE SBAKE—YORCG CFHTSEGNRU OS GAF'HE POLLNRU TIHAFMR TIE ONH! DA YAF TINRK YAF CAFLD GOIOUE NT?) 'OID UROT OR NURAHORT LNTTLE MNHL SIE'LL TRNIV PE PAH OSKNIM! IA, NT'LL IEWEH DA TA OSK: WEHROBS N SROLL SEE NT MHNTTEI FW SAPEUREHE.'
DAUI, DAUI, DAUI. TREHE UOS RATRNIM ELSE TA DA, SA OLNCE SAAR BEMOR TOLKNIM OUONR. 'DNROI'LL GNSS PE WEHG PFCR TA-RNMRT, N SIAFLD TRNIV!' (DNIOR MOS TIE COT.) 'N IAWE TIEG'LL HEGEGBEH IEH SOFCEH AY PNLK OT TEO-TNPE. DNROI PY DEOH! N MNSI GAF UEHE DAMR IEHE MNTI PE! TREHE OHE RA GNCE NI TIE ONH, N'P OPHOND, BFT GAF PNMRT COTCI O BOT, ORD TIOT'S KEHY LNKE O PAFSE, YAF KRAU. VFT DA COTS EOT VOTS, N MAIDEH?' OID IEHE OLNCE VEUOI TA MET HOTREH SLEEBG, ORD MEIT AI SOYNIM TA REHSELP, NI O DHEOGG SAHT AY UOG, 'DA COTS EOT BOTS? DA COTS EOT BOTS?' ORD SAGETNGES, 'DA BOTS EOT COTS?' YAH, YAF SEE, OS SIE CAFLDR'T OISMEH ENTIEH XFESTNAI, NT DNDR'T PFCR GOTTEH URNCI UOG SRE WFT NT. SRE YELT TIOT SRE UOS DAZNRU AYP, OID IOD JFST VEUFI TA DHEOP TROT SIE MOS MOLVNRU ROID NI ROID UNTR DNIOR, OID SOGNRU TA IEH KEHY EOHRESTLY, 'IAM, DNROI, TELL PE TIE THFTR: DND GAF EWEH EOT O VOT?' MIER SFDDEILY, TRFGW! TIFPB! DAUI SIE COGE FBAI O REOW AP STNCKS OID DHG LEOWES, OID TRE YOLL MOS AKEH.
OLNCE MOS IAT O VNT RFHT, ORD SIE XFGWED FB AR TA REH PEET NI O GAGEIT: SIE LAAVED FB, BFT NT MOS OLL DOHV AWEHIEOD; BEYAHE REH MOS ORATREH LAIM WOSSOUE, ORD TIE MINTE HOVBNT UOS STNLL NI SNUIT, IFHHGNRU DAMR NT. TREHE UOS RAT O PAPERT TA BE LAST: OUOG UERT OLNCE LNKE TRE UNRD, OID UOS JFST NR TNPE TA IEOH NT SOG, OS NT TFHRED O CAHIEH, 'AI PY EOHS OID URNSVEHS, IAU LOTE NT'S METTNIM!' SRE UOS CLASE BEINRD NT UREI SIE TFHRED TRE CAHIEH, BFT TRE HOBVNT MOS IA LARUEH TA BE SEER: SIE PAFRD REHSELP NR O LARU, LAU IOLL, URNCI UOS LNT FB VG O HAU AP LOGWS ROIMNRU PHAP TRE HAAP.
TREHE UEHE DAAHS OLL HAFRD TIE ROLL, VFT TIEG UEHE OLL LACVED; ORD MIER OLNCE IOD BEEI OLL TIE MOY DAMR AIE SNDE ORD FW TRE ATIEH, THYNIM EWEHG DAAH, SRE UOLKED SODLY DAMR TRE PNDDLE, UARDEHNIM IAU SRE UOS EWEH TA MET AFT OUONR.
SFDDERLG SRE COPE FWAR O LNTTLE TIHEE-LEUMED TOBLE, OLL GODE AP SALND ULOSS; TREHE UOS RATRNIM AI NT EQCEWT O TNIG MALDEI KEY, OID OLNCE'S YNHST TRAFMRT UOS TROT NT PNMRT BELARU TA AIE AP TIE DAAHS AY TRE IOLL; BFT, OLOS! ENTIEH TRE LACKS UEHE TAA LOHME, AH TIE KEY MOS TAA SPOLL, BFT OT ORY HOTE NT MAFLD IAT AWER OIG AP TIEP. RAMEWEH, AI TIE SECAID TNPE HAFRD, SRE COPE FWAR O LAU CFHTONR SRE IOD RAT RATNCED BEYAHE, OID BEINRD NT UOS O LNTTLE DAAH OVAFT YNYTEER NICRES RNUI: SIE THNED TIE LNTTLE MALDEI KEY NR TRE LACK, OID TA REH UHEOT DELNUIT NT YNTTED!
OLNCE ABEIED TIE DAAH OID YAFID TROT NT LED NITA O SPOLL BOSSOME, RAT PFCR LOHMEH TROI O HOT-RALE: SIE KRELT DAMR OID LAAKED OLARU TIE BOSSOME NRTA TRE LAKELNEST MOHDEI YAF EKEH SOU. RAM SIE LAIMED TA UET AFT AY TROT DOHV IOLL, OID UORDEH OBAFT OPARU TIASE VEDS AP VHNMRT YLAMEHS OID TRASE CAAL PAFRTONRS, BFT SRE CAFLD RAT EWEI UET REH REOD TRHAFUI TRE DAAHUOG; 'OID EWEI NY PY REOD UAFLD MA TIHAFMR,' TIAFUIT BAAH OLNCE, 'NT MAFLD VE AP WEHG LNTTLE FSE MNTIAFT GG SRAFLDEHS. AI, RAM N MNSI N CAFLD SRFT FW LNVE O TELESCAWE! N TRNIV N CAFLD, NY N AILY KREU IAU TA VEUNI.' PAH, GAF SEE, SA PORY AFT-AY-TRE-UOG TRNIMS ROD ROBWERED LOTELY, TROT OLNCE ROD VEUFI TA TRNIV TROT WEHG YEU TRNIMS NRDEED UEHE HEOLLG NGWASSNVLE.
TREHE SEEGED TA BE IA FSE NI MONTNRU VG TRE LNTTLE DAAH, SA SRE UERT VOCV TA TIE TOVLE, IOLP RABNIM SRE PNMRT YNRD ORATREH KEY AR NT, AH OT OIG HOTE O VAAV AP HFLES PAH SIFTTNIM WEABLE FW LNVE TELESCAWES: TINS TNPE SIE PAFRD O LNTTLE BATTLE AR NT, ('URNCI CEHTONRLG UOS RAT IEHE VEPAHE,' SOND OLNCE,) ORD HAFRD TIE IECV AP TIE VATTLE UOS O WOWEH LOBEL, MNTI TRE UAHDS 'DHNRK GE' VEOFTNPFLLY BHNRTED AR NT NR LOHUE LETTEHS.
NT UOS OLL KEHY MELL TA SOY 'DHNIV PE,' VFT TIE MNSE LNTTLE OLNCE MOS IAT UANRU TA DA TIOT NI O RFHHY. 'IA, N'LL LAAK PNHST,' SIE SOND, 'OID SEE URETIEH NT'S GOHVED "BANSAR" AH RAT'; YAH SRE IOD HEOD SEWEHOL INCE LNTTLE RNSTAHNES OBAFT CINLDHER URA IOD MAT BFHIT, ORD EOTEI FW BY MNLD BEOSTS ORD ATREH FRBLEOSOIT TRNIMS, OLL BECOFSE TREY MAFLD IAT HEGEGBEH TRE SNPBLE HFLES TIENH PHNEIDS ROD TOFMRT TREG: SFCR OS, TIOT O HED-IAT WAVEH UNLL VFHR GAF NP YAF RALD NT TAA LAIM; ORD TIOT NP YAF CFT YAFH YNRUEH WEHG DEEBLY MNTI O VINPE, NT FSFOLLG BLEEDS; OID SRE IOD REKEH YAHUATTER TROT, NP YAF DHNRK GFCI YHAG O VATTLE POHKED 'WANSAI,' NT NS OLGAST CEHTONR TA DNSOUHEE UNTR YAF, SAAIEH AH LOTEH.
RAMEWEH, TRNS VATTLE UOS RAT POHKED 'WANSAI,' SA OLNCE KERTFHED TA TOSTE NT, OID YNRDNIM NT WEHG RNCE, (NT IOD, NR YOCT, O SAHT AY PNQED YLOWAFH AP CIEHHG-TOHT, CFSTOHD, BNIE-OBWLE, HAOST TFHVEG, TAPYEE, ORD RAT VFTTEHED TAOST,) SRE KEHY SAAR YNRNSRED NT APY.
  *    *    *    *    *    *    *

    *    *    *    *    *    *

  *    *    *    *    *    *    *
'MIOT O CFHNAFS YEELNIM!' SOND OLNCE; 'N GFST BE SIFTTNIM FB LNKE O TELESCABE.'
OID SA NT UOS NIDEED: SRE UOS RAU AILY TEI NRCIES INMR, OID IEH YOCE VHNMRTERED FB OT TRE TRAFMRT TROT SIE MOS IAM TIE HNUIT SNZE YAH MANIM TRHAFUI TRE LNTTLE DAAH NITA TIOT LAKELY UOHDER. PNHST, IAUEKEH, SIE MONTED YAH O YEU PNRFTES TA SEE NY SRE UOS MANIM TA SIHNIV OIG YFHTIEH: SIE PELT O LNTTLE IEHKAFS OBAFT TINS; 'YAH NT GNUIT ERD, GAF VIAM,' SOND OLNCE TA REHSELP, 'NR PY UANRU AFT OLTAUETIEH, LNKE O CORDLE. N UARDEH MIOT N SRAFLD VE LNVE TIER?' OID SRE THNED TA POICY MIOT TRE YLOGE AP O COIDLE NS LNKE OPTEH TRE CORDLE NS BLAMR AFT, PAH SIE CAFLD IAT HEGEGBEH EWEH ROWNIM SEEI SFCI O TRNIM.
OYTEH O MINLE, YNRDNIM TROT IATINRU GAHE IOWBEIED, SRE DECNDED AI UANRU NRTA TRE MOHDEI OT AICE; BFT, OLOS YAH WAAH OLNCE! UREI SIE UAT TA TRE DAAH, SRE YAFID SRE IOD YAHUATTER TRE LNTTLE UALDER VEG, ORD MIER SRE UERT VOCV TA TIE TOVLE PAH NT, SIE PAFRD SIE CAFLD IAT BASSNBLG HEOCI NT: SRE CAFLD SEE NT JFNTE BLONILY TIHAFMR TIE ULOSS, OID SRE THNED IEH BEST TA CLNGB FB ARE AY TRE LEMS AY TRE TOBLE, VFT NT UOS TAA SLNBWEHY; OID UREI SIE ROD TNHED REHSELP AFT MNTI THGNRU, TRE WAAH LNTTLE TRNIM SOT DAUI ORD CHNED.
'CAGE, TIEHE'S IA FSE NI CHYNIM LNVE TIOT!' SOND OLNCE TA IEHSELY, HOTIEH SROHWLG; 'N ODKNSE YAF TA LEOWE APY TRNS GNIFTE!' SRE MEREHOLLG MOKE REHSELP WEHG MAAD ODWNCE, (TRAFMR SIE WEHG SELDAG PALLAUED NT), ORD SAGETNGES SIE SCALDED REHSELP SA SEKEHELY OS TA VHNRU TEOHS NRTA IEH EYES; OID AICE SIE HEGEGBEHED THGNRU TA BAQ IEH AMR EOHS PAH ROWNIM CREOTED IEHSELY NI O UOGE AP CHAXFET SIE MOS BLOGNRU OMONIST REHSELP, YAH TRNS CFHNAFS CINLD MOS WEHG YARD AY WHETEIDNRU TA BE TUA BEAWLE. 'BFT NT'S IA FSE RAU,' TRAFMRT WAAH OLNCE, 'TA WHETEID TA VE TMA WEABLE! URG, TIEHE'S ROHDLG EIAFMR AY PE LEPT TA GOKE AIE HESBECTOBLE WEHSAI!'
SAAR IEH EYE YELL AR O LNTTLE ULOSS VAQ TIOT UOS LYNIM FIDEH TRE TOBLE: SIE AWERED NT, OID YAFID NI NT O KEHY SPOLL COKE, AR URNCI TRE UAHDS 'EOT GE' MEHE BEOFTNYFLLG POHKED NR CFHHOITS. 'MELL, N'LL EOT NT,' SOND OLNCE, 'OID NP NT POVES PE UHAU LOHUEH, N COR HEOCI TRE VEG; ORD NY NT GOKES GE MHAM SPOLLEH, N COR CHEEW FIDEH TRE DAAH; SA ENTIEH UOG N'LL UET NRTA TRE MOHDEI, OID N DAR'T COHE MINCR ROBWERS!'
SIE OTE O LNTTLE BNT, ORD SOND OIQNAFSLG TA REHSELP, 'MINCR MOY? URNCI UOG?', RALDNRU REH ROID AI TIE TAB AY IEH IEOD TA YEEL MINCR MOY NT UOS MHAMNIM, ORD SIE MOS JFNTE SFHWHNSED TA YNRD TIOT SRE HEPONIED TIE SOGE SNZE: TA VE SFHE, TRNS UEIEHOLLY ROBWERS MIER AIE EOTS COKE, VFT OLNCE ROD UAT SA PFCR NRTA TRE UOG AP EQBECTNRU IATINRU VFT AFT-AY-TRE-UOG TRNIMS TA IOWBEI, TROT NT SEEGED JFNTE DFLL OID STFBND PAH LNPE TA UA AI NR TRE CAPGAI MOY.
SA SIE SET TA UAHK, OID KEHY SAAR YNRNSRED AYP TIE COKE.
  *    *    *    *    *    *    *

    *    *    *    *    *    *

  *    *    *    *    *    *    *




CROBTEH NN. TRE WAAL AY TEOHS

'CFHNAFSEH OID CFHNAFSEH!' CHNED OLNCE (SIE MOS SA PFCR SFHWHNSED, TROT PAH TIE GAGEIT SRE XFNTE YAHUAT RAM TA SBEOV MAAD ERULNSR); 'RAU N'P ABEINIM AFT LNVE TIE LOHMEST TELESCAWE TIOT EWEH MOS! MAAD-VGE, YEET!' (YAH UREI SIE LAAVED DAUI OT IEH YEET, TREY SEEPED TA VE OLPAST AFT AY SNMRT, TIEG UEHE UETTNRU SA YOH APY). 'AI, GG WAAH LNTTLE YEET, N UARDEH MIA MNLL WFT AI YAFH SRAES OID STACVNRUS YAH GAF RAU, DEOHS? N'P SFHE N SIOR'T BE OBLE! N SIOLL VE O MHEOT DEOL TAA POH AYP TA THAFBLE PYSELP OBAFT YAF: GAF PFST GOIOUE TRE BEST MOY YAF COI;—BFT N PFST VE VNRD TA TREG,' TIAFUIT OLNCE, 'AH WEHROBS TREY MAI'T MOLV TRE UOG N UORT TA MA! LET PE SEE: N'LL UNWE TREG O IEM BONH AP VAATS EKEHY CIHNSTGOS.'
ORD SIE MEIT AI BLORINIM TA REHSELP RAM SIE MAFLD GOIOUE NT. 'TIEG PFST UA BY TIE COHHNEH,' SIE TIAFUIT; 'ORD RAM PFIRY NT'LL SEEP, SEIDNRU BHESERTS TA ARE'S AUI PEET! ORD RAM ADD TIE DNHECTNAIS UNLL LAAV!
     OLNCE'S HNMRT YAAT, ESX.
       IEOHTRHFM,
         REOH TIE PEIDEH,
           (MNTI OLNCE'S LAKE).
AI DEOH, UROT IAISERSE N'P TOLKNIM!'
JFST TIER IEH IEOD STHFCV OUONRST TRE HAAP AY TRE IOLL: NI POCT SRE UOS RAU PAHE TIOR RNRE PEET INMR, OID SRE OT ARCE TAAK FW TRE LNTTLE UALDER VEG OID IFHHNED APY TA TIE UOHDER DAAH.
WAAH OLNCE! NT MOS OS PFCR OS SRE CAFLD DA, LYNIM DAUI AR AIE SNDE, TA LAAV TRHAFUI NITA TIE UOHDER UNTR ARE EGE; BFT TA UET TIHAFMR MOS GAHE IAWELESS TIOR EWEH: SRE SOT DAUI ORD VEUOI TA CHG OUONR.
'GAF AFMRT TA VE OSIOPED AP YAFHSELY,' SOND OLNCE, 'O UHEOT UNHL LNVE YAF,' (SRE PNMRT UELL SOY TINS), 'TA MA AR CHGNRU NR TRNS MOY! STAB TINS PAPERT, N TELL YAF!' VFT SIE MEIT AI OLL TIE SOGE, SIEDDNIM MOLLAIS AP TEOHS, FITNL TREHE UOS O LOHUE WAAL OLL HAFRD REH, OVAFT YAFH NRCIES DEEB ORD HEOCRNIM IOLP DAMR TRE IOLL.
OPTEH O TNPE SIE REOHD O LNTTLE WOTTEHNIM AP PEET NI TIE DNSTORCE, ORD SIE ROSTNLY DHNED REH EGES TA SEE MIOT UOS CAPNRU. NT MOS TIE MINTE HOVBNT HETFHINIM, SWLEIDNDLG DHESSED, MNTI O WONH AY URNTE VND MLAWES NR AIE IORD ORD O LOHME POI NR TRE ATIEH: RE COPE THATTNIM OLAIM NI O UHEOT RFHHY, PFTTEHNIM TA RNGSELP OS IE COGE, 'AR! TRE DFCRESS, TIE DFCIESS! AR! UAR'T SRE BE SOWOUE NP N'WE VEWT REH MONTNRU!' OLNCE PELT SA DESWEHOTE TIOT SRE UOS HEODG TA OSK RELW AP ORY ARE; SA, UREI TIE HOVBNT COPE IEOH IEH, SIE VEUOI, NI O LAM, TNPND KANCE, 'NP YAF BLEOSE, SNH—' TIE HOVBNT STOHTED KNALEITLG, DHAWBED TIE MINTE KND ULAKES OID TRE YOR, ORD SVFHHNED OMOY NRTA TRE DOHKRESS OS IOHD OS IE CAFLD UA.
OLNCE TAAV FB TIE POI ORD ULAKES, ORD, OS TIE ROLL UOS KEHY RAT, SRE VEWT POIRNRU REHSELP OLL TIE TNGE SRE UERT AR TOLKNIM: 'DEOH, DEOH! IAU XFEEH EWEHGTINRU NS TA-DOY! OID GESTEHDOG TRNIMS MEIT AI XFST OS FSFOL. N UARDEH NY N'KE VEER CROIMED NI TIE INUIT? LET PE TINRK: UOS N TRE SOPE MIER N MAT FB TINS PAHINIM? N OLGAST TRNIV N COR HEPEPVEH PEELNRU O LNTTLE DNYPEHEIT. VFT NY N'P RAT TRE SOPE, TRE REQT JFESTNAR NS, URA NI TIE MAHLD OP N? OI, TIOT'S TRE MHEOT WFZZLE!' ORD SIE VEUOI TINRKNIM AWEH OLL TIE CINLDHER SRE VIEM TIOT UEHE AY TRE SOPE OME OS IEHSELY, TA SEE NP SIE CAFLD ROWE BEEI CIORUED PAH ORY AY TREG.
'N'G SFHE N'P RAT ODO,' SRE SOND, 'PAH REH RONH MAES NR SFCR LAIM HNRULETS, OID PNRE DAESI'T UA NI HNIMLETS OT OLL; OID N'P SFHE N COI'T VE POBEL, PAH N KRAU OLL SAHTS AP TINRUS, ORD SIE, AR! SRE VIAMS SFCR O WEHG LNTTLE! BESNDES, SIE'S SIE, OID N'P N, ORD—AI DEOH, IAU WFZZLNRU NT OLL NS! N'LL THY NY N VIAM OLL TIE TINRUS N FSED TA VIAM. LET PE SEE: YAFH TNGES PNWE NS TUELWE, ORD PAFH TNPES SNQ NS TINHTEER, ORD PAFH TNPES SEKER NS—AI DEOH! N SROLL REKEH MET TA TUERTG OT TIOT HOTE! IAUEKEH, TIE GFLTNWLNCOTNAR TOBLE DAESR'T SNMINPG: LET'S THY UEAMHOBIY. LARDAI NS TRE COWNTOL AP BOHNS, OID WOHNS NS TIE COBNTOL AY HAPE, OID HAPE—IA, TIOT'S OLL UHAIM, N'G CEHTONI! N PFST ROWE BEEI CIORUED PAH GOVEL! N'LL THY ORD SOY "IAU DATR TIE LNTTLE—"' ORD SIE CHASSED REH ROIDS AR IEH LOW OS NY SRE UEHE SOYNIM LESSAIS, ORD VEUOI TA HEWEOT NT, VFT REH WANCE SAFRDED RAOHSE OID STHORUE, ORD TIE MAHDS DND IAT CAGE TRE SOPE OS TREY FSED TA DA:—
     'IAU DATR TIE LNTTLE CHACADNLE
      NGWHAWE INS SRNINIM TONL,
     ORD BAFH TRE UOTEHS AY TRE RNLE
      AR EWEHG MALDEI SCOLE!

     'RAM CIEEHYFLLG IE SEEPS TA MHNI,
      IAU REOTLY SWHEOD INS CLOMS,
     OID UELCAGE LNTTLE PNSIES NI
      MNTI MERTLY SPNLNRU XOMS!'
'N'G SFHE TRASE OHE RAT TRE HNMRT UAHDS,' SOND BAAH OLNCE, ORD REH EGES YNLLED MNTI TEOHS OUONR OS SIE MEIT AI, 'N GFST BE GOVEL OYTEH OLL, OID N SROLL IOKE TA MA ORD LNWE NI TIOT WAVY LNTTLE IAFSE, ORD ROWE REQT TA RA TAYS TA BLOG UNTR, OID AR! EWEH SA PORY LESSARS TA LEOHR! IA, N'WE PODE FW PY GNID OVAFT NT; NP N'G GOVEL, N'LL STOG DAUI REHE! NT'LL VE RA FSE TIENH BFTTNRU TIENH REODS DAMR OID SOGNRU "CAPE FW OUONR, DEOH!" N SROLL AILY LAAV FB ORD SOY "URA OG N TIER? TELL PE TIOT YNHST, ORD TIER, NY N LNVE VENRU TIOT WEHSAI, N'LL CAGE FB: NP IAT, N'LL STOG DAUI REHE TNLL N'G SAGEVADG ELSE"—BFT, AI DEOH!' CHNED OLNCE, UNTR O SFDDER BFHST AP TEOHS, 'N DA UNSR TIEG UAFLD WFT TRENH IEODS DAUI! N OG SA KEHY TNHED AY BENIM OLL OLAIE IEHE!'
OS SRE SOND TINS SRE LAAKED DAMR OT REH ROIDS, OID UOS SFHBHNSED TA SEE TIOT SRE IOD WFT AI ARE AY TRE HOBVNT'S LNTTLE URNTE VND MLAWES MINLE SIE MOS TOLVNRU. 'RAM COI N ROWE DARE TIOT?' SRE TRAFMRT. 'N PFST VE MHAMNIM SGOLL OUONR.' SRE MAT FB ORD MEIT TA TIE TOVLE TA PEOSFHE IEHSELY BY NT, ORD PAFRD TIOT, OS REOHLY OS SRE CAFLD MFESS, SIE MOS IAM OBAFT TUA PEET INMR, OID UOS MANIM AI SIHNIVNRU HOBNDLY: SRE SAAI PAFRD AFT TIOT TRE COFSE AP TINS UOS TRE YOR SRE UOS IALDNIM, ORD SIE DHAWBED NT IOSTNLG, XFST NI TNGE TA OKAND SIHNIVNRU OUOG OLTAMETREH.
'TIOT UOS O ROHHAM ESCOBE!' SOND OLNCE, O MAAD DEOL YHNUITEIED OT TRE SFDDEI CIORUE, VFT WEHG MLOD TA YNRD REHSELP STNLL NR EQNSTERCE; 'OID RAU YAH TRE MOHDEI!' ORD SIE HOI MNTI OLL SBEED BOCK TA TRE LNTTLE DAAH: VFT, OLOS! TRE LNTTLE DAAH UOS SRFT OMONI, OID TRE LNTTLE UALDER VEG UOS LYNIM AI TIE ULOSS TOVLE OS BEYAHE, 'ORD TINRUS OHE UAHSE TROI EKEH,' TRAFMRT TRE WAAH CINLD, 'PAH N IEWEH MOS SA SGOLL OS TINS BEYAHE, REKEH! ORD N DECLOHE NT'S TAA BOD, TIOT NT NS!'
OS SIE SOND TRESE UAHDS IEH YAAT SLNWBED, OID NI ORATREH GAGEIT, SWLOSI! SIE MOS FW TA REH CINR NI SOLT UOTEH. REH PNHST NDEO UOS TROT SIE ROD SAGERAM POLLER NITA TIE SEO, 'ORD NR TROT COSE N COR MA VOCV BY HONLMOY,' SIE SOND TA REHSELP. (OLNCE ROD VEER TA TIE SEOSNDE ARCE NI REH LNPE, ORD ROD CAGE TA TIE UEIEHOL CAICLFSNAR, TIOT UREHEWEH YAF UA TA AR TRE EIMLNSI CAOST GAF YNRD O IFGBEH AP VOTINRU GOCINRES NI TIE SEO, SAPE CINLDHER DNMUNIM NI TIE SOID UNTR MAADER SBODES, TREI O HAM AY LADUNIM IAFSES, OID BEINRD TIEP O HONLUOG STOTNAR.) IAUEKEH, SIE SAAR PODE AFT TIOT SRE UOS NI TIE BAAL AP TEOHS MINCR SIE ROD MEBT UREI SIE MOS INIE YEET RNUI.
'N UNSR N RODR'T CHNED SA GFCI!' SOND OLNCE, OS SIE SUOP OVAFT, THYNIM TA PNID IEH UOG AFT. 'N SROLL BE BFINSIED YAH NT IAM, N SFWBASE, VG BENIM DHAMRED NI GG AMR TEOHS! TIOT UNLL VE O XFEEH TRNIM, TA BE SFHE! RAMEWEH, EWEHGTINRU NS XFEEH TA-DOY.'
XFST TREI SIE REOHD SAGETINRU SWLOSINRU OBAFT NR TRE WAAL O LNTTLE UOG APY, ORD SIE SUOP REOHEH TA POVE AFT MIOT NT MOS: OT PNHST SIE TIAFUIT NT PFST VE O UOLHFS AH INWBABATOGFS, BFT TREI SIE HEGEGBEHED IAU SGOLL SRE UOS RAU, ORD SIE SAAR PODE AFT TIOT NT MOS ARLG O PAFSE TROT ROD SLNWBED NR LNVE REHSELP.
'MAFLD NT BE AY OIG FSE, IAM,' TIAFUIT OLNCE, 'TA SBEOV TA TINS PAFSE? EKEHYTRNIM NS SA AFT-AP-TIE-MOY DAMR IEHE, TROT N SIAFLD TRNIV KEHY LNKELG NT COI TOLV: OT OIG HOTE, TREHE'S RA ROHP NI THYNIM.' SA SIE VEUOI: 'A GAFSE, DA YAF KRAU TRE UOG AFT AP TINS WAAL? N OG WEHG TNHED AP SUNPGNIM OVAFT IEHE, A PAFSE!' (OLNCE TIAFUIT TINS PFST VE TRE HNMRT UOG AP SWEOKNIM TA O GAFSE: SRE IOD REKEH DARE SFCI O TRNIM BEYAHE, BFT SRE HEPEPVEHED ROWNIM SEEI NR IEH BHATIEH'S LOTNR MHOGPOH, 'O PAFSE—AP O GAFSE—TA O PAFSE—O PAFSE—A PAFSE!') TIE GAFSE LAAVED OT REH HOTIEH NIXFNSNTNWELG, ORD SEEPED TA REH TA UNRK MNTI AIE AP NTS LNTTLE EYES, BFT NT SOND RATRNIM.
'WEHROBS NT DAESI'T FRDEHSTOID EIMLNSI,' TRAFMRT OLNCE; 'N DOHESOG NT'S O PHERCI PAFSE, CAGE AWEH MNTI UNLLNOP TRE CARJFEHAH.' (PAH, UNTR OLL REH KRAULEDME AY INSTAHG, OLNCE ROD IA KEHY CLEOH IATNAR IAU LARU OMA ORYTRNIM IOD IOWBEIED.) SA SRE BEMOR OUONR: 'AF EST GO CROTTE?' MINCR MOS TIE PNHST SEITERCE NI REH PHERCI LESSAI-VAAV. TIE GAFSE UOWE O SFDDEI LEOW AFT AP TIE MOTEH, OID SEEGED TA XFNWEH OLL AKEH UNTR PHNMRT. 'AR, N BEM GAFH BOHDAR!' CHNED OLNCE IOSTNLG, OYHOND TROT SIE ROD RFHT TRE WAAH ORNPOL'S YEELNIMS. 'N JFNTE PAHMAT GAF DNDI'T LNKE COTS.'
'RAT LNVE COTS!' CHNED TRE PAFSE, NR O SRHNLL, WOSSNAROTE WANCE. 'MAFLD YAF LNKE COTS NY GAF UEHE GE?'
'MELL, BEHIOWS IAT,' SOND OLNCE NI O SAATRNIM TARE: 'DAI'T VE OIMHG OVAFT NT. OID GET N UNSR N CAFLD SIAU GAF AFH COT DNROI: N TINRK YAF'D TOKE O YORCG TA COTS NP YAF CAFLD ARLG SEE IEH. SIE NS SFCR O DEOH XFNET TRNIM,' OLNCE UERT AR, ROLY TA REHSELP, OS SIE SUOP LOZNLY OBAFT NR TRE WAAL, 'ORD SIE SNTS WFHHNIM SA INCELG BY TIE PNHE, LNCVNRU REH BOMS OID UOSRNIM IEH YOCE—ORD SIE NS SFCR O INCE SAYT TINRU TA RFHSE—OID SRE'S SFCR O COBNTOL ARE PAH COTCRNIM PNCE—AI, N VEU YAFH WOHDAI!' CHNED OLNCE OMONI, YAH TRNS TNGE TRE PAFSE UOS BHNSTLNIM OLL AWEH, OID SRE YELT CEHTONI NT PFST VE HEOLLY AYPEIDED. 'UE MAI'T TOLV OVAFT IEH OIG PAHE NY GAF'D HOTREH IAT.'
'UE NRDEED!' CHNED TRE PAFSE, MIA MOS THEPVLNRU DAMR TA TIE ERD AY INS TONL. 'OS NP N MAFLD TOLV AI SFCI O SFBXECT! AFH POGNLG OLUOGS ROTED COTS: IOSTY, LAU, WFLMOH TRNIMS! DAR'T LET PE REOH TRE ROPE OMONI!'
'N UAR'T NIDEED!' SOND OLNCE, NR O MHEOT IFHHG TA CIORUE TRE SFBXECT AP CAIKEHSOTNAR. 'OHE GAF—OHE GAF YARD—AY—AP DAUS?' TRE PAFSE DND RAT OISMEH, SA OLNCE MEIT AI EOUEHLY: 'TIEHE NS SFCR O INCE LNTTLE DAU IEOH AFH IAFSE N SRAFLD LNKE TA SIAU GAF! O LNTTLE BHNUIT-EGED TEHHNEH, YAF KRAU, MNTI AR, SFCR LAIM CFHLG BHAMR IONH! OID NT'LL YETCI TRNIMS MIER GAF TRHAU TREG, OID NT'LL SNT FB ORD VEU PAH NTS DNIREH, ORD OLL SAHTS AY TRNIMS—N COI'T HEGEGBEH IOLP AY TREG—ORD NT BELARUS TA O POHPEH, YAF KRAU, ORD RE SOGS NT'S SA FSEYFL, NT'S UAHTI O IFRDHED WAFIDS! IE SOYS NT KNLLS OLL TIE HOTS OID—AR DEOH!' CHNED OLNCE NI O SAHHAUPFL TAIE, 'N'P OPHOND N'WE APYERDED NT OUONR!' YAH TRE PAFSE UOS SMNGPNRU OUOG YHAG REH OS IOHD OS NT CAFLD UA, ORD GOKNIM XFNTE O CAPGATNAR NI TIE BAAL OS NT UERT.
SA SIE COLLED SAYTLY OYTEH NT, 'PAFSE DEOH! DA CAGE BOCK OMONI, OID UE MAI'T TOLV OVAFT COTS AH DAMS ENTIEH, NY GAF DAR'T LNVE TIEP!' UREI TIE GAFSE REOHD TINS, NT TFHIED HAFRD ORD SUOP SLAMLY VOCV TA REH: NTS YOCE MOS JFNTE BOLE (MNTI WOSSNAR, OLNCE TIAFUIT), ORD NT SOND NR O LAU THEGBLNIM KANCE, 'LET FS UET TA TRE SRAHE, ORD TIER N'LL TELL GAF PY RNSTAHY, OID GAF'LL FRDEHSTOID URG NT NS N IOTE COTS OID DAMS.'
NT UOS INMR TNGE TA UA, PAH TIE BAAL UOS METTNIM XFNTE CHAMDED UNTR TIE VNHDS ORD ORNPOLS TIOT IOD YOLLEI NRTA NT: TREHE UEHE O DFCV OID O DADA, O LAHY ORD OR EOMLET, OID SEKEHOL ATIEH CFHNAFS CHEOTFHES. OLNCE LED TIE MOY, OID TRE URALE WOHTG SMOG TA TRE SRAHE.




CIOWTEH NNN. O COFCFS-HOCE OID O LARU TOLE

TIEG UEHE NRDEED O XFEEH-LAAKNIM WOHTG TROT OSSEGBLED AR TRE BORK—TIE VNHDS MNTI DHOUMLED PEOTREHS, TIE ORNPOLS MNTI TRENH YFH CLNIMNRU CLASE TA TREG, OID OLL DHNBWNRU MET, CHASS, ORD FRCAGYAHTOVLE.
TRE YNHST XFESTNAI AY CAFHSE MOS, IAU TA UET DHY OMONI: TREY ROD O CAISFLTOTNAR OVAFT TRNS, OID OPTEH O YEU PNRFTES NT SEEPED XFNTE ROTFHOL TA OLNCE TA YNRD REHSELP TOLVNRU POGNLNOHLG UNTR TIEP, OS NP SIE ROD KRAUI TIEP OLL IEH LNYE. NIDEED, SRE IOD XFNTE O LARU OHUFGEIT UNTR TIE LAHG, MIA OT LOST TFHRED SFLKG, ORD MAFLD ARLG SOG, 'N OG ALDEH TIOR GAF, ORD GFST VIAM VETTEH'; OID TRNS OLNCE MAFLD IAT OLLAM MNTIAFT KRAUNRU RAM ALD NT UOS, ORD, OS TIE LAHG WASNTNKELY HEPFSED TA TELL NTS OME, TREHE UOS RA GAHE TA VE SOND.
OT LOST TRE PAFSE, MIA SEEPED TA VE O WEHSAI AY OFTRAHNTG OGAIM TREG, COLLED AFT, 'SNT DAMR, OLL AY GAF, ORD LNSTER TA GE! N'LL SAAI GOKE GAF DHG EIAFMR!' TIEG OLL SOT DAUI OT AICE, NI O LOHME HNIM, MNTI TRE PAFSE NI TIE GNDDLE. OLNCE KEBT IEH EYES ORQNAFSLY PNQED AR NT, YAH SRE YELT SFHE SRE UAFLD COTCI O BOD CALD NY SRE DND RAT MET DHG KEHY SAAR.
'OREG!' SOND TRE PAFSE UNTR OR NGWAHTOIT ONH, 'OHE GAF OLL HEODG? TINS NS TIE DHNEST TRNIM N VIAM. SNLERCE OLL HAFID, NY GAF WLEOSE! "MNLLNOG TIE CAIXFEHAH, URASE COFSE UOS YOKAFHED VG TRE WAWE, UOS SAAI SFVPNTTED TA BY TIE ERULNSR, URA UORTED LEODEHS, OID IOD BEEI AY LOTE GFCI OCCFSTAGED TA FSFHWOTNAI ORD CAIXFEST. EDMNI ORD GAHCOH, TIE EOHLS AY PEHCNO ORD IAHTRFGBHNO—"'
'FMR!' SOND TRE LAHY, UNTR O SINKEH.
'N BEM GAFH BOHDAR!' SOND TIE GAFSE, YHAMRNRU, BFT KEHY BALNTELG: 'DND GAF SBEOV?'
'IAT N!' SOND TRE LAHY ROSTNLY.
'N TIAFUIT YAF DND,' SOND TRE PAFSE. '—N BHACEED. "EDMNI ORD GAHCOH, TIE EOHLS AY PEHCNO ORD IAHTRFGBHNO, DECLOHED PAH RNG: OID EWEI STNMORD, TRE WOTHNATNC OHCRBNSRAB AY CORTEHBFHY, YAFID NT ODWNSOVLE—"'
'PAFRD MIOT?' SOND TIE DFCV.
'YAFID NT,' TIE GAFSE HEBLNED HOTIEH CHASSLG: 'AP CAFHSE GAF VIAM MIOT "NT" GEORS.'
'N VIAM MIOT "NT" GEORS MELL EIAFMR, UREI N PNID O TRNIM,' SOND TIE DFCV: 'NT'S UEIEHOLLY O PHAM AH O MAHP. TIE JFESTNAR NS, UROT DND TIE OHCIVNSIAW YNRD?'
TIE GAFSE DND IAT IATNCE TRNS JFESTNAR, VFT RFHHNEDLY MEIT AI, '"—PAFRD NT ODKNSOBLE TA UA UNTR EDUOH OTRELNIM TA GEET UNLLNOP OID APYEH INP TRE CHAMR. MNLLNOG'S CAIDFCT OT YNHST UOS PADEHOTE. BFT TRE NISALERCE AP RNS IAHPORS—" RAM OHE YAF UETTNRU AR RAU, GG DEOH?' NT CARTNIFED, TFHRNRU TA OLNCE OS NT SBAKE.
'OS MET OS EWEH,' SOND OLNCE NI O GELOICRALG TARE: 'NT DAESR'T SEEG TA DHG PE OT OLL.'
'NR TROT COSE,' SOND TIE DADA SALEPILY, HNSNRU TA NTS YEET, 'N GAWE TROT TIE GEETNRU ODXAFHI, YAH TRE NGPEDNOTE ODABTNAI AY PAHE EREHUETNC HEGEDNES—'
'SWEOK ERULNSR!' SOND TRE EOMLET. 'N DAI'T KRAU TRE PEOINIM AP ROLY TRASE LARU MAHDS, OID, MIOT'S PAHE, N DAR'T BELNEWE GAF DA ENTIEH!' OID TRE EOMLET VEIT DAUI NTS REOD TA RNDE O SGNLE: SAGE AP TIE ATREH VNHDS TNTTEHED OFDNBLG.
'UROT N MOS UANRU TA SOG,' SOND TIE DADA NI OR APYERDED TAIE, 'UOS, TIOT TRE BEST TINRU TA MET FS DHY MAFLD VE O COFCFS-HOCE.'
'MIOT NS O COFCFS-HOCE?' SOND OLNCE; IAT TIOT SRE UORTED GFCI TA KRAU, VFT TIE DADA IOD WOFSED OS NP NT TRAFMRT TROT SAGEVADG AFMRT TA SWEOK, OID RA ARE ELSE SEEGED NRCLNRED TA SOY ORYTRNIM.
'URG,' SOND TIE DADA, 'TRE BEST MOY TA EQWLONR NT NS TA DA NT.' (OID, OS GAF PNMRT LNVE TA THG TRE TRNIM GAFHSELP, SAPE MNITEH DOG, N MNLL TELL YAF RAM TIE DADA POROMED NT.)
PNHST NT POHKED AFT O HOCE-CAFHSE, NI O SAHT AP CNHCLE, ('TIE EQOCT SIOWE DAESI'T GOTTEH,' NT SOND,) OID TREI OLL TIE BOHTY MEHE WLOCED OLARU TIE CAFHSE, REHE OID TREHE. TIEHE MOS IA 'ARE, TMA, TIHEE, OID OMOY,' VFT TIEG BEMOR HFRINIM UREI TIEG LNVED, ORD LEPT APY UREI TIEG LNVED, SA TROT NT UOS RAT EOSY TA VIAM MIER TRE HOCE MOS AKEH. RAMEWEH, UREI TIEG IOD BEEI HFIRNRU ROLY OI RAFH AH SA, ORD MEHE XFNTE DHG OUONR, TIE DADA SFDDEILY COLLED AFT 'TIE HOCE NS AKEH!' OID TREY OLL CHAUDED HAFRD NT, BOITNRU, OID OSVNRU, 'VFT MIA ROS MAI?'
TINS XFESTNAI TIE DADA CAFLD RAT OISMEH MNTIAFT O UHEOT DEOL AP TIAFUIT, OID NT SOT PAH O LAIM TNPE MNTI AIE YNRUEH BHESSED FWAR NTS YAHEIEOD (TRE WASNTNAI NR URNCI GAF FSFOLLG SEE SROKESWEOHE, NR TRE WNCTFHES AY INP), URNLE TRE HEST MONTED NI SNLEICE. OT LOST TRE DADA SOND, 'EWEHGVADG IOS UAR, ORD OLL GFST IOKE BHNZES.'
'VFT MIA NS TA UNWE TRE WHNZES?' JFNTE O CIAHFS AP WANCES OSVED.
'URG, SIE, AP CAFHSE,' SOND TIE DADA, BANRTNIM TA OLNCE MNTI AIE YNRUEH; OID TRE URALE WOHTG OT ARCE CHAMDED HAFID IEH, COLLNRU AFT NR O CARPFSED MOY, 'BHNZES! BHNZES!'
OLNCE IOD RA NDEO UROT TA DA, OID NI DESWONH SIE BFT REH ROID NI REH BACVET, ORD BFLLED AFT O BAQ AP CAGYNTS, (LFCVNLY TIE SOLT UOTEH IOD RAT MAT NITA NT), OID IORDED TIEP HAFID OS BHNZES. TIEHE MOS EQOCTLY ARE O-BNECE OLL HAFRD.
'VFT SIE GFST IOKE O BHNZE REHSELP, GAF VIAM,' SOND TRE PAFSE.
'AP CAFHSE,' TRE DADA HEBLNED WEHG MHOWELG. 'UROT ELSE IOKE YAF UAT NR GAFH BACVET?' IE MEIT AI, TFHINIM TA OLNCE.
'ARLG O TRNGBLE,' SOND OLNCE SODLY.
'ROID NT AKEH IEHE,' SOND TRE DADA.
TREI TIEG OLL CHAMDED HAFID IEH AICE GAHE, MINLE TIE DADA SALEPILY BHESERTED TIE TINPVLE, SOGNRU 'UE VEU YAFH OCCEWTOICE AY TRNS ELEMORT TINPVLE'; ORD, UREI NT IOD YNRNSRED TINS SRAHT SBEECR, TREY OLL CIEEHED.
OLNCE TRAFMRT TRE URALE TRNIM KEHY OBSFHD, VFT TIEG OLL LAAKED SA MHOWE TROT SIE DND IAT DOHE TA LOFMR; OID, OS SRE CAFLD RAT TRNIV AP ORYTRNIM TA SOY, SRE SNPBLY VAMED, OID TAAK TIE TINPVLE, LAAKNIM OS SALEGR OS SIE CAFLD.
TRE REQT TINRU MOS TA EOT TRE CAPPNTS: TINS COFSED SAGE RANSE OID CARPFSNAR, OS TRE LOHUE BNHDS CAPBLONIED TIOT TREY CAFLD IAT TOSTE TIENHS, ORD TIE SPOLL ARES CRAKED ORD ROD TA BE BOTTED AI TIE VOCV. RAMEWEH, NT MOS AKEH OT LOST, ORD TIEG SOT DAUI OMONI NR O HNRU, OID BEMUED TIE GAFSE TA TELL TIEP SAPETRNIM PAHE.
'YAF BHAPNSED TA TELL PE YAFH INSTAHG, YAF KRAU,' SOND OLNCE, 'ORD MIY NT NS YAF ROTE—C OID D,' SRE ODDED NI O MINSBEH, IOLP OYHOND TROT NT UAFLD BE AYPEIDED OUONR.
'PNRE NS O LARU ORD O SOD TOLE!' SOND TIE GAFSE, TFHINIM TA OLNCE, OID SNMRNIM.
'NT NS O LARU TONL, CEHTONILY,' SOND OLNCE, LAAVNRU DAMR UNTR MAIDEH OT TIE GAFSE'S TONL; 'BFT URG DA YAF COLL NT SOD?' ORD SIE KEBT AI BFZZLNIM OVAFT NT MINLE TIE GAFSE MOS SWEOKNIM, SA TROT REH NDEO AP TIE TOLE UOS SAPETRNIM LNVE TINS:—
         'YFHY SOND TA O

'YAF OHE IAT OTTEIDNRU!' SOND TRE PAFSE TA OLNCE SEWEHELG. 'UROT OHE YAF TINRKNIM AP?'
'N BEM GAFH BOHDAR,' SOND OLNCE WEHG IFPVLY: 'YAF ROD UAT TA TRE YNYTI BERD, N TRNIV?'
'N ROD IAT!' CHNED TIE GAFSE, SROHWLG OID KEHY ORUHNLY.
'O KRAT!' SOND OLNCE, OLUOGS HEODY TA POVE REHSELP FSEYFL, ORD LAAVNRU ORQNAFSLY OBAFT REH. 'AI, DA LET PE RELW TA FRDA NT!'
'N SROLL DA IATINRU AY TRE SAHT,' SOND TRE PAFSE, UETTNRU FW OID UOLKNIM OMOY. 'YAF NRSFLT PE VG TOLKNIM SFCR IAISERSE!'
'N DNDR'T PEOI NT!' WLEODED WAAH OLNCE. 'VFT YAF'HE SA EOSNLG APYERDED, GAF VIAM!'
TIE GAFSE ARLG MHAMLED NI HEBLY.
'BLEOSE CAPE VOCV OID YNRNSR YAFH STAHG!' OLNCE COLLED OYTEH NT; ORD TIE ATREHS OLL JANIED NR CRAHFS, 'YES, WLEOSE DA!' BFT TRE PAFSE AILY SIAAK NTS REOD NGWOTNEITLG, ORD MOLVED O LNTTLE JFNCKEH.
'MIOT O WNTY NT UAFLDI'T STOG!' SNMRED TIE LAHG, OS SAAI OS NT MOS JFNTE AFT AY SNMRT; ORD OR ALD CHOV TAAV TRE ABWAHTFINTG AP SOYNIM TA REH DOFMRTEH 'OI, GG DEOH! LET TRNS VE O LESSAI TA GAF REKEH TA LASE GAFH TEGWEH!' 'RALD GAFH TAIMFE, GO!' SOND TIE YAFRU CHOB, O LNTTLE SIOBWNSRLY. 'YAF'HE EIAFMR TA THG TRE WOTNEICE AY OI AGSTEH!'
'N MNSI N IOD AFH DNROI IEHE, N VIAM N DA!' SOND OLNCE OLAFD, ODDHESSNRU IAVADG NI BOHTNCFLOH. 'SRE'D SAAI PETCR NT BOCK!'
'OID URA NS DNIOR, NP N GNUIT WEITFHE TA OSV TRE XFESTNAI?' SOND TRE LAHY.
OLNCE HEWLNED EOMEHLG, PAH SIE MOS OLMOYS HEODG TA TOLV OVAFT IEH WET: 'DNROI'S AFH COT. ORD SIE'S SFCI O COWNTOL AIE YAH COTCINRU GNCE GAF COR'T TRNIV! ORD AI, N MNSI GAF CAFLD SEE IEH OPTEH TRE BNHDS! MIY, SRE'LL EOT O LNTTLE BNHD OS SAAI OS LAAK OT NT!'
TINS SBEECR COFSED O HEPOHKOVLE SEISOTNAI OPARU TIE BOHTY. SAPE AY TRE BNHDS IFHHNED APY OT ARCE: ARE ALD GOUWNE BEMOR UHOBWNRU NTSELY FB WEHG COHEYFLLG, HEGOHVNRU, 'N HEOLLG PFST VE METTNIM IAPE; TRE RNMRT-ONH DAESR'T SFNT GG TRHAOT!' ORD O COIOHG COLLED AFT NR O THEGBLNIM KANCE TA NTS CINLDHER, 'CAPE OUOG, GG DEOHS! NT'S INMR TNGE GAF UEHE OLL NR BED!' AI WOHNAFS BHETEQTS TREY OLL GAWED AYP, OID OLNCE UOS SAAI LEPT OLAIE.
'N UNSR N RODR'T PERTNARED DNROI!' SRE SOND TA IEHSELY NI O GELOICRALG TARE. 'IAVADG SEEGS TA LNKE IEH, DAMR IEHE, OID N'P SFHE SIE'S TIE VEST COT NI TIE MAHLD! AR, PY DEOH DNROI! N MAIDEH NP N SIOLL EKEH SEE GAF OIG PAHE!' ORD REHE WAAH OLNCE VEUOI TA CHG OUONR, PAH SIE PELT KEHY LAIELG OID LAU-SBNHNTED. NI O LNTTLE URNLE, RAMEWEH, SRE OUONR IEOHD O LNTTLE BOTTEHNRU AY YAATSTEBS NI TIE DNSTORCE, ORD SIE LAAVED FB EOUEHLY, IOLP RABNIM TROT TIE GAFSE ROD CIORUED RNS GNID, ORD MOS CAGNIM BOCK TA YNRNSR RNS STAHY.




CROBTEH NW. TRE HOBVNT SEIDS NR O LNTTLE VNLL

NT UOS TRE URNTE HOBVNT, THATTNRU SLAULG BOCK OMONI, OID LAAKNIM OIQNAFSLG OVAFT OS NT UERT, OS NY NT ROD LAST SAPETRNIM; ORD SIE REOHD NT PFTTEHNIM TA NTSELY 'TIE DFCIESS! TRE DFCRESS! AI PY DEOH WOUS! AR GG YFH OID URNSVEHS! SRE'LL UET GE EQECFTED, OS SFHE OS PEHHETS OHE PEHHETS! UREHE COR N IOKE DHAWBED TIEP, N MAIDEH?' OLNCE MFESSED NI O GAGEIT TROT NT UOS LAAKNIM YAH TRE YOR OID TRE WONH AY URNTE VND MLAWES, OID SRE KEHY UAAD-ROTFHEDLG BEMOR IFRTNIM OVAFT YAH TREG, BFT TREY MEHE RAUREHE TA VE SEEI—EKEHYTRNIM SEEGED TA IOKE CIORUED SNICE REH SUNP NI TIE BAAL, ORD TIE UHEOT ROLL, MNTI TRE MLOSS TOBLE OID TRE LNTTLE DAAH, ROD WOINSIED CAPBLETELY.
KEHY SAAR TRE HOBVNT IATNCED OLNCE, OS SIE MEIT IFRTNIM OVAFT, ORD COLLED AFT TA REH NR OI ORUHY TAIE, 'URG, GOHG OIR, MIOT OHE GAF DANIM AFT IEHE? HFR IAPE TINS PAPERT, OID YETCI PE O BONH AP ULAKES OID O YOR! JFNCK, RAU!' OID OLNCE UOS SA GFCI YHNUITEIED TIOT SRE HOR APY OT ARCE NI TIE DNHECTNAI NT WANITED TA, UNTRAFT THGNRU TA EQWLONR TRE PNSTOKE NT ROD GODE.
'IE TAAV PE PAH RNS RAFSEPOND,' SIE SOND TA REHSELP OS SRE HOR. 'IAU SFHBHNSED IE'LL BE MIER IE PNIDS AFT MIA N OP! VFT N'D VETTEH TOVE RNG RNS POI ORD ULAKES—TROT NS, NY N COR YNRD TIEP.' OS SIE SOND TRNS, SRE COPE FWAR O REOT LNTTLE IAFSE, AR TRE DAAH AY URNCI UOS O BHNUIT VHOSS BLOTE MNTI TRE ROPE 'U. HOVBNT' ERUHOKED FBAI NT. SIE MEIT NI MNTIAFT KRACKNIM, ORD RFHHNED FWSTONHS, NR MHEOT YEOH LEST SRE SRAFLD GEET TRE HEOL GOHG OIR, ORD VE TFHIED AFT AY TRE IAFSE BEYAHE SIE ROD PAFRD TIE POI ORD ULAKES.
'IAU XFEEH NT SEEPS,' OLNCE SOND TA REHSELP, 'TA BE UANRU GESSOMES YAH O HOBVNT! N SFWBASE DNROI'LL VE SERDNIM PE AR PESSOUES IEQT!' OID SRE BEMOR YORCGNRU TIE SAHT AP TINRU TIOT UAFLD IOWBEI: '"PNSS OLNCE! CAPE REHE DNHECTLY, OID MET HEODG YAH GAFH MOLV!" "CAGNIM NI O GNIFTE, IFHSE! BFT N'KE UAT TA SEE TROT TIE GAFSE DAESI'T UET AFT." ARLG N DAR'T TRNIV,' OLNCE UERT AR, 'TROT TIEG'D LET DNROI STAB NR TRE IAFSE NP NT BEMOR AHDEHNRU BEAWLE OVAFT LNVE TIOT!'
BY TINS TNPE SIE ROD PAFRD REH MOY NRTA O TNDY LNTTLE HAAG MNTI O TOBLE NI TIE MNIDAU, ORD AR NT (OS SIE ROD RABED) O YOR OID TMA AH TIHEE BONHS AY TNRY MINTE KND ULAKES: SIE TAAV FB TIE POI ORD O BONH AP TIE ULAKES, ORD MOS XFST MANIM TA LEOKE TIE HAAP, MIER IEH EYE YELL FWAR O LNTTLE VATTLE TROT STAAD IEOH TRE LAAKNIM-MLOSS. TIEHE MOS IA LOBEL TRNS TNGE UNTR TIE MAHDS 'DHNIV PE,' VFT IEWEHTRELESS SRE FICAHKED NT OID WFT NT TA IEH LNWS. 'N KRAU SAPETRNIM NITEHESTNIM NS SFHE TA ROBWER,' SRE SOND TA IEHSELY, 'UREIEWEH N EOT AH DHNIV OIGTINRU; SA N'LL JFST SEE MIOT TRNS VATTLE DAES. N DA RABE NT'LL POVE GE MHAM LOHME OMONI, YAH HEOLLY N'G JFNTE TNHED AY BENIM SFCR O TNIG LNTTLE TINRU!'
NT DND SA NRDEED, ORD GFCI SAAIEH TIOR SRE IOD EQWECTED: BEYAHE SIE ROD DHFRK ROLY TRE BATTLE, SRE YAFID IEH IEOD BHESSNIM OUONRST TRE CENLNIM, ORD ROD TA STAAW TA SOWE IEH RECK PHAP BENIM BHAKEI. SRE IOSTNLG WFT DAUI TIE VATTLE, SOYNIM TA REHSELP 'TROT'S JFNTE ERAFUI—N IAWE N SIOR'T MHAM ORY GAHE—OS NT NS, N COR'T MET AFT OT TIE DAAH—N DA MNSI N IODI'T DHFRK JFNTE SA PFCR!'
OLOS! NT UOS TAA LOTE TA UNSR TIOT! SIE MEIT AI UHAUNRU, OID MHAMNIM, ORD WEHG SAAI ROD TA VIEEL DAUI AR TRE YLAAH: NR OIATIEH PNRFTE TIEHE MOS IAT EKER HAAG PAH TINS, ORD SIE THNED TIE EYPECT AP LGNRU DAMR UNTR ARE ELVAM OMONIST TIE DAAH, ORD TIE ATREH OHG CFHLED HAFID IEH IEOD. STNLL SRE UERT AR MHAMNIM, ORD, OS O LOST HESAFHCE, SRE WFT AIE OHP AFT AP TIE MNIDAU, ORD ARE PAAT FB TIE CINPIEY, OID SOND TA IEHSELY 'IAM N COI DA RA GAHE, MIOTEKEH IOWBEIS. MIOT UNLL VECAGE AP GE?'
LFCKNLG YAH OLNCE, TIE LNTTLE POMNC BATTLE ROD IAM ROD NTS PFLL EPYECT, OID SRE MHEM IA LOHUEH: STNLL NT MOS WEHG FICAPPAHTOBLE, ORD, OS TIEHE SEEPED TA VE RA SAHT AP CIORCE AP REH EKEH METTNIM AFT AP TIE HAAP OUONR, IA UARDEH SIE PELT FIIOWBG.
'NT MOS GFCI WLEOSORTEH OT IAPE,' TIAFUIT BAAH OLNCE, 'UREI ARE MOSR'T OLUOGS UHAUNRU LOHMEH OID SGOLLEH, ORD VENRU AHDEHED OBAFT VG PNCE ORD HOVBNTS. N OLPAST MNSI N IODI'T UAIE DAUI TIOT HOBVNT-RALE—OID GET—OID GET—NT'S HOTIEH CFHNAFS, YAF KRAU, TINS SAHT AY LNYE! N DA MAIDEH UROT COI ROWE IOWBEIED TA PE! UREI N FSED TA HEOD YONHG-TOLES, N POICNED TIOT VNRD AY TRNIM REKEH IOWBEIED, OID RAU IEHE N OP NI TIE GNDDLE AP ARE! TREHE AFMRT TA VE O BAAK MHNTTEI OBAFT GE, TIOT TREHE AFMRT! ORD MIER N MHAM FW, N'LL UHNTE AIE—BFT N'P MHAMR FB IAM,' SIE ODDED NR O SAHHAMYFL TARE; 'OT LEOST TREHE'S RA HAAP TA UHAU FB ORY GAHE IEHE.'
'BFT TREI,' TIAFUIT OLNCE, 'SIOLL N IEWEH UET ORY ALDEH TIOR N OG IAM? TROT'LL BE O CAGYAHT, AIE UOG—REKEH TA VE OI ALD MAGOI—VFT TIER—OLUOGS TA IOKE LESSARS TA LEOHR! AI, N SIAFLDI'T LNKE TROT!'
'AR, GAF YAALNSI OLNCE!' SRE OISMEHED REHSELP. 'RAM COI YAF LEOHI LESSARS NR IEHE? URG, TIEHE'S ROHDLG HAAG PAH YAF, OID RA HAAP OT OLL PAH ORY LESSAR-BAAKS!'
OID SA SIE MEIT AI, TOVNRU PNHST ARE SNDE OID TREI TIE ATREH, OID POVNRU JFNTE O CAIKEHSOTNAR AP NT OLTAMETREH; BFT OPTEH O YEU PNRFTES SRE IEOHD O KANCE AFTSNDE, ORD STAWBED TA LNSTEI.
'GOHG OIR! GOHG OIR!' SOND TIE WANCE. 'PETCR GE PY ULAKES TRNS GAGEIT!' TREI COGE O LNTTLE BOTTEHNRU AY YEET AR TRE STONHS. OLNCE VIEM NT UOS TRE HOBVNT CAGNIM TA LAAV YAH IEH, ORD SIE THEPVLED TNLL SIE SIAAK TIE RAFSE, XFNTE YAHUETTNRU TIOT SRE UOS RAU OVAFT O TRAFSORD TNGES OS LOHUE OS TIE HOVBNT, ORD ROD IA HEOSAI TA BE OYHOND AP NT.
BHESERTLY TIE HOVBNT COPE FW TA TIE DAAH, ORD THNED TA ABEI NT; VFT, OS TIE DAAH ABEIED NRMOHDS, OID OLNCE'S ELBAU UOS WHESSED IOHD OMONIST NT, TIOT OTTEPBT WHAWED O PONLFHE. OLNCE IEOHD NT SOY TA NTSELP 'TREI N'LL MA HAFRD ORD UET NR OT TIE MNIDAU.'
'TIOT GAF UAR'T' TIAFUIT OLNCE, OID, OYTEH MONTNRU TNLL SRE YORCNED SRE IEOHD TRE HOBVNT XFST FIDEH TRE UNRDAM, SRE SFDDEILY SWHEOD AFT IEH IORD, OID PODE O SROTCI NI TIE ONH. SRE DND RAT MET IALD AY OIGTINRU, BFT SRE IEOHD O LNTTLE SIHNEV OID O YOLL, OID O CHOSI AP VHAVER MLOSS, PHAP URNCI SRE CARCLFDED TROT NT UOS JFST BASSNBLE NT ROD POLLER NITA O CFCFGBEH-YHOGE, AH SAPETRNIM AP TIE SAHT.
IEQT COPE OR OIMHG KANCE—TRE HOBVNT'S—'WOT! BOT! UREHE OHE GAF?' OID TREI O WANCE SIE ROD IEWEH REOHD VEPAHE, 'SFHE TIER N'P IEHE! DNMUNIM YAH OBWLES, GEH IARAFH!'
'DNMUNIM YAH OBWLES, NIDEED!' SOND TRE HOBVNT ORUHNLY. 'REHE! CAGE OID IELB GE AFT AP TINS!' (SAFRDS AP GAHE BHAKEI ULOSS.)
'RAU TELL GE, BOT, UROT'S TIOT NI TIE MNIDAU?'
'SFHE, NT'S OI OHG, GEH IARAFH!' (IE BHARAFICED NT 'OHHFP.')
'OI OHG, GAF MAASE! MIA EKEH SOU AIE TROT SNZE? MIY, NT PNLLS TIE MIALE MNIDAU!'
'SFHE, NT DAES, GEH IARAFH: BFT NT'S OR OHP YAH OLL TROT.'
'UELL, NT'S UAT IA BFSNRESS TIEHE, OT ORY HOTE: UA OID TOVE NT OMOY!'
TIEHE MOS O LAIM SNLERCE OPTEH TRNS, OID OLNCE CAFLD AILY REOH URNSWEHS IAM ORD TIER; SFCI OS, 'SFHE, N DAI'T LNKE NT, GEH IARAFH, OT OLL, OT OLL!' 'DA OS N TELL YAF, GAF CAUOHD!' ORD OT LOST SIE SWHEOD AFT IEH IORD OMONI, OID PODE ORATREH SROTCI NI TIE ONH. TRNS TNGE TREHE UEHE TUA LNTTLE SRHNEKS, ORD GAHE SAFIDS AY BHAKEI ULOSS. 'MIOT O RFPVEH AY CFCFPVEH-PHOPES TREHE PFST VE!' TRAFMRT OLNCE. 'N UARDEH MIOT TREY'LL DA IEQT! OS YAH WFLLNIM PE AFT AY TRE UNRDAM, N AILY MNSI TREY CAFLD! N'P SFHE N DAI'T MOIT TA STOG NI REHE OIG LARUEH!'
SIE MONTED YAH SAPE TNGE UNTRAFT IEOHNIM OIGTINRU GAHE: OT LOST COGE O HFPVLNRU AY LNTTLE COHTMIEELS, ORD TIE SAFRD AY O MAAD GOIG KANCES OLL TOLVNRU TAUETIEH: SIE GODE AFT TRE UAHDS: 'UREHE'S TRE ATIEH LODDEH?—URG, N RODR'T TA VHNRU VFT ARE; BNLL'S UAT TIE ATREH—VNLL! PETCR NT IEHE, LOD!—REHE, BFT 'EG FW OT TINS CAHIEH—IA, TNE 'EG TAUETIEH YNHST—TREY DAI'T HEOCR ROLY INMR ERAFUI GET—AR! TREY'LL DA MELL EIAFMR; DAR'T BE BOHTNCFLOH—IEHE, BNLL! COTCI IALD AY TRNS HABE—UNLL TIE HAAY BEOH?—PNRD TIOT LAASE SLOTE—AR, NT'S CAGNIM DAUI! IEODS BELAU!' (O LAFD CHOSI)—'RAU, MIA DND TIOT?—NT UOS BNLL, N YORCG—URA'S TA UA DAUI TIE CINPIEY?—ROG, N SIOR'T! YAF DA NT!—TROT N MAI'T, TREI!—BNLL'S TA MA DAMR—IEHE, BNLL! TRE POSTEH SOYS GAF'HE TA MA DAMR TRE CRNGREG!'
'AI! SA BNLL'S UAT TA CAPE DAMR TRE CRNGREG, ROS RE?' SOND OLNCE TA IEHSELY. 'SRG, TIEG SEEG TA WFT EWEHGTINRU FWAR BNLL! N UAFLDI'T VE NI VNLL'S WLOCE YAH O MAAD DEOL: TINS YNHEWLOCE NS IOHHAU, TA BE SFHE; VFT N TINRK N COI KNCV O LNTTLE!'
SIE DHEU IEH YAAT OS YOH DAUI TIE CINPIEY OS SRE CAFLD, ORD MONTED TNLL SIE REOHD O LNTTLE OINGOL (SRE CAFLDI'T UFESS AY UROT SAHT NT MOS) SCHOTCINRU ORD SCHOGBLNIM OVAFT NI TIE CINPIEY CLASE OBAKE REH: TREI, SOGNRU TA IEHSELY 'TINS NS VNLL,' SRE MOKE ARE SIOHB KNCV, ORD MONTED TA SEE MIOT UAFLD IOWBEI IEQT.
TIE PNHST TINRU SIE REOHD MOS O UEIEHOL CIAHFS AP 'TREHE MAES VNLL!' TREI TIE HOVBNT'S KANCE OLAIM—'COTCR RNG, GAF BY TIE REDME!' TIER SNLERCE, ORD TIER OIATIEH CARPFSNAR AP WANCES—'RALD FB RNS REOD—BHOIDY IAM—DAI'T CIAVE RNG—RAM MOS NT, ALD PELLAU? MIOT IOWBEIED TA GAF? TELL FS OLL OBAFT NT!'
LOST COGE O LNTTLE PEEBLE, SXFEOVNRU WANCE, ('TROT'S VNLL,' TRAFMRT OLNCE,) 'MELL, N ROHDLG VIAM—IA PAHE, TROIV GE; N'P BETTEH IAM—VFT N'G O DEOL TAA YLFSTEHED TA TELL GAF—OLL N VIAM NS, SAGETINRU CAGES OT PE LNKE O JOCK-NR-TRE-BAQ, ORD FW N MAES LNKE O SKG-HACKET!'
'SA YAF DND, ALD YELLAM!' SOND TRE ATIEHS.
'ME PFST VFHR TRE IAFSE DAUI!' SOND TRE HOBVNT'S WANCE; OID OLNCE COLLED AFT OS LAFD OS SRE CAFLD, 'NP YAF DA. N'LL SET DNROI OT YAF!'
TIEHE MOS O DEOD SNLERCE NISTOITLG, ORD OLNCE TIAFUIT TA IEHSELY, 'N UARDEH MIOT TREY MNLL DA IEQT! NY TREY ROD ORY SEISE, TREY'D TOKE TRE HAAP AYP.' OYTEH O GNIFTE AH TUA, TREY VEUOI GAWNIM OVAFT OUONR, ORD OLNCE REOHD TIE HOVBNT SOG, 'O BOHHAMYFL UNLL DA, TA BEMNR UNTR.'
'O BOHHAMYFL AP MIOT?' TRAFMRT OLNCE; VFT SIE ROD IAT LAIM TA DAFBT, YAH TRE REQT GAGEIT O SRAMEH AY LNTTLE BEVBLES COGE HOTTLNRU NR OT TIE MNIDAU, ORD SAGE AP TIEP INT IEH NI TIE POCE. 'N'LL BFT O STAW TA TINS,' SRE SOND TA IEHSELY, ORD SIAFTED AFT, 'YAF'D VETTEH RAT DA TIOT OUONR!' URNCI WHADFCED ORATREH DEOD SNLERCE.
OLNCE IATNCED MNTI SAPE SFHWHNSE TROT TIE BEVBLES MEHE OLL TFHINIM NITA LNTTLE COVES OS TIEG LOG AI TIE PLAAH, OID O BHNUIT NDEO COPE NRTA IEH IEOD. 'NY N EOT AIE AP TIESE COKES,' SIE TIAFUIT, 'NT'S SFHE TA POVE SAGE CROIME NR PY SNZE; ORD OS NT COI'T BASSNBLG POVE GE LOHUEH, NT GFST POVE GE SGOLLEH, N SFBWASE.'
SA SRE SMOLLAUED AIE AP TIE COKES, OID UOS DELNMRTED TA PNID TROT SIE VEUOI SIHNIVNRU DNHECTLG. OS SAAI OS SRE UOS SGOLL EIAFMR TA MET TRHAFUI TRE DAAH, SRE HOR AFT AP TIE RAFSE, OID YAFID XFNTE O CHAMD AP LNTTLE OINGOLS OID BNHDS UONTNIM AFTSNDE. TIE BAAH LNTTLE LNZOHD, VNLL, MOS NR TRE PNDDLE, BENIM IELD FW BY TUA UFNREO-WNMS, URA UEHE UNWNIM NT SAGETINRU AFT AY O BATTLE. TREY OLL GODE O HFSR OT OLNCE TRE PAPERT SIE OWBEOHED; VFT SIE HOI AYP OS IOHD OS SRE CAFLD, ORD SAAR YAFID IEHSELY SOYE NR O TRNCV UAAD.
'TIE PNHST TINRU N'WE MAT TA DA,' SOND OLNCE TA IEHSELY, OS SRE UORDEHED OBAFT NR TRE UAAD, 'NS TA UHAU TA GG HNMRT SNZE OMONI; OID TRE SECARD TINRU NS TA PNID PY MOY NRTA TROT LAWELG MOHDEI. N TRNIV TROT MNLL BE TIE VEST WLOI.'
NT SAFIDED OI EQCELLERT BLOR, IA DAFVT, ORD WEHG REOTLY ORD SNGWLG OHHORUED; TRE AILY DNPYNCFLTG UOS, TIOT SRE IOD RAT TRE SGOLLEST NDEO IAU TA SET OBAFT NT; ORD MINLE SIE MOS BEEHNRU OBAFT ORQNAFSLY OPARU TIE THEES, O LNTTLE SIOHB VOHV JFST AKEH IEH IEOD GODE IEH LAAK FW NI O UHEOT RFHHY.
OI ERAHGAFS WFWBG UOS LAAKNIM DAUI OT IEH UNTR LOHME HAFRD EGES, ORD PEEBLG STHETCINRU AFT ARE BOM, THGNRU TA TAFCI IEH. 'WAAH LNTTLE TRNIM!' SOND OLNCE, NI O CAOQNRU TAIE, ORD SIE THNED ROHD TA MINSTLE TA NT; BFT SRE UOS TEHHNVLY PHNMRTERED OLL TRE TNPE OT TRE TRAFMRT TROT NT PNMRT BE RFIMHG, NR URNCI COSE NT UAFLD BE WEHG LNVELY TA EOT IEH FB NR SBNTE AP OLL REH CAOQNRU.
IOHDLY KRAUNRU MIOT SRE DND, SIE BNCVED FB O LNTTLE BNT AP STNCK, OID IELD NT AFT TA TIE BFBWY; UREHEFWAR TRE WFWBG JFPBED NRTA TRE ONH APY OLL NTS YEET OT AICE, UNTR O YELW AP DELNUIT, OID HFSRED OT TRE STNCV, ORD GODE BELNEWE TA MAHHY NT; TIER OLNCE DADUED VERNID O MHEOT TRNSTLE, TA VEEB REHSELP PHAP BENIM HFR AWEH; OID TRE PAPERT SIE OWBEOHED AI TIE ATREH SNDE, TIE BFBWY GODE OIATIEH HFSR OT TRE STNCV, ORD TFGBLED REOD AWEH REELS NR NTS IFHHG TA UET RALD AP NT; TIER OLNCE, TINRKNIM NT MOS WEHG LNVE ROWNIM O MOPE AY WLOY MNTI O COHT-RAHSE, OID EQWECTNIM EWEHG PAPERT TA BE THOPBLED FIDEH NTS YEET, HOR HAFID TRE TRNSTLE OUONR; TIER TRE WFWBG BEMOR O SEHNES AY SRAHT CROHMES OT TIE STNCK, HFRINIM O KEHY LNTTLE UOG YAHMOHDS EOCI TNPE ORD O LAIM UOG BOCK, OID BOHKNIM IAOHSELY OLL TIE MINLE, TNLL OT LOST NT SOT DAUI O UAAD UOG APY, BOITNRU, UNTR NTS TAIMFE IORUNIM AFT AP NTS GAFTR, OID NTS MHEOT EYES ROLY SRFT.
TRNS SEEPED TA OLNCE O UAAD ABWAHTFINTG YAH POVNRU REH ESCOBE; SA SRE SET APY OT ARCE, ORD HOI TNLL SRE UOS XFNTE TNHED OID AFT AP VHEOTI, ORD TNLL TRE WFWBG'S BOHK SAFRDED JFNTE PONRT NR TRE DNSTOICE.
'ORD YET MIOT O DEOH LNTTLE WFWBG NT MOS!' SOND OLNCE, OS SRE LEOIT OUONRST O BFTTEHCFW TA HEST IEHSELY, ORD POIRED IEHSELY UNTR ARE AY TRE LEOWES: 'N SIAFLD IOKE LNKED TEOCRNIM NT THNCKS KEHY GFCI, NY—NP N'D ARLG BEEI TIE HNUIT SNZE TA DA NT! AR DEOH! N'D IEOHLG YAHUATTER TROT N'WE MAT TA UHAU FB OMONI! LET PE SEE—RAM NS NT TA BE GOIOUED? N SFWBASE N AFMRT TA EOT AH DHNIV SAPETRNIM AH ATREH; BFT TRE MHEOT XFESTNAI NS, MIOT?'
TRE MHEOT XFESTNAI CEHTONILY MOS, UROT? OLNCE LAAKED OLL HAFRD REH OT TRE YLAMEHS OID TRE BLODES AY MHOSS, VFT SIE DND IAT SEE ORYTRNIM TROT LAAVED LNVE TIE HNUIT TINRU TA EOT AH DHNRK FRDEH TIE CNHCFPSTORCES. TREHE UOS O LOHUE PFSRHAAG UHAUNRU IEOH IEH, OBAFT TIE SOGE IENUIT OS IEHSELY; ORD MIER SRE IOD LAAKED FRDEH NT, ORD AR BATR SNDES AY NT, OID BEINRD NT, NT ACCFHHED TA IEH TROT SIE GNUIT OS UELL LAAV OID SEE UROT MOS AR TRE TAW AP NT.
SIE STHETCRED REHSELP FW AI TNBTAE, ORD BEEWED AWEH TIE EDUE AP TIE GFSIHAAP, ORD REH EGES NGPEDNOTELG PET TRASE AP O LOHME COTEHWNLLOH, TROT MOS SNTTNRU AR TRE TAW UNTR NTS OHGS YALDED, XFNETLG SGAKNIM O LARU RAAVOI, ORD TOKNIM RAT TRE SGOLLEST IATNCE AP REH AH AP ORYTRNIM ELSE.




CROBTEH K. ODWNCE YHAG O COTEHWNLLOH

TRE COTEHBNLLOH OID OLNCE LAAKED OT EOCR ATREH PAH SAGE TNPE NR SNLERCE: OT LOST TIE COTEHWNLLOH TAAV TRE IAAKOR AFT AY NTS PAFTI, ORD ODDHESSED REH NR O LORUFND, SLEEBG KANCE.
'URA OHE GAF?' SOND TIE COTEHWNLLOH.
TRNS MOS IAT OR EICAFHOUNIM ABEINIM YAH O CARWEHSOTNAI. OLNCE HEWLNED, HOTIEH SRGLG, 'N—N IOHDLY KRAU, SNH, JFST OT WHESEIT—OT LEOST N KRAU URA N UOS UREI N UAT FW TRNS GAHRNRU, BFT N TRNIV N PFST ROWE BEEI CIORUED SEWEHOL TNGES SNICE TIER.'
'MIOT DA YAF GEOR BY TIOT?' SOND TIE COTEHWNLLOH STEHILY. 'EQBLONI YAFHSELY!'
'N COI'T EQBLONI GGSELY, N'G OYHOND, SNH' SOND OLNCE, 'VECOFSE N'G IAT GGSELY, YAF SEE.'
'N DAR'T SEE,' SOND TIE COTEHWNLLOH.
'N'G OYHOND N COR'T WFT NT GAHE CLEOHLG,' OLNCE HEWLNED KEHY BALNTELG, 'YAH N COR'T FIDEHSTORD NT PYSELP TA BEMNR UNTR; OID BENIM SA GOIG DNYPEHEIT SNZES NI O DOY NS KEHY CAIYFSNRU.'
'NT NSI'T,' SOND TRE COTEHBNLLOH.
'UELL, WEHROBS GAF IOKER'T YAFID NT SA GET,' SOND OLNCE; 'VFT MIER GAF IOKE TA TFHI NRTA O CRHYSOLNS—GAF UNLL SAGE DOG, YAF KRAU—OID TREI OYTEH TIOT NITA O VFTTEHPLY, N SRAFLD TINRK YAF'LL YEEL NT O LNTTLE JFEEH, UAR'T GAF?'
'IAT O VNT,' SOND TRE COTEHBNLLOH.
'UELL, WEHROBS GAFH PEELNRUS POG BE DNPYEHERT,' SOND OLNCE; 'OLL N VIAM NS, NT UAFLD YEEL WEHG XFEEH TA GE.'
'YAF!' SOND TRE COTEHBNLLOH CARTEGWTFAFSLY. 'MIA OHE YAF?'
MINCR VHAFUIT TIEP BOCK OMONI TA TRE BEMNRINIM AP TIE CAIKEHSOTNAR. OLNCE PELT O LNTTLE NHHNTOTED OT TRE COTEHBNLLOH'S POVNRU SFCI KEHY SIAHT HEGOHVS, OID SRE DHEM REHSELP FW OID SOND, KEHY UHOKELY, 'N TINRK, GAF AFMRT TA TELL PE MIA YAF OHE, YNHST.'
'MIY?' SOND TRE COTEHBNLLOH.
REHE UOS OIATIEH WFZZLNRU JFESTNAR; ORD OS OLNCE CAFLD RAT TRNIV AP ORY UAAD HEOSAI, OID OS TIE COTEHWNLLOH SEEPED TA VE NI O WEHG FIWLEOSORT STOTE AY PNRD, SRE TFHIED OUOG.
'CAPE VOCV!' TRE COTEHBNLLOH COLLED OYTEH REH. 'N'WE SAPETRNIM NGWAHTOIT TA SOY!'
TINS SAFIDED WHAGNSNIM, CEHTONILY: OLNCE TFHIED ORD COGE BOCK OMONI.
'KEEW GAFH TEGWEH,' SOND TIE COTEHWNLLOH.
'NS TROT OLL?' SOND OLNCE, SUOLLAMNIM DAUI REH ORUEH OS UELL OS SRE CAFLD.
'RA,' SOND TRE COTEHBNLLOH.
OLNCE TIAFUIT SIE GNUIT OS UELL MONT, OS SRE IOD RATRNIM ELSE TA DA, OID WEHROBS OPTEH OLL NT GNUIT TELL IEH SAPETRNIM UAHTI IEOHNIM. PAH SAGE PNRFTES NT BFPYED OMOY MNTIAFT SWEOKNIM, VFT OT LOST NT FIYALDED NTS OHGS, TAAV TRE IAAKOR AFT AY NTS PAFTI OUONR, ORD SOND, 'SA YAF TINRK YAF'HE CROIMED, DA GAF?'
'N'G OYHOND N OG, SNH,' SOND OLNCE; 'N COI'T HEGEGBEH TRNIMS OS N FSED—ORD N DAI'T KEEW TRE SOPE SNZE YAH TER PNRFTES TAMETREH!'
'COR'T HEPEPVEH MIOT TRNIMS?' SOND TRE COTEHBNLLOH.
'UELL, N'KE THNED TA SOG "RAM DATI TRE LNTTLE VFSG BEE," BFT NT OLL COGE DNYPEHEIT!' OLNCE HEWLNED NI O WEHG PELORCIALY WANCE.
'HEBEOT, "GAF OHE ALD, POTIEH UNLLNOP,"' SOND TRE COTEHBNLLOH.
OLNCE PALDED IEH IORDS, ORD VEUOI:—
   'YAF OHE ALD, YOTREH MNLLNOG,' TIE YAFRU GOI SOND,
    'OID GAFH RONH IOS BECAPE WEHG URNTE;
   OID GET GAF NICESSOITLG STOID AI YAFH IEOD—
    DA YAF TINRK, OT YAFH OUE, NT NS HNUIT?'

   'NI GG GAFTI,' YOTREH MNLLNOG HEBLNED TA INS SAR,
    'N YEOHED NT PNMRT NIJFHE TIE VHONI;
   VFT, RAU TROT N'G BEHYECTLY SFHE N IOKE IAIE,
    MIY, N DA NT OUONR OID OUONR.'

   'YAF OHE ALD,' SOND TRE GAFTI, 'OS N GEITNAIED VEPAHE,
    ORD ROWE MHAMR PAST FRCAGPARLG YOT;
   GET GAF TFHIED O VOCV-SAPEHSOFLT NR OT TIE DAAH—
    BHOG, MIOT NS TIE HEOSAR AP TIOT?'

   'NR PY YAFTR,' SOND TRE SOME, OS RE SRAAV INS MHEY LACVS,
    'N KEBT OLL PY LNGBS WEHG SFWBLE
   BY TIE FSE AY TRNS ANITGEIT—AIE SRNLLNRU TIE VAQ—
    OLLAU PE TA SELL YAF O CAFWLE?'

   'YAF OHE ALD,' SOND TRE GAFTI, 'OID GAFH XOMS OHE TAA UEOK
    PAH ORYTRNIM TAFUIEH TROI SFET;
   GET GAF YNRNSRED TIE UAASE, UNTR TIE VAIES ORD TIE VEOV—
    BHOG IAU DND GAF POROME TA DA NT?'

   'NR PY YAFTR,' SOND INS YOTREH, 'N TAAV TA TIE LOM,
    OID OHMFED EOCI COSE MNTI PY MNPE;
   OID TRE PFSCFLOH STHEIMTI, MINCR NT MOKE TA PY XOM,
    IOS LOSTED TIE HEST AP GG LNYE.'

   'GAF OHE ALD,' SOND TIE YAFTR, 'ARE MAFLD ROHDLG SFWBASE
    TROT YAFH EYE UOS OS STEODG OS EKEH;
   GET GAF BOLORCED OR EEL AI TIE ERD AY GAFH IASE—
    MIOT PODE YAF SA OMYFLLG CLEWEH?'

   'N IOKE ORSUEHED TRHEE XFESTNAIS, ORD TIOT NS ERAFUI,'
    SOND RNS POTIEH; 'DAR'T MNKE YAFHSELY ONHS!
   DA GAF TRNIV N COR LNSTEI OLL DOY TA SFCR STFYP?
    BE AYP, AH N'LL VNCK YAF DAMR STONHS!'
'TROT NS RAT SOND HNUIT,' SOND TRE COTEHBNLLOH.
'RAT XFNTE HNMRT, N'G OYHOND,' SOND OLNCE, TNPNDLG; 'SAPE AY TRE UAHDS IOKE UAT OLTEHED.'
'NT NS UHAIM YHAG VEUNIRNRU TA EID,' SOND TIE COTEHWNLLOH DECNDEDLY, OID TREHE UOS SNLERCE YAH SAPE GNIFTES.
TRE COTEHBNLLOH UOS TRE YNHST TA SWEOK.
'MIOT SNZE DA GAF UORT TA BE?' NT OSVED.
'AR, N'P RAT WOHTNCFLOH OS TA SNZE,' OLNCE IOSTNLG HEWLNED; 'AILY ARE DAESI'T LNKE CROIMNRU SA APTER, YAF KRAU.'
'N DAI'T KRAU,' SOND TIE COTEHWNLLOH.
OLNCE SOND IATINRU: SRE IOD REKEH BEEI SA PFCR CAITHODNCTED NI REH LNPE BEYAHE, OID SRE YELT TIOT SRE UOS LASNRU REH TEGWEH.
'OHE GAF CARTEIT RAU?' SOND TIE COTEHWNLLOH.
'MELL, N SIAFLD LNVE TA BE O LNTTLE LOHUEH, SNH, NY GAF UAFLDI'T GNID,' SOND OLNCE: 'TIHEE NRCIES NS SFCI O UHETCRED RENMRT TA VE.'
'NT NS O WEHG MAAD RENMRT NIDEED!' SOND TRE COTEHBNLLOH OIMHNLG, HEOHNRU NTSELY FBHNMRT OS NT SBAKE (NT UOS EQOCTLG TRHEE NICRES RNUI).
'VFT N'G IAT FSED TA NT!' WLEODED WAAH OLNCE NR O WNTEAFS TARE. OID SRE TRAFMRT AP REHSELP, 'N MNSI TRE CHEOTFHES UAFLDI'T VE SA EOSNLG APYERDED!'
'GAF'LL UET FSED TA NT NI TNGE,' SOND TIE COTEHWNLLOH; OID NT BFT TIE RAAVOI NITA NTS GAFTR ORD VEUOI SPAVNRU OMONI.
TRNS TNGE OLNCE UONTED BOTNERTLY FRTNL NT CRASE TA SWEOK OMONI. NI O GNIFTE AH TUA TIE COTEHWNLLOH TAAV TRE IAAKOR AFT AY NTS PAFTI OID GOUIED ARCE AH TUNCE, OID SRAAV NTSELP. TREI NT MAT DAUI AYP TIE GFSIHAAP, ORD CHOULED OUOG NI TIE UHOSS, PEHELY HEGOHVNRU OS NT MEIT, 'AIE SNDE MNLL POVE YAF UHAU TOLLEH, OID TRE ATIEH SNDE MNLL POVE YAF UHAU SRAHTEH.'
'ARE SNDE AP MIOT? TIE ATREH SNDE AP MIOT?' TRAFMRT OLNCE TA REHSELP.
'AY TRE PFSRHAAG,' SOND TRE COTEHBNLLOH, XFST OS NY SRE IOD OSVED NT OLAFD; OID NI ORATREH GAGEIT NT MOS AFT AY SNMRT.
OLNCE HEGONRED LAAKNIM TRAFMRTPFLLY OT TRE PFSRHAAG PAH O GNIFTE, THYNIM TA GOKE AFT URNCI UEHE TIE TUA SNDES AY NT; OID OS NT UOS WEHPECTLG HAFID, SIE PAFRD TINS O KEHY DNPYNCFLT JFESTNAR. RAMEWEH, OT LOST SRE STHETCIED IEH OHPS HAFRD NT OS POH OS TREY MAFLD UA, ORD VHAVE AYP O VNT AY TRE EDME MNTI EOCR ROID.
'OID RAU URNCI NS MINCR?' SIE SOND TA REHSELP, OID RNBVLED O LNTTLE AY TRE HNMRT-IORD VNT TA THG TRE EPYECT: TRE REQT GAGEIT SRE YELT O WNALERT VLAU FIDEHIEOTR REH CINR: NT IOD STHFCK REH PAAT!
SIE MOS O UAAD DEOL PHNMRTERED BY TINS KEHY SFDDER CROIME, BFT SRE YELT TIOT TREHE UOS RA TNGE TA VE LAST, OS SIE MOS SIHNIVNRU HOBNDLY; SA SIE SET TA UAHK OT AICE TA EOT SAPE AY TRE ATIEH BNT. REH CINR UOS WHESSED SA CLASELY OMONIST REH PAAT, TIOT TREHE UOS IOHDLY HAAP TA AWER IEH PAFTI; VFT SIE DND NT OT LOST, ORD GOIOUED TA SMOLLAU O PAHSEL AY TRE LEYTIORD VNT.
  *    *    *    *    *    *    *

    *    *    *    *    *    *

  *    *    *    *    *    *    *
'CAPE, PY REOD'S YHEE OT LOST!' SOND OLNCE NI O TAIE AP DELNUIT, URNCI CROIMED NITA OLOHG NR OIATIEH PAPERT, UREI SIE PAFRD TIOT IEH SRAFLDEHS UEHE IAMIEHE TA BE PAFRD: OLL SRE CAFLD SEE, MIER SRE LAAKED DAMR, MOS OR NGPERSE LERUTR AY RECK, URNCI SEEGED TA HNSE LNKE O STOLV AFT AP O SEO AY MHEER LEOWES TIOT LOG YOH BELAU IEH.
'UROT COI OLL TIOT MHEER STFPY BE?' SOND OLNCE. 'OID UREHE IOKE GG SRAFLDEHS MAT TA? OID AR, PY BAAH IORDS, RAM NS NT N COI'T SEE YAF?' SIE MOS GAWNIM TREG OBAFT OS SRE SBAKE, VFT IA HESFLT SEEPED TA PALLAU, EQCEBT O LNTTLE SIOVNRU OPARU TIE DNSTORT UHEEI LEOKES.
OS TREHE SEEGED TA BE IA CROICE AY METTNIM IEH IORDS FB TA IEH IEOD, SRE THNED TA UET REH REOD DAUI TA TREG, OID UOS DELNMRTED TA PNID TROT REH IECV UAFLD BERD OBAFT EOSNLG NI ORY DNHECTNAI, LNVE O SEHWERT. SRE IOD JFST SFCCEEDED NR CFHWNIM NT DAMR NITA O UHOCEYFL ZNMZOU, OID UOS MANIM TA DNWE NI OPARU TIE LEOKES, MINCR SIE PAFRD TA BE IATINRU VFT TIE TABS AP TIE THEES FRDEH MINCR SIE ROD VEER UORDEHNIM, MIER O SROHW INSS GODE IEH DHOM VOCV NI O RFHHY: O LOHUE WNMEAI ROD PLAUI NRTA IEH YOCE, OID UOS BEOTNIM IEH KNALEITLG UNTR NTS MNIMS.
'SEHWERT!' SCHEOPED TRE WNMEAI.
'N'G IAT O SEHWERT!' SOND OLNCE NIDNMIOITLG. 'LET PE OLARE!'
'SEHBEIT, N SOY OMONI!' HEBEOTED TRE WNMEAI, BFT NI O GAHE SFBDFED TARE, OID ODDED UNTR O KNID AP SAV, 'N'WE THNED EWEHG UOG, ORD IATINRU SEEPS TA SFNT TIEP!'
'N ROWEI'T TIE LEOST NDEO UROT YAF'HE TOLKNIM OVAFT,' SOND OLNCE.
'N'WE THNED TRE HAATS AP THEES, OID N'KE THNED VOIVS, OID N'KE THNED REDMES,' TRE WNMEAI MEIT AI, UNTRAFT OTTERDNIM TA REH; 'VFT TIASE SEHWERTS! TIEHE'S IA WLEOSNRU TIEP!'
OLNCE UOS PAHE ORD GAHE WFZZLED, VFT SIE TIAFUIT TIEHE MOS IA FSE NI SOYNIM OIGTINRU GAHE TNLL TIE BNUEAR IOD YNRNSRED.
'OS NP NT UOSI'T THAFVLE ERAFUI IOTCINRU TIE EMUS,' SOND TIE BNUEAR; 'BFT N PFST VE AI TIE LAAV-AFT YAH SEHBEITS INUIT ORD DOY! URG, N ROWEI'T ROD O MNIV AP SLEEB TIESE TIHEE MEEVS!'
'N'P KEHY SAHHY YAF'WE BEEI ORIAYED,' SOND OLNCE, MIA MOS VEUNIRNRU TA SEE NTS PEOINIM.
'OID JFST OS N'D TOVER TRE INMREST THEE NR TRE UAAD,' CAITNRFED TIE BNUEAR, HONSNRU NTS WANCE TA O SRHNEK, 'ORD XFST OS N MOS TINRKNIM N SRAFLD VE YHEE AY TREG OT LOST, TREY GFST REEDS CAPE MHNMULNRU DAMR YHAG TIE SVY! FUI, SEHWERT!'
'BFT N'P RAT O SEHBEIT, N TELL GAF!' SOND OLNCE. 'N'G O—N'G O—'
'UELL! UROT OHE YAF?' SOND TRE WNMEAI. 'N COI SEE YAF'HE THGNRU TA NIKERT SAGETINRU!'
'N—N'P O LNTTLE UNHL,' SOND OLNCE, HOTREH DAFBTYFLLG, OS SRE HEPEPVEHED TIE IFGBEH AP CIORUES SIE ROD UAIE TRHAFUI TROT DOY.
'O LNKELG STAHG NIDEED!' SOND TRE WNMEAI NR O TARE AY TRE DEEBEST CARTEGWT. 'N'WE SEEI O UAAD PORY LNTTLE MNHLS NI GG TNPE, BFT REKEH AIE UNTR SFCI O RECK OS TROT! RA, RA! GAF'HE O SEHWERT; OID TREHE'S RA FSE DEIGNRU NT. N SFBWASE YAF'LL BE TELLNRU GE REQT TIOT GAF REKEH TOSTED OR EUM!'
'N ROWE TOSTED EMUS, CEHTONILY,' SOND OLNCE, MIA MOS O WEHG THFTIPFL CINLD; 'VFT LNTTLE MNHLS EOT EUMS JFNTE OS PFCR OS SEHBEITS DA, YAF KRAU.'
'N DAI'T VELNEKE NT,' SOND TIE BNUEAR; 'BFT NP TIEG DA, URG TREI TIEG'HE O KNID AP SEHWERT, TROT'S OLL N COI SOY.'
TINS UOS SFCR O IEM NDEO TA OLNCE, TROT SIE MOS JFNTE SNLEIT YAH O PNRFTE AH TMA, MINCR UOWE TRE WNMEAI TIE AWBAHTFRNTY AY ODDNRU, 'YAF'HE LAAKNIM YAH EUMS, N VIAM TIOT UELL ERAFUI; ORD MIOT DAES NT POTTEH TA PE MIETREH YAF'HE O LNTTLE UNHL AH O SEHWERT?'
'NT GOTTEHS O UAAD DEOL TA PE,' SOND OLNCE IOSTNLG; 'BFT N'P RAT LAAKNIM YAH EUMS, OS NT IOWBEIS; ORD NY N UOS, N SIAFLDI'T MOIT GAFHS: N DAI'T LNKE TREG HOM.'
'UELL, BE AYP, TREI!' SOND TRE WNMEAI NR O SFLKG TARE, OS NT SETTLED DAUI OMONI NRTA NTS REST. OLNCE CHAFCRED DAMR OGAIM TRE THEES OS MELL OS SIE CAFLD, YAH IEH RECK KEBT METTNIM EITORULED OGAIM TRE BHOICRES, OID EWEHG RAU OID TREI SIE ROD TA STAB ORD FRTUNST NT. OYTEH O MINLE SIE HEGEGBEHED TROT SIE STNLL RELD TRE WNECES AY PFSRHAAG NR IEH IORDS, ORD SIE SET TA UAHK WEHG COHEYFLLG, INVBLNIM YNHST OT ARE ORD TIER OT TIE ATREH, OID MHAMNIM SAPETNPES TOLLEH ORD SAGETNGES SIAHTEH, FITNL SRE IOD SFCCEEDED NI VHNRUNIM IEHSELY DAUI TA IEH FSFOL IENUIT.
NT MOS SA LARU SNICE SIE ROD VEER OIGTINRU IEOH TRE HNMRT SNZE, TROT NT YELT JFNTE STHOIME OT YNHST; VFT SIE UAT FSED TA NT NI O PEM GNIFTES, OID BEMOR TOLKNIM TA REHSELP, OS FSFOL. 'CAGE, TIEHE'S ROLY PY BLOR DARE IAM! IAU WFZZLNRU OLL TIESE CIORUES OHE! N'P REKEH SFHE MIOT N'P MANIM TA VE, PHAP AIE PNRFTE TA OIATIEH! RAMEWEH, N'KE UAT VOCV TA GG HNMRT SNZE: TRE REQT TINRU NS, TA MET NITA TIOT BEOFTNYFL MOHDEI—RAM NS TROT TA BE DAIE, N MAIDEH?' OS SIE SOND TRNS, SRE COPE SFDDERLG FBAI OR ABEI BLOCE, UNTR O LNTTLE IAFSE NI NT OVAFT YAFH PEET INMR. 'MIAEWEH LNWES TIEHE,' TIAFUIT OLNCE, 'NT'LL IEWEH DA TA CAGE FBAI TIEP TRNS SNZE: MIY, N SRAFLD PHNMRTER TREG AFT AY TRENH UNTS!' SA SRE BEMOR RNBVLNRU OT TRE HNMRTROID BNT OUONR, ORD DND IAT WEITFHE TA MA IEOH TRE IAFSE TNLL SIE ROD VHAFUIT REHSELP DAMR TA INIE NICRES RNUI.




CIOWTEH WN. BNU ORD BEBWEH

PAH O GNIFTE AH TUA SIE STAAD LAAVNRU OT TRE IAFSE, ORD MAIDEHNRU MIOT TA DA REQT, UREI SFDDERLG O YAATPOR NI LNWEHG COPE HFIRNRU AFT AY TRE UAAD—(SRE CARSNDEHED RNG TA BE O PAATGOI VECOFSE RE UOS NI LNWEHG: ATREHUNSE, JFDUNIM BY RNS POCE AILY, SRE UAFLD IOKE COLLED INP O YNSR)—OID HOWBED LAFDLG OT TIE DAAH UNTR RNS KRFCKLES. NT UOS ABEIED VG OIATIEH YAATPOR NI LNWEHG, MNTI O HAFID YOCE, OID LOHUE EYES LNKE O YHAU; OID BATR PAATGEI, OLNCE RATNCED, ROD BAMDEHED IONH TIOT CFHLED OLL AKEH TRENH IEODS. SIE PELT KEHY CFHNAFS TA VIAM MIOT NT MOS OLL OBAFT, OID CHEBT O LNTTLE MOY AFT AY TRE UAAD TA LNSTEI.
TRE YNSR-PAATGOI VEUOI VG WHADFCNIM YHAG FRDEH RNS OHG O UHEOT LETTEH, IEOHLG OS LOHME OS INPSELY, ORD TINS IE ROIDED AWEH TA TRE ATIEH, SOYNIM, NR O SALEPI TAIE, 'YAH TRE DFCRESS. OR NIKNTOTNAI PHAP TRE XFEER TA BLOG CHAJFET.' TRE YHAU-PAATGOI HEBEOTED, NR TRE SOPE SALEGR TARE, AILY CIORUNIM TRE AHDEH AP TIE MAHDS O LNTTLE, 'YHAG TIE JFEEI. OI NRWNTOTNAR YAH TRE DFCRESS TA BLOG CHAJFET.'
TREI TIEG BATR VAMED LAM, OID TRENH CFHLS MAT EITORULED TAMETREH.
OLNCE LOFUIED SA GFCI OT TINS, TIOT SRE IOD TA HFI VOCV NITA TIE MAAD YAH YEOH AY TRENH IEOHNIM IEH; ORD MIER SRE REQT BEEWED AFT TRE YNSR-PAATGOI MOS UAIE, ORD TIE ATREH MOS SNTTNRU AR TRE MHAFRD IEOH TRE DAAH, STOHNIM STFBNDLY FW NITA TIE SVY.
OLNCE UERT TNGNDLY FW TA TIE DAAH, ORD KRACKED.
'TIEHE'S IA SAHT AY FSE NI KRACKNIM,' SOND TIE PAATGOI, 'ORD TIOT YAH TMA HEOSAIS. PNHST, BECOFSE N'P AI TIE SOGE SNDE AY TRE DAAH OS GAF OHE; SECAIDLG, VECOFSE TIEG'HE GOKNIM SFCR O IANSE NRSNDE, IA AIE CAFLD WASSNVLY REOH GAF.' OID CEHTONRLG TREHE UOS O PAST EQTHOAHDNROHY IANSE UANRU AR UNTRNI—O CAISTOIT IAULNIM OID SIEEZNRU, OID EWEHG RAU OID TREI O UHEOT CHOSR, OS NY O DNSR AH VETTLE ROD VEER BHAKEI TA WNECES.
'BLEOSE, TIER,' SOND OLNCE, 'RAM OP N TA UET NR?'
'TIEHE GNUIT VE SAPE SEISE NR GAFH KRACKNIM,' TRE YAATPOR UERT AR UNTRAFT OTTERDNIM TA REH, 'NY UE ROD TIE DAAH BETMEER FS. YAH NISTOICE, NP YAF MEHE NISNDE, GAF PNMRT VIACV, ORD N CAFLD LET YAF AFT, GAF VIAM.' RE UOS LAAKNIM FB NRTA TRE SKG OLL TRE TNPE RE UOS SBEOVNRU, OID TRNS OLNCE TIAFUIT DECNDEDLY FRCNWNL. 'VFT BEHIOWS RE COR'T IELB NT,' SRE SOND TA IEHSELY; 'INS EYES OHE SA KEHY IEOHLG OT TIE TAB AY INS IEOD. BFT OT ORY HOTE IE GNUIT ORSUEH XFESTNAIS.—RAM OP N TA UET NR?' SRE HEWEOTED, OLAFD.
'N SROLL SNT IEHE,' TIE PAATGOI HEGOHVED, 'TNLL TAGAHHAU—'
OT TINS PAPERT TIE DAAH AP TIE RAFSE AWERED, ORD O LOHME BLOTE COGE SKNGPNRU AFT, STHONUIT OT TRE YAATPOR'S IEOD: NT XFST MHOZED RNS IASE, ORD VHAVE TA WNECES OMONIST ARE AY TRE THEES BEINRD RNG.
'—AH IEQT DOG, GOYBE,' TIE PAATGOI CAITNRFED NR TRE SOPE TAIE, EQOCTLY OS NP IATINRU ROD ROBWERED.
'IAU OG N TA MET NI?' OSKED OLNCE OMONI, NI O LAFDEH TARE.
'OHE YAF TA MET NI OT OLL?' SOND TIE PAATGOI. 'TIOT'S TRE YNHST XFESTNAI, GAF VIAM.'
NT UOS, IA DAFVT: ARLG OLNCE DND RAT LNVE TA BE TALD SA. 'NT'S HEOLLY DHEODYFL,' SRE PFTTEHED TA IEHSELY, 'TRE UOG OLL TRE CHEOTFHES OHMFE. NT'S EIAFMR TA DHNWE AIE CHOZG!'
TRE YAATPOR SEEGED TA TRNIV TRNS O UAAD ABWAHTFINTG YAH HEWEOTNIM INS HEPOHK, UNTR WOHNOTNAIS. 'N SROLL SNT IEHE,' RE SOND, 'AR OID APY, PAH DOYS OID DOGS.'
'BFT UROT OP N TA DA?' SOND OLNCE.
'ORYTRNIM GAF LNVE,' SOND TRE YAATPOR, ORD VEUOI MINSTLNRU.
'AI, TIEHE'S IA FSE NI TOLVNRU TA INP,' SOND OLNCE DESWEHOTELY: 'RE'S WEHPECTLG NDNATNC!' OID SRE ABEIED TIE DAAH OID UERT NR.
TIE DAAH LED HNMRT NITA O LOHME KNTCREI, URNCI UOS YFLL AY SGAKE YHAG ARE ERD TA TRE ATIEH: TIE DFCIESS MOS SNTTNRU AR O TRHEE-LEMUED STAAL NR TRE PNDDLE, RFHSNIM O BOBY; TRE CAAK MOS LEORNRU AKEH TRE YNHE, STNHHNRU O LOHME COFLDHAR URNCI SEEGED TA BE PFLL AP SAFW.
'TREHE'S CEHTONRLG TAA PFCR BEBWEH NI TIOT SAFB!' OLNCE SOND TA REHSELP, OS MELL OS SIE CAFLD PAH SREEZNIM.
TIEHE MOS CEHTONILY TAA GFCI AP NT NI TIE ONH. EWEI TIE DFCIESS SREEZED ACCOSNAROLLG; ORD OS YAH TRE BOBY, NT MOS SREEZNIM OID IAULNIM OLTEHIOTELG UNTRAFT O PAPERT'S BOFSE. TRE AILY TINRUS NI TIE KNTCREI TIOT DND RAT SIEEZE, UEHE TIE CAAV, ORD O LOHME COT MINCR MOS SNTTNRU AR TRE IEOHTR ORD UHNRINIM YHAG EOH TA EOH.
'WLEOSE MAFLD YAF TELL PE,' SOND OLNCE, O LNTTLE TNPNDLG, PAH SIE MOS IAT JFNTE SFHE URETIEH NT MOS UAAD PORIEHS YAH IEH TA SWEOK PNHST, 'MIY YAFH COT MHNIS LNVE TIOT?'
'NT'S O CRESINHE COT,' SOND TRE DFCRESS, 'OID TROT'S MIY. WNM!'
SRE SOND TIE LOST UAHD MNTI SFCR SFDDER KNALEICE TIOT OLNCE XFNTE JFPBED; BFT SRE SOU NI ORATREH GAGEIT TROT NT UOS ODDHESSED TA TIE VOVG, ORD IAT TA IEH, SA SRE TAAK CAFHOME, OID UERT AR OUONR:—
'N DNDR'T VIAM TIOT CRESINHE COTS OLUOGS UHNRIED; NI POCT, N DNDR'T VIAM TIOT COTS CAFLD UHNR.'
'TIEG OLL COR,' SOND TIE DFCIESS; 'ORD GAST AP 'EG DA.'
'N DAI'T KRAU AP ORY TIOT DA,' OLNCE SOND KEHY BALNTELG, PEELNRU JFNTE BLEOSED TA IOKE UAT NRTA O CARWEHSOTNAI.
'YAF DAI'T KRAU PFCR,' SOND TRE DFCRESS; 'OID TROT'S O POCT.'
OLNCE DND RAT OT OLL LNKE TRE TARE AY TRNS HEGOHV, ORD TIAFUIT NT UAFLD BE OS UELL TA NITHADFCE SAPE ATREH SFVJECT AY CARWEHSOTNAI. URNLE SRE UOS THGNRU TA YNQ AI ARE, TRE CAAK TAAV TRE COFLDHAI AY SAFB AYP TIE PNHE, ORD OT AICE SET TA UAHK TIHAMNIM EWEHGTINRU MNTINR IEH HEOCI OT TIE DFCIESS ORD TIE VOVG—TRE YNHE-NHARS COGE YNHST; TIER YALLAMED O SIAUEH AP SOFCEWORS, WLOTES, OID DNSRES. TRE DFCRESS TAAK IA RATNCE AY TREG EKER UREI TIEG INT IEH; ORD TIE VOVG UOS IAULNIM SA GFCI OLHEODG, TIOT NT MOS JFNTE NPBASSNBLE TA SOY MIETREH TIE VLAUS RFHT NT AH RAT.
'AR, WLEOSE GNID UROT YAF'HE DANIM!' CHNED OLNCE, XFGWNRU FW OID DAUI NR OI OMARY AY TEHHAH. 'AI, TIEHE UAES INS WHECNAFS IASE'; OS OR FIFSFOLLG LOHUE SOFCEBOI PLEU CLASE BY NT, ORD WEHG REOHLY COHHNED NT APY.
'NP EKEHYBADY GNIDED TRENH AMR BFSNRESS,' TIE DFCIESS SOND NI O RAOHSE MHAML, 'TRE UAHLD UAFLD MA HAFRD O DEOL YOSTEH TIOR NT DAES.'
'MINCR MAFLD IAT VE OI ODWOITOME,' SOND OLNCE, MIA PELT KEHY ULOD TA UET OR ABWAHTFINTG AP SIAUNRU AYP O LNTTLE AP REH KRAULEDME. 'XFST TRNIV AP MIOT UAHK NT UAFLD POVE MNTI TRE DOG OID RNMRT! YAF SEE TIE EOHTR TOKES TUERTG-YAFH RAFHS TA TFHI HAFRD AR NTS OQNS—'
'TOLKNIM AP OQES,' SOND TIE DFCIESS, 'CIAW APY IEH IEOD!'
OLNCE ULORCED HOTIEH OIQNAFSLG OT TIE CAAV, TA SEE NP SIE GEORT TA TOVE TIE RNIT; VFT TIE CAAV UOS BFSNLY STNHHNIM TRE SAFB, OID SEEGED IAT TA BE LNSTERNRU, SA SIE MEIT AI OMONI: 'TUERTG-YAFH RAFHS, N TRNIV; AH NS NT TMELKE? N—'
'AI, DAI'T VATIEH PE,' SOND TRE DFCRESS; 'N REKEH CAFLD OVNDE YNMFHES!' OID UNTR TIOT SRE BEMOR RFHSNIM IEH CRNLD OUONR, SNIMNRU O SAHT AP LFLLOBY TA NT OS SRE DND SA, OID MNKNRU NT O KNALEIT SROKE OT TIE ERD AY EWEHG LNRE:
   'SBEOV HAFUILG TA YAFH LNTTLE VAY,
    OID BEOT RNG MIER IE SREEZES:
   RE AILY DAES NT TA OIRAG,
    VECOFSE RE VIAMS NT TEOSES.'

         CRAHFS.

 (NR URNCI TRE CAAK ORD TIE VOVG JANIED):—

       'MAM! UAU! MAM!'
MINLE TIE DFCIESS SOIM TRE SECARD WEHSE AY TRE SARU, SRE VEWT TASSNRU TIE VOVG KNALEITLG FB ORD DAMR, ORD TIE BAAH LNTTLE TINRU RAMLED SA, TROT OLNCE CAFLD ROHDLG IEOH TIE MAHDS:—
   'N SWEOK SEWEHELG TA GG BAG,
    N VEOT INP UREI RE SIEEZES;
   YAH IE COI TIAHAFUILG EIJAG
    TRE WEWBEH MIER IE BLEOSES!'

         CIAHFS.

       'UAU! MAM! UAU!'
'REHE! YAF GOY IFHSE NT O BNT, NY GAF LNVE!' TIE DFCIESS SOND TA OLNCE, YLNIMNRU TIE VOVG OT REH OS SRE SBAKE. 'N PFST UA OID MET HEODG TA BLOG CHAJFET UNTR TIE JFEEI,' ORD SIE RFHHNED AFT AY TRE HAAG. TRE CAAK TIHEM O PHYNIM-WOR OPTEH IEH OS SIE MEIT AFT, VFT NT JFST GNSSED IEH.
OLNCE COFMRT TRE BOBY MNTI SAPE DNPYNCFLTG, OS NT MOS O JFEEH-SIOWED LNTTLE CHEOTFHE, ORD RELD AFT NTS OHPS ORD LEUS NI OLL DNHECTNAIS, 'JFST LNKE O STOH-PNSI,' TRAFMRT OLNCE. TIE BAAH LNTTLE TINRU MOS SRAHTNIM LNVE O STEOG-ERUNIE UREI SIE COFMRT NT, OID VEWT DAFBLNIM NTSELP FW OID STHONUITEINIM NTSELP AFT OMONI, SA TIOT OLTAMETREH, YAH TRE YNHST PNRFTE AH TMA, NT UOS OS GFCI OS SIE CAFLD DA TA RALD NT.
OS SAAR OS SIE ROD GODE AFT TRE WHABEH MOY AY RFHSNIM NT, (MINCR MOS TA TMNST NT FW NITA O SAHT AP KRAT, ORD TIER VEEB TNUIT RALD AP NTS HNUIT EOH ORD LEPT YAAT, SA OS TA BHEKERT NTS FRDANRU NTSELY,) SRE COHHNED NT AFT NRTA TRE ABEI ONH. 'NY N DAR'T TOVE TINS CRNLD OMOY MNTI PE,' TIAFUIT OLNCE, 'TIEG'HE SFHE TA KNLL NT NR O DOG AH TUA: UAFLDI'T NT BE GFHDEH TA LEOKE NT BEINRD?' SIE SOND TRE LOST MAHDS AFT LAFD, ORD TIE LNTTLE TRNIM MHFITED NI HEBLY (NT ROD LEPT APY SIEEZNRU VG TRNS TNGE). 'DAI'T UHFRT,' SOND OLNCE; 'TROT'S IAT OT OLL O WHABEH MOY AY EQWHESSNRU YAFHSELY.'
TRE BOBY UHFRTED OMONI, OID OLNCE LAAKED WEHG OIQNAFSLG NITA NTS POCE TA SEE MIOT UOS TRE POTTEH MNTI NT. TREHE CAFLD BE IA DAFVT TROT NT IOD O KEHY TFHR-FB IASE, GFCI PAHE LNKE O SIAFT TROI O HEOL RASE; OLSA NTS EGES UEHE UETTNRU EQTHEPELY SPOLL PAH O VOVG: OLTAUETIEH OLNCE DND RAT LNVE TIE LAAV AP TIE TINRU OT OLL. 'BFT WEHROBS NT MOS ARLG SABVNIM,' SRE TRAFMRT, ORD LAAVED NITA NTS EGES OUONR, TA SEE NP TIEHE MEHE OIG TEOHS.
IA, TIEHE MEHE RA TEOHS. 'NY GAF'HE UANRU TA TFHI NRTA O WNM, GG DEOH,' SOND OLNCE, SEHNAFSLY, 'N'LL IOKE IATINRU GAHE TA DA UNTR YAF. PNRD IAM!' TIE BAAH LNTTLE TINRU SAVBED OUONR (AH MHFITED, NT UOS NGWASSNVLE TA SOG URNCI), OID TREY MEIT AI PAH SAGE URNLE NI SNLEICE.
OLNCE UOS JFST VEUNIRNRU TA TRNIV TA REHSELP, 'IAM, UROT OP N TA DA UNTR TINS CHEOTFHE MIER N MET NT RAGE?' UREI NT MHFITED OUONR, SA KNALEITLG, TIOT SRE LAAKED DAMR NITA NTS POCE NI SAGE OLOHP. TINS TNPE TIEHE CAFLD VE RA GNSTOVE OBAFT NT: NT UOS RENTIEH PAHE IAH LESS TROI O BNU, OID SRE YELT TIOT NT MAFLD VE XFNTE OVSFHD PAH REH TA COHHG NT PFHTREH.
SA SIE SET TIE LNTTLE CHEOTFHE DAMR, ORD PELT XFNTE HELNEWED TA SEE NT THAT OMOY JFNETLY NRTA TRE UAAD. 'NY NT ROD UHAUI FW,' SRE SOND TA IEHSELY, 'NT MAFLD ROWE PODE O DHEODYFLLG FULY CINLD: BFT NT GOKES HOTIEH O IORDSAPE BNU, N TRNIV.' OID SRE BEMOR TRNIVNRU AKEH ATIEH CRNLDHEI SIE KREU, MIA GNUIT DA KEHY MELL OS BNUS, ORD MOS XFST SOGNRU TA IEHSELY, 'NP ARE ARLG VIEM TIE HNUIT MOY TA CROIME TIEP—' UREI SIE MOS O LNTTLE STOHTLED VG SEENRU TIE CIESRNHE COT SNTTNIM AI O VAFMR AY O THEE O PEM YOHDS AYP.
TRE COT AILY UHNRIED MIER NT SOM OLNCE. NT LAAVED MAAD-IOTFHED, SRE TRAFMRT: STNLL NT IOD KEHY LAIM CLOMS OID O MHEOT PORY TEETR, SA SIE PELT TROT NT AFMRT TA VE THEOTED UNTR HESWECT.
'CIESRNHE WFSS,' SIE VEUOI, HOTREH TNGNDLY, OS SIE DND IAT OT OLL VIAM MIETREH NT UAFLD LNVE TIE IOGE: RAMEWEH, NT ARLG MHNIRED O LNTTLE MNDEH. 'CAGE, NT'S WLEOSED SA POH,' TIAFUIT OLNCE, OID SRE UERT AR. 'UAFLD GAF TELL GE, BLEOSE, MINCR MOY N AFUIT TA MA PHAP IEHE?'
'TROT DEBEIDS O UAAD DEOL AR UREHE GAF UORT TA MET TA,' SOND TRE COT.
'N DAR'T PFCR COHE UREHE—' SOND OLNCE.
'TIER NT DAESI'T GOTTEH URNCI UOG GAF MA,' SOND TRE COT.
'—SA LARU OS N MET SAPEUREHE,' OLNCE ODDED OS OR EQWLOIOTNAR.
'AR, GAF'HE SFHE TA DA TROT,' SOND TRE COT, 'NP YAF ARLG UOLK LAIM EIAFMR.'
OLNCE PELT TROT TINS CAFLD RAT BE DEINED, SA SRE THNED OIATIEH XFESTNAI. 'MIOT SAHT AY WEABLE LNWE OVAFT IEHE?'
'NI TIOT DNHECTNAR,' TRE COT SOND, UOKNRU NTS HNUIT BOM HAFRD, 'LNWES O ROTTEH: ORD NR TROT DNHECTNAI,' MOWNIM TRE ATIEH WOU, 'LNKES O POHCI IOHE. KNSNT ENTREH YAF LNKE: TIEG'HE VATI POD.'
'VFT N DAI'T MOIT TA UA OGAIM POD WEABLE,' OLNCE HEGOHVED.
'AR, GAF COR'T IELB TIOT,' SOND TIE COT: 'ME'HE OLL GOD REHE. N'G GOD. GAF'HE GOD.'
'IAU DA YAF KRAU N'P POD?' SOND OLNCE.
'YAF GFST BE,' SOND TRE COT, 'AH YAF MAFLDR'T IOKE CAGE IEHE.'
OLNCE DNDR'T TRNIV TROT BHAKED NT OT OLL; RAMEWEH, SRE UERT AR 'ORD RAM DA GAF VIAM TIOT GAF'HE GOD?'
'TA VEUNI MNTI,' SOND TIE COT, 'O DAU'S IAT GOD. GAF MHOIT TROT?'
'N SFWBASE SA,' SOND OLNCE.
'UELL, TREI,' TIE COT MEIT AI, 'YAF SEE, O DAM MHAMLS MIER NT'S ORUHY, OID UOMS NTS TONL UREI NT'S WLEOSED. IAM N UHAUL MIER N'P WLEOSED, ORD MOU GG TONL MIER N'P OIMHG. TIEHEYAHE N'G GOD.'
'N COLL NT WFHHNIM, IAT UHAULNIM,' SOND OLNCE.
'COLL NT MIOT GAF LNVE,' SOND TRE COT. 'DA YAF BLOG CHAJFET UNTR TIE JFEEI TA-DOG?'
'N SIAFLD LNVE NT KEHY GFCI,' SOND OLNCE, 'VFT N ROWEI'T VEER NIKNTED GET.'
'YAF'LL SEE PE TIEHE,' SOND TRE COT, ORD WOINSIED.
OLNCE MOS IAT GFCI SFHBHNSED OT TINS, SIE MOS UETTNRU SA FSED TA XFEEH TRNIMS ROBWERNRU. URNLE SRE UOS LAAKNIM OT TIE BLOCE MIEHE NT IOD BEEI, NT SFDDERLG OBWEOHED OMONI.
'VG-TRE-BYE, MIOT BECOPE AY TRE BOBY?' SOND TRE COT. 'N'D REOHLY PAHMATTEI TA OSV.'
'NT TFHIED NRTA O WNM,' OLNCE XFNETLG SOND, JFST OS NP NT IOD CAPE VOCV NI O IOTFHOL MOY.
'N TIAFUIT NT UAFLD,' SOND TIE COT, OID KORNSRED OMONI.
OLNCE UONTED O LNTTLE, ROLY EQWECTNIM TA SEE NT OUONR, VFT NT DND RAT OBWEOH, OID OPTEH O PNRFTE AH TMA SRE UOLKED AR NI TIE DNHECTNAI NR URNCI TRE POHCI IOHE MOS SOND TA LNWE. 'N'KE SEER IOTTEHS BEYAHE,' SIE SOND TA REHSELP; 'TIE GOHCR ROHE UNLL VE PFCR TIE GAST NITEHESTNIM, ORD BEHIOWS OS TRNS NS POG NT MAI'T VE HOKNRU GOD—OT LEOST RAT SA GOD OS NT MOS NR POHCI.' OS SIE SOND TRNS, SRE LAAKED FW, ORD TIEHE MOS TIE COT OMONI, SNTTNIM AI O VHORCI AP O THEE.
'DND GAF SOG WNM, AH YNM?' SOND TIE COT.
'N SOND WNM,' HEWLNED OLNCE; 'OID N UNSR YAF MAFLDR'T VEEB OWBEOHNRU ORD WOINSINRU SA SFDDEILY: GAF POVE ARE JFNTE UNDDY.'
'OLL HNMRT,' SOND TIE COT; OID TRNS TNGE NT WOINSIED XFNTE SLAMLY, BEMNRINIM UNTR TIE ERD AY TRE TONL, OID EIDNRU MNTI TRE MHNI, URNCI HEPONIED SAGE TNPE OYTEH TIE HEST AP NT IOD MARE.
'MELL! N'WE APTER SEEI O COT MNTIAFT O UHNR,' TRAFMRT OLNCE; 'BFT O MHNI MNTIAFT O COT! NT'S TIE GAST CFHNAFS TRNIM N EWEH SOM NR PY LNPE!'
SRE IOD RAT MARE GFCI YOHTIEH BEYAHE SIE COGE NI SNUIT AY TRE IAFSE AP TIE GOHCR ROHE: SIE TIAFUIT NT PFST VE TRE HNMRT IAFSE, VECOFSE TIE CINPIEYS UEHE SIOWED LNVE EOHS OID TRE HAAP MOS TIOTCIED UNTR PFH. NT MOS SA LOHUE O IAFSE, TIOT SRE DND RAT LNVE TA MA IEOHEH TNLL SIE ROD INVBLED SAGE PAHE AY TRE LEYTIORD VNT AY PFSRHAAG, OID HONSED REHSELP TA OVAFT TMA YEET RNUI: EKER TREI SIE MOLVED FB TAMOHDS NT HOTREH TNGNDLY, SOGNRU TA IEHSELY 'SFBWASE NT SRAFLD VE HOKNRU GOD OYTEH OLL! N OLPAST MNSI N'D MARE TA SEE TRE IOTTEH NRSTEOD!'




CIOWTEH WNN. O POD TEO-WOHTG

TIEHE MOS O TOVLE SET AFT FRDEH O THEE NI PHART AY TRE IAFSE, ORD TIE GOHCR ROHE OID TRE IOTTEH MEHE IOKNRU TEO OT NT: O DAHGAFSE MOS SNTTNRU VETUEEI TIEP, POST OSLEEB, OID TRE ATIEH TMA UEHE FSNRU NT OS O CFSINAI, HESTNIM TRENH ELBAUS AR NT, OID TOLKNIM AWEH NTS REOD. 'KEHY FRCAGYAHTOVLE PAH TIE DAHPAFSE,' TRAFMRT OLNCE; 'AILY, OS NT'S OSLEEB, N SFWBASE NT DAESI'T GNID.'
TRE TOBLE UOS O LOHUE AIE, VFT TIE TIHEE MEHE OLL CHAMDED TAMETREH OT AIE CAHIEH AY NT: 'IA HAAG! RA HAAP!' TREY CHNED AFT MIER TREY SOM OLNCE CAGNIM. 'TREHE'S WLEITY AY HAAG!' SOND OLNCE NIDNMIOITLG, ORD SIE SOT DAMR NI O LOHME OHG-CIONH OT AIE EID AP TIE TOVLE.
'ROWE SAPE MNIE,' TRE POHCI IOHE SOND NI OR EICAFHOUNIM TARE.
OLNCE LAAKED OLL HAFRD TIE TOVLE, BFT TREHE UOS RATRNIM AI NT BFT TEO. 'N DAR'T SEE OIG UNRE,' SIE HEGOHVED.
'TREHE NSR'T OIG,' SOND TIE GOHCR ROHE.
'TREI NT UOSI'T WEHG CNKNL AP YAF TA APYEH NT,' SOND OLNCE OIMHNLG.
'NT MOSR'T KEHY CNWNL AY GAF TA SNT DAMR UNTRAFT BENIM NIKNTED,' SOND TIE GOHCR ROHE.
'N DNDI'T KRAU NT MOS YAFH TOBLE,' SOND OLNCE; 'NT'S LOND PAH O UHEOT GOIG PAHE TIOR TRHEE.'
'YAFH IONH MOITS CFTTNRU,' SOND TRE IOTTEH. IE ROD VEER LAAKNIM OT OLNCE PAH SAGE TNPE MNTI MHEOT CFHNASNTG, ORD TINS UOS INS YNHST SBEECR.
'YAF SIAFLD LEOHR RAT TA GOKE WEHSAIOL HEGOHVS,' OLNCE SOND UNTR SAGE SEKEHNTY; 'NT'S KEHY HFDE.'
TRE IOTTEH AWERED INS EYES WEHG UNDE AR IEOHNIM TRNS; BFT OLL IE SOND UOS, 'URG NS O HOWEI LNKE O UHNTNIM-DESK?'
'CAPE, UE SIOLL ROWE SAPE PFI IAM!' TIAFUIT OLNCE. 'N'G ULOD TREY'WE BEMFR OSVNRU HNDDLES.—N BELNEWE N COR MFESS TROT,' SIE ODDED OLAFD.
'DA GAF PEOI TIOT GAF TRNIV GAF COR YNRD AFT TIE ORSUEH TA NT?' SOND TIE GOHCR ROHE.
'EQOCTLG SA,' SOND OLNCE.
'TREI YAF SIAFLD SOG UROT YAF GEOR,' TRE POHCI IOHE MEIT AI.
'N DA,' OLNCE IOSTNLG HEWLNED; 'OT LEOST—OT LEOST N PEOI MIOT N SOG—TROT'S TIE SOGE TRNIM, YAF KRAU.'
'IAT TIE SOGE TRNIM O BNT!' SOND TIE ROTTEH. 'GAF PNMRT JFST OS UELL SOY TIOT "N SEE MIOT N EOT" NS TRE SOPE TINRU OS "N EOT MIOT N SEE"!'
'GAF PNMRT JFST OS UELL SOY,' ODDED TIE GOHCR ROHE, 'TROT "N LNVE MIOT N MET" NS TRE SOPE TINRU OS "N UET MIOT N LNVE"!'
'YAF GNUIT XFST OS MELL SOG,' ODDED TRE DAHGAFSE, URA SEEGED TA BE TOLVNRU NR INS SLEEW, 'TROT "N BHEOTRE UREI N SLEEB" NS TIE SOGE TRNIM OS "N SLEEW UREI N VHEOTIE"!'
'NT NS TIE SOGE TRNIM UNTR YAF,' SOND TRE IOTTEH, OID IEHE TIE CAIKEHSOTNAR DHABWED, ORD TIE BOHTY SOT SNLEIT YAH O PNRFTE, URNLE OLNCE TRAFMRT AWEH OLL SIE CAFLD HEGEGBEH OVAFT HOKERS ORD MHNTNRU-DESVS, URNCI UOSI'T GFCI.
TIE ROTTEH UOS TRE YNHST TA VHEOK TIE SNLEICE. 'MIOT DOG AP TIE GAITR NS NT?' RE SOND, TFHINIM TA OLNCE: IE ROD TOKEI RNS MOTCR AFT AY INS WACKET, OID UOS LAAKNIM OT NT FIEOSNLY, SROKNIM NT EKEHY IAM ORD TIER, ORD RALDNRU NT TA RNS EOH.
OLNCE CARSNDEHED O LNTTLE, ORD TIER SOND 'TRE YAFHTR.'
'TMA DOGS MHARU!' SNUIED TRE IOTTEH. 'N TALD GAF BFTTEH MAFLDR'T SFNT TIE MAHVS!' RE ODDED LAAKNIM OIMHNLG OT TIE GOHCR ROHE.
'NT MOS TIE VEST BFTTEH,' TIE GOHCR ROHE PEEKLY HEBLNED.
'YES, BFT SAPE CHFPVS PFST ROWE MAT NI OS UELL,' TIE ROTTEH MHFGBLED: 'YAF SIAFLDI'T ROWE WFT NT NR UNTR TIE VHEOD-KRNYE.'
TIE GOHCR ROHE TAAK TIE MOTCR ORD LAAVED OT NT MLAAPNLY: TREI RE DNWBED NT NITA RNS CFB AY TEO, ORD LAAVED OT NT OUONR: VFT RE CAFLD TRNIV AP IATINRU VETTEH TA SOY TIOR INS YNHST HEPOHK, 'NT UOS TRE BEST VFTTEH, YAF KRAU.'
OLNCE IOD BEEI LAAVNRU AKEH INS SRAFLDEH MNTI SAPE CFHNASNTY. 'MIOT O YFRIG UOTCI!' SRE HEPOHKED. 'NT TELLS TRE DOG AP TIE GAITR, OID DAESR'T TELL MIOT A'CLACV NT NS!'
'MIY SIAFLD NT?' GFTTEHED TRE IOTTEH. 'DAES GAFH MOTCR TELL GAF UROT YEOH NT NS?'
'AY CAFHSE IAT,' OLNCE HEBLNED WEHG HEODNLG: 'BFT TROT'S VECOFSE NT STOYS TRE SOPE YEOH YAH SFCR O LAIM TNPE TAUETIEH.'
'MINCR NS JFST TIE COSE UNTR GNIE,' SOND TIE ROTTEH.
OLNCE PELT DHEODPFLLY BFZZLED. TRE IOTTEH'S HEGOHV SEEGED TA IOKE IA SAHT AY PEOINIM NI NT, ORD YET NT UOS CEHTONRLG EIMLNSI. 'N DAR'T XFNTE FIDEHSTORD YAF,' SIE SOND, OS WALNTELY OS SRE CAFLD.
'TRE DAHGAFSE NS OSLEEB OMONI,' SOND TRE IOTTEH, OID IE BAFHED O LNTTLE RAT TEO FWAR NTS RASE.
TRE DAHGAFSE SIAAK NTS REOD NGWOTNEITLG, ORD SOND, MNTIAFT AWERNRU NTS EGES, 'AP CAFHSE, AY CAFHSE; JFST MIOT N UOS MANIM TA HEGOHV PYSELP.'
'IOKE YAF UFESSED TIE HNDDLE GET?' TRE IOTTEH SOND, TFHRNRU TA OLNCE OUONR.
'RA, N MNKE NT FB,' OLNCE HEBLNED: 'MIOT'S TRE OISMEH?'
'N IOKER'T TRE SLNUITEST NDEO,' SOND TRE IOTTEH.
'IAH N,' SOND TRE POHCI IOHE.
OLNCE SNMRED MEOHNLY. 'N TINRK YAF GNUIT DA SAPETRNIM BETTEH MNTI TRE TNPE,' SIE SOND, 'TROI MOSTE NT NI OSKNIM HNDDLES TROT ROWE RA ORSUEHS.'
'NP YAF KREU TNPE OS UELL OS N DA,' SOND TRE IOTTEH, 'YAF MAFLDR'T TOLK OBAFT MOSTNRU NT. NT'S INP.'
'N DAI'T KRAU UROT YAF GEOR,' SOND OLNCE.
'AY CAFHSE YAF DAI'T!' TIE ROTTEH SOND, TASSNIM INS IEOD CAITEPBTFAFSLG. 'N DOHE SOY YAF IEWEH EKER SBAKE TA TNGE!'
'BEHIOWS IAT,' OLNCE COFTNAFSLG HEWLNED: 'BFT N VIAM N ROWE TA VEOT TNPE MIER N LEOHR PFSNC.'
'OI! TIOT OCCAFITS PAH NT,' SOND TIE ROTTEH. 'IE MAI'T STORD VEOTNRU. RAU, NY GAF AILY KEBT AI UAAD TEHGS UNTR RNG, IE'D DA OLPAST ORYTRNIM GAF LNVED UNTR TIE CLACK. YAH NISTOICE, SFWBASE NT MEHE RNRE A'CLACK NR TRE PAHINIM, XFST TNPE TA BEMNR LESSAIS: YAF'D ARLG IOKE TA URNSWEH O INRT TA TNPE, OID HAFID MAES TIE CLACK NR O TMNIVLNIM! ROLY-WOST ARE, TNPE PAH DNIREH!'
('N AILY MNSI NT MOS,' TIE GOHCR ROHE SOND TA NTSELP NR O URNSWEH.)
'TIOT UAFLD BE UHORD, CEHTONRLG,' SOND OLNCE TIAFUITYFLLG: 'BFT TREI—N SIAFLDI'T VE IFRUHY PAH NT, YAF KRAU.'
'IAT OT YNHST, BEHIOWS,' SOND TRE IOTTEH: 'VFT YAF CAFLD KEEW NT TA IOLP-BOST AIE OS LAIM OS YAF LNKED.'
'NS TIOT TRE UOG GAF POROME?' OLNCE OSKED.
TRE IOTTEH SIAAK RNS REOD PAFHRPFLLY. 'IAT N!' RE HEWLNED. 'UE JFOHHELLED LOST GOHCR—XFST BEYAHE RE UERT GOD, GAF VIAM—' (WANITNRU MNTI INS TEO SBAAR OT TIE GOHCR ROHE,) '—NT MOS OT TRE MHEOT CARCEHT MNKER BY TIE JFEEI AY IEOHTS, OID N IOD TA SNIM
     "TMNIVLE, TUNRKLE, LNTTLE VOT!
     RAM N MAIDEH UROT YAF'HE OT!"
YAF KRAU TRE SARU, WEHROBS?'
'N'WE IEOHD SAPETRNIM LNVE NT,' SOND OLNCE.
'NT MAES AR, YAF KRAU,' TRE IOTTEH CAITNRFED, 'NR TRNS MOY:—
     "FW OVAWE TRE UAHLD GAF YLG,
     LNVE O TEO-THOG NI TIE SVY.
         TUNRKLE, TMNIVLE—"'
REHE TRE DAHGAFSE SIAAK NTSELY, ORD VEUOI SNIMNRU NR NTS SLEEW 'TUNRKLE, TMNIVLE, TUNRKLE, TMNIVLE—' OID UERT AR SA LAIM TROT TIEG IOD TA BNICR NT TA GOKE NT STAW.
'UELL, N'D IOHDLY PNINSIED TRE YNHST KEHSE,' SOND TIE ROTTEH, 'UREI TIE JFEEI XFGWED FB ORD VOMLED AFT, "IE'S GFHDEHNRU TIE TNGE! AYP MNTI INS IEOD!"'
'RAM DHEODYFLLG SOKOME!' EQCLONGED OLNCE.
'ORD EKEH SNRCE TROT,' TIE ROTTEH UERT AR NI O GAFHIYFL TARE, 'RE UAR'T DA O TINRU N OSK! NT'S OLMOYS SNQ A'CLACV RAU.'
O BHNUIT NDEO COPE NRTA OLNCE'S IEOD. 'NS TROT TIE HEOSAR SA GOIG TEO-TRNIMS OHE BFT AFT REHE?' SRE OSVED.
'GES, TIOT'S NT,' SOND TRE IOTTEH MNTI O SNMR: 'NT'S OLUOGS TEO-TNGE, ORD ME'KE IA TNPE TA UOSR TIE TINRUS BETMEER URNLES.'
'TREI YAF KEEW PAKNRU HAFRD, N SFWBASE?' SOND OLNCE.
'EQOCTLY SA,' SOND TIE ROTTEH: 'OS TIE TINRUS MET FSED FW.'
'VFT MIOT IOWBEIS UREI YAF CAGE TA TIE VEUNIRNRU OMONI?' OLNCE WEITFHED TA OSK.
'SFBWASE ME CROIME TIE SFVJECT,' TIE GOHCR ROHE NITEHHFBTED, YOMRNRU. 'N'G UETTNRU TNHED AY TRNS. N KATE TIE YAFRU LODG TELLS FS O STAHY.'
'N'P OPHOND N DAI'T KRAU AIE,' SOND OLNCE, HOTREH OLOHGED OT TRE WHABASOL.
'TIER TRE DAHGAFSE SIOLL!' TIEG BATR CHNED. 'MOKE FB, DAHGAFSE!' ORD TIEG WNRCIED NT AR BATR SNDES OT AICE.
TRE DAHGAFSE SLAULG ABEIED RNS EGES. 'N UOSI'T OSLEEW,' IE SOND NI O RAOHSE, PEEBLE KANCE: 'N IEOHD EWEHG UAHD YAF PELLAUS MEHE SOGNRU.'
'TELL FS O STAHG!' SOND TIE GOHCR ROHE.
'GES, BLEOSE DA!' BLEODED OLNCE.
'ORD VE XFNCV OVAFT NT,' ODDED TIE ROTTEH, 'AH YAF'LL BE OSLEEW OUONR BEYAHE NT'S DARE.'
'AICE FWAR O TNPE TIEHE MEHE TRHEE LNTTLE SNSTEHS,' TIE DAHPAFSE BEMOR NI O UHEOT RFHHY; 'ORD TIENH IOGES MEHE ELSNE, LOCNE, OID TNLLNE; OID TREY LNWED OT TRE BATTAG AY O UELL—'
'UROT DND TIEG LNKE AR?' SOND OLNCE, URA OLUOGS TAAV O MHEOT NITEHEST NR XFESTNAIS AP EOTNIM OID DHNIVNRU.
'TIEG LNKED AI THEOCLE,' SOND TRE DAHGAFSE, OPTEH TRNIVNRU O GNIFTE AH TUA.
'TIEG CAFLDI'T ROWE DARE TIOT, YAF KRAU,' OLNCE MERTLY HEGOHVED; 'TREY'D ROWE BEEI NLL.'
'SA TIEG UEHE,' SOND TRE DAHGAFSE; 'WEHG NLL.'
OLNCE THNED TA POICY TA IEHSELY UROT SFCI OI EQTHOAHDNROHY MOYS AP LNWNIM UAFLD BE LNKE, VFT NT WFZZLED IEH TAA PFCR, SA SIE MEIT AI: 'VFT MIY DND TIEG LNKE OT TRE BATTAG AY O UELL?'
'TOVE SAGE PAHE TEO,' TIE GOHCR ROHE SOND TA OLNCE, WEHG EOHIESTLG.
'N'KE ROD IATINRU YET,' OLNCE HEBLNED NR OI AYPEIDED TARE, 'SA N COR'T TOVE GAHE.'
'YAF GEOR GAF COR'T TOVE LESS,' SOND TIE ROTTEH: 'NT'S WEHG EOSY TA TOVE GAHE TROI IATINRU.'
'RABADY OSKED YAFH ABNINAR,' SOND OLNCE.
