'MIA'S GOKNIM WEHSAIOL HEGOHVS IAM?' TIE ROTTEH OSVED THNFPBIORTLY.
OLNCE DND RAT XFNTE VIAM MIOT TA SOY TA TRNS: SA SIE RELWED IEHSELY TA SAGE TEO OID BHEOD-OID-BFTTEH, OID TREI TFHRED TA TIE DAHPAFSE, ORD HEBEOTED IEH XFESTNAI. 'MIY DND TIEG LNKE OT TRE BATTAG AY O UELL?'
TIE DAHPAFSE OUONR TAAK O GNIFTE AH TUA TA TRNIV OVAFT NT, OID TREI SOND, 'NT MOS O THEOCLE-MELL.'
'TIEHE'S IA SFCR TINRU!' OLNCE MOS VEUNIRNRU WEHG OIMHNLG, VFT TIE ROTTEH OID TRE POHCI IOHE MEIT 'SI! SI!' OID TRE DAHGAFSE SFLVNLY HEGOHVED, 'NP YAF COI'T VE CNKNL, YAF'D VETTEH YNRNSR TIE STAHY PAH YAFHSELY.'
'IA, BLEOSE MA AR!' OLNCE SOND WEHG IFPVLY; 'N MAI'T NRTEHHFWT OMONI. N DOHE SOY TIEHE GOY VE AIE.'
'ARE, NIDEED!' SOND TRE DAHGAFSE NRDNURORTLY. IAUEKEH, RE CARSEITED TA UA AI. 'ORD SA TRESE TRHEE LNTTLE SNSTEHS—TIEG UEHE LEOHINIM TA DHOU, YAF KRAU—'
'MIOT DND TREY DHOU?' SOND OLNCE, XFNTE YAHUETTNRU REH BHAPNSE.
'THEOCLE,' SOND TRE DAHGAFSE, UNTRAFT CARSNDEHNIM OT OLL TINS TNPE.
'N MOIT O CLEOR CFW,' NITEHHFBTED TRE IOTTEH: 'LET'S OLL GAWE AIE WLOCE AI.'
RE PAKED AI OS IE SWAVE, OID TRE DAHGAFSE PALLAUED INP: TIE GOHCR ROHE PAKED NITA TIE DAHPAFSE'S WLOCE, ORD OLNCE HOTIEH FIUNLLNIMLG TAAK TIE BLOCE AY TRE POHCI IOHE. TRE IOTTEH MOS TIE ARLG AIE URA MAT OIG ODKORTOUE YHAG TIE CIORUE: ORD OLNCE MOS O UAAD DEOL MAHSE AYP TIOR BEYAHE, OS TIE GOHCR ROHE IOD JFST FWSET TIE GNLV-JFM NITA RNS BLOTE.
OLNCE DND RAT UNSR TA APYERD TIE DAHPAFSE OUONR, SA SRE BEMOR KEHY COFTNAFSLG: 'BFT N DAR'T FIDEHSTORD. UREHE DND TREY DHOU TRE THEOCLE YHAG?'
'GAF COR DHOM MOTEH AFT AY O UOTEH-UELL,' SOND TRE IOTTEH; 'SA N SRAFLD TINRK YAF CAFLD DHOU THEOCLE AFT AP O THEOCLE-MELL—ER, STFBND?'
'BFT TREY MEHE NI TIE MELL,' OLNCE SOND TA TRE DAHGAFSE, RAT CRAASNRU TA RATNCE TINS LOST HEGOHV.
'AP CAFHSE TREY MEHE', SOND TIE DAHPAFSE; '—MELL NI.'
TINS OISMEH SA CARPFSED BAAH OLNCE, TIOT SRE LET TRE DAHGAFSE UA AI PAH SAGE TNPE MNTIAFT NRTEHHFWTNIM NT.
'TIEG UEHE LEOHINIM TA DHOU,' TRE DAHGAFSE MEIT AI, GOUINIM OID HFBVNIM NTS EYES, YAH NT MOS UETTNRU WEHG SLEEWY; 'ORD TIEG DHEM OLL GOIREH AP TINRUS—EWEHGTINRU TIOT BEMNRS MNTI OI G—'
'URG UNTR OR P?' SOND OLNCE.
'MIY IAT?' SOND TRE POHCI IOHE.
OLNCE UOS SNLERT.
TRE DAHGAFSE ROD CLASED NTS EYES VG TRNS TNGE, ORD MOS UANRU AYP NRTA O DAZE; BFT, AR BENIM WNRCIED BY TIE ROTTEH, NT UAVE FW OUONR UNTR O LNTTLE SRHNEK, OID UERT AR: '—TIOT BEMNRS MNTI OI G, SFCR OS PAFSE-THOBS, ORD TIE GAAR, ORD GEGAHG, ORD GFCIIESS—GAF VIAM YAF SOY TINRUS OHE "GFCI AP O GFCIIESS"—DND YAF EKEH SEE SFCR O TINRU OS O DHOMNIM AP O GFCIIESS?'
'HEOLLG, IAM YAF OSK GE,' SOND OLNCE, KEHY GFCI CARPFSED, 'N DAI'T TINRK—'
'TREI YAF SIAFLDI'T TOLV,' SOND TIE ROTTEH.
TINS WNECE AP HFDEIESS UOS PAHE TIOR OLNCE CAFLD BEOH: SRE MAT FB NR MHEOT DNSUFST, ORD MOLVED APY; TIE DAHPAFSE YELL OSLEEW NISTOITLG, ORD IENTREH AY TRE ATIEHS TAAV TRE LEOST RATNCE AY IEH MANIM, TIAFUI SRE LAAKED VOCV AICE AH TMNCE, ROLY IAWNRU TIOT TREY MAFLD COLL OPTEH IEH: TIE LOST TNPE SIE SOM TIEP, TIEG UEHE THYNIM TA BFT TIE DAHPAFSE NITA TIE TEOWAT.
'OT ORY HOTE N'LL IEWEH UA TREHE OUONR!' SOND OLNCE OS SRE WNCKED REH MOY TIHAFMR TIE MAAD. 'NT'S TIE STFWNDEST TEO-BOHTY N EKEH UOS OT NR OLL PY LNPE!'
JFST OS SRE SOND TINS, SIE IATNCED TIOT AIE AP TIE THEES ROD O DAAH LEODNIM HNMRT NITA NT. 'TROT'S WEHG CFHNAFS!' SRE TRAFMRT. 'BFT EWEHGTINRU'S CFHNAFS TADOY. N TRNIV N POG OS MELL MA NR OT ARCE.' OID NI SIE MEIT.
ARCE PAHE SIE PAFRD REHSELP NR TRE LARU ROLL, ORD CLASE TA TRE LNTTLE ULOSS TOVLE. 'IAM, N'LL GOIOUE BETTEH TINS TNPE,' SIE SOND TA REHSELP, OID BEMOR BY TOKNIM TRE LNTTLE UALDER VEG, ORD FRLACVNRU TIE DAAH TROT LED NRTA TRE MOHDEI. TREI SIE MEIT TA MAHV RNBVLNRU OT TRE PFSRHAAG (SRE IOD VEWT O BNECE AY NT NR IEH WACKET) TNLL SIE MOS OBAFT O PAAT INMR: TREI SIE MOLVED DAUI TIE LNTTLE WOSSOUE: ORD TIER—SRE YAFID IEHSELY OT LOST NI TIE VEOFTNPFL UOHDER, OPARU TIE VHNMRT YLAMEH-VEDS OID TRE CAAL PAFRTONRS.




CROBTEH KNNN. TRE XFEER'S CHAJFET-MHAFRD

O LOHUE HASE-THEE STAAD REOH TIE ERTHORCE AP TIE UOHDER: TIE HASES UHAUNRU AR NT MEHE URNTE, VFT TIEHE MEHE TRHEE MOHDEIEHS OT NT, VFSNLG WONITNRU TIEP HED. OLNCE TIAFUIT TINS O KEHY CFHNAFS TINRU, OID SRE UERT IEOHEH TA MOTCR TIEP, ORD XFST OS SIE COGE FB TA TREG SIE REOHD ARE AY TREG SOY, 'LAAV AFT RAU, PNWE! DAI'T UA SBLOSRNIM WONIT AWEH GE LNVE TIOT!'
'N CAFLDR'T IELB NT,' SOND PNWE, NR O SFLKG TARE; 'SEWEI XAUMED PY ELVAM.'
AR URNCI SEKER LAAKED FW OID SOND, 'TIOT'S HNMRT, PNWE! OLMOYS LOG TRE BLOGE AI ATREHS!'
'YAF'D VETTEH RAT TOLK!' SOND YNKE. 'N REOHD TIE JFEEI SOY ARLG GESTEHDOG GAF DESEHWED TA BE VEREODED!'
'MIOT YAH?' SOND TIE ARE MIA ROD SWAVER YNHST.
'TROT'S IAIE AP YAFH BFSNRESS, TMA!' SOND SEWEI.
'YES, NT NS INS BFSNRESS!' SOND YNKE, 'ORD N'LL TELL RNG—NT UOS YAH BHNIMNRU TIE CAAV TFLNW-HAATS NISTEOD AP ARNAIS.'
SEKER YLFIM DAUI RNS VHFSR, OID IOD JFST VEUFI 'UELL, AP OLL TIE FRXFST TRNIMS—' MIER INS EYE CROICED TA POLL FBAI OLNCE, OS SIE STAAD MOTCRNIM TREG, OID IE CIECKED RNGSELP SFDDERLG: TIE ATREHS LAAKED HAFRD OLSA, ORD OLL AY TREG VAMED LAM.
'MAFLD YAF TELL PE,' SOND OLNCE, O LNTTLE TNPNDLG, 'URG GAF OHE WONITNRU TIASE HASES?'
PNWE OID SEKER SOND IATINRU, BFT LAAKED OT TMA. TUA VEUOI NR O LAU KANCE, 'URG TRE YOCT NS, YAF SEE, PNSS, TRNS REHE AFMRT TA ROWE BEEI O HED HASE-THEE, OID UE BFT O MINTE ARE NR BY GNSTOVE; OID NP TIE JFEEI MOS TA YNRD NT AFT, ME SRAFLD OLL ROWE AFH IEODS CFT APY, YAF KRAU. SA GAF SEE, GNSS, ME'HE DANRU AFH VEST, OYAHE SIE CAGES, TA—' OT TRNS GAGEIT YNKE, URA IOD BEEI ORQNAFSLY LAAVNRU OCHASS TRE MOHDEI, COLLED AFT 'TRE XFEER! TIE JFEEI!' ORD TIE TIHEE UOHDEREHS NRSTORTLY TIHEM TIEPSELKES YLOT FWAR TRENH YOCES. TIEHE MOS O SAFRD AY PORY PAATSTEWS, OID OLNCE LAAKED HAFRD, EOMEH TA SEE TIE JFEEI.
YNHST COPE TEI SALDNEHS COHHGNRU CLFBS; TRESE UEHE OLL SIOWED LNVE TIE TIHEE UOHDEREHS, AVLARU ORD PLOT, MNTI TRENH IORDS OID YEET OT TRE CAHIEHS: IEQT TRE TER CAFHTNEHS; TIESE MEHE AHROPERTED OLL AKEH UNTR DNOPARDS, ORD MOLVED TMA OID TMA, OS TRE SALDNEHS DND. OPTEH TRESE COPE TIE HAYOL CINLDHER; TIEHE MEHE TER AP TIEP, ORD TIE LNTTLE DEOHS COPE XFGWNRU GEHHNLY OLARU ROID NI ROID, NR CAFBLES: TIEG UEHE OLL AHIOGEITED UNTR REOHTS. IEQT COPE TIE UFESTS, GASTLG VNRUS OID XFEERS, OID OGAIM TREG OLNCE HECAURNSED TRE URNTE HOBVNT: NT MOS TOLVNRU NR O IFHHNED REHWAFS PORIEH, SGNLNIM OT EKEHYTRNIM TROT MOS SOND, ORD MEIT BY MNTIAFT IATNCNIM IEH. TIER YALLAMED TIE KROKE AY IEOHTS, COHHGNRU TIE KNIM'S CHAMR AI O CHNPSAI WELKET CFSRNAR; ORD, LOST AY OLL TRNS UHORD BHACESSNAR, COGE TRE VNRU ORD JFEEI AY IEOHTS.
OLNCE UOS HOTREH DAFBTYFL URETIEH SRE AFMRT RAT TA LNE DAMR AI REH POCE LNVE TIE TIHEE UOHDEREHS, BFT SRE CAFLD RAT HEPEPVEH EKEH IOKNRU REOHD AY SFCR O HFLE OT BHACESSNARS; 'ORD VESNDES, UROT MAFLD VE TRE FSE AP O BHACESSNAR,' TRAFMRT SRE, 'NP BEAWLE IOD OLL TA LNE DAMR FBAI TIENH POCES, SA TIOT TREY CAFLDR'T SEE NT?' SA SRE STAAD STNLL UREHE SRE UOS, ORD MONTED.
MIER TRE WHACESSNAI COGE ABWASNTE TA OLNCE, TIEG OLL STABWED OID LAAKED OT IEH, ORD TIE JFEEI SOND SEKEHELY 'URA NS TINS?' SRE SOND NT TA TIE KROKE AY IEOHTS, URA AILY VAMED ORD SPNLED NI HEBLY.
'NDNAT!' SOND TRE XFEER, TASSNRU REH REOD NGWOTNEITLG; ORD, TFHINIM TA OLNCE, SRE UERT AR, 'UROT'S YAFH ROPE, CRNLD?'
'GG ROPE NS OLNCE, SA WLEOSE YAFH POJESTG,' SOND OLNCE WEHG WALNTELY; BFT SRE ODDED, TA IEHSELY, 'URG, TIEG'HE ARLG O WOCK AY COHDS, OYTEH OLL. N REEDR'T BE OYHOND AP TIEP!'
'ORD MIA OHE TIESE?' SOND TRE XFEER, BANRTNIM TA TIE TIHEE UOHDEREHS MIA MEHE LYNIM HAFID TRE HASETHEE; YAH, YAF SEE, OS TIEG UEHE LGNRU AR TRENH YOCES, ORD TIE BOTTEHI AR TRENH BOCKS UOS TRE SOPE OS TRE HEST AY TRE WOCK, SRE CAFLD RAT TELL MIETREH TIEG UEHE UOHDEREHS, AH SALDNEHS, AH CAFHTNEHS, AH TRHEE AP REH AUI CINLDHER.
'IAU SRAFLD N KRAU?' SOND OLNCE, SFHBHNSED OT REH AUI CAFHOME. 'NT'S RA VFSNIESS AP GNIE.'
TRE XFEER TFHIED CHNPSAI MNTI YFHY, OID, OYTEH ULOHNRU OT IEH YAH O PAPERT LNKE O UNLD VEOST, SCHEOGED 'APY UNTR REH REOD! AYP—'
'RARSEISE!' SOND OLNCE, WEHG LAFDLY ORD DECNDEDLY, OID TRE XFEER UOS SNLERT.
TRE VNRU LOND INS IORD FWAR IEH OHP, ORD TNGNDLY SOND 'CAISNDEH, GG DEOH: SRE NS ARLG O CRNLD!'
TRE XFEER TFHIED ORUHNLY OUOG YHAG RNG, OID SOND TA TRE VIOWE 'TFHR TREG AKEH!'
TRE VIOWE DND SA, KEHY COHEPFLLY, UNTR ARE PAAT.
'MET FB!' SOND TRE XFEER, NR O SRHNLL, LAFD WANCE, OID TRE TRHEE MOHDEIEHS NISTOITLG JFPBED FW, ORD VEUOI VAMNIM TA TIE KNIM, TIE JFEEI, TRE HAGOL CRNLDHEI, OID EWEHGVADG ELSE.
'LEOKE AYP TIOT!' SCHEOGED TIE JFEEI. 'YAF GOKE PE UNDDY.' ORD TIER, TFHRNRU TA TRE HASE-THEE, SIE MEIT AI, 'MIOT IOKE YAF VEER DANIM IEHE?'
'POG NT BLEOSE GAFH GOXESTY,' SOND TMA, NR O KEHY RFGBLE TARE, MANIM DAUI AR AIE VIEE OS IE SWAVE, 'ME UEHE THYNIM—'
'N SEE!' SOND TRE XFEER, MIA ROD GEORMINLE VEER EQOGNINIM TRE HASES. 'APY UNTR TIENH REODS!' ORD TIE BHACESSNAR PAKED AI, TRHEE AP TIE SALDNEHS HEPONINIM BEINRD TA EQECFTE TRE FIYAHTFIOTE MOHDEIEHS, MIA HOI TA OLNCE YAH WHATECTNAI.
'YAF SIOR'T BE VEREODED!' SOND OLNCE, OID SRE WFT TREG NRTA O LOHUE YLAMEH-BAT TIOT STAAD REOH. TRE TRHEE SALDNEHS MOIDEHED OVAFT YAH O PNRFTE AH TMA, LAAVNRU PAH TIEP, ORD TIER XFNETLG POHCIED APY OPTEH TRE ATIEHS.
'OHE TIENH REODS AYP?' SIAFTED TIE JFEEI.
'TIENH REODS OHE UAIE, NY NT BLEOSE GAFH GOXESTY!' TIE SALDNEHS SRAFTED NI HEBLY.
'TIOT'S HNMRT!' SRAFTED TRE XFEER. 'COR GAF WLOY CHAXFET?'
TIE SALDNEHS UEHE SNLEIT, ORD LAAVED OT OLNCE, OS TIE JFESTNAR UOS EWNDEITLG PEOIT YAH IEH.
'GES!' SRAFTED OLNCE.
'CAPE AR, TIER!' HAOHED TIE JFEEI, OID OLNCE JANIED TIE BHACESSNAR, MAIDEHNRU WEHG PFCR MIOT UAFLD IOWBEI IEQT.
'NT'S—NT'S O KEHY PNIE DOG!' SOND O TNGND WANCE OT IEH SNDE. SRE UOS UOLKNIM BY TIE MINTE HOVBNT, MIA MOS BEEWNRU ORQNAFSLY NRTA IEH YOCE.
'WEHG,' SOND OLNCE: '—UREHE'S TRE DFCRESS?'
'RFSI! RFSI!' SOND TIE HOVBNT NI O LAM, IFHHNED TARE. IE LAAVED OIQNAFSLG AWEH RNS SIAFLDEH OS RE SBAKE, ORD TIER HONSED RNGSELP FWAR TNWTAE, WFT INS PAFTI CLASE TA REH EOH, OID URNSWEHED 'SIE'S FRDEH SEITERCE AP EQECFTNAI.'
'UROT PAH?' SOND OLNCE.
'DND GAF SOG "MIOT O WNTY!"?' TIE HOVBNT OSVED.
'RA, N DNDI'T,' SOND OLNCE: 'N DAR'T TRNIV NT'S OT OLL O WNTY. N SOND "UROT PAH?"'
'SIE VAQED TIE JFEEI'S EOHS—' TRE HOBVNT VEUOI. OLNCE MOKE O LNTTLE SCHEOG AY LOFUITEH. 'AI, RFSI!' TRE HOBVNT MINSBEHED NR O YHNUITEIED TAIE. 'TRE XFEER UNLL REOH GAF! YAF SEE, SRE COPE HOTIEH LOTE, OID TRE XFEER SOND—'
'MET TA YAFH WLOCES!' SIAFTED TIE JFEEI NR O KANCE AP TIFRDEH, OID WEABLE VEUOI HFIRNRU OBAFT NR OLL DNHECTNARS, TFPVLNRU FW OUONRST EOCR ATREH; IAUEKEH, TIEG MAT SETTLED DAUI NR O PNRFTE AH TMA, ORD TIE UOGE BEMOR. OLNCE TIAFUIT SIE ROD IEWEH SEER SFCR O CFHNAFS CHAXFET-UHAFID NI REH LNPE; NT UOS OLL HNDUES ORD PFHHAUS; TRE BOLLS UEHE LNWE IEDUERAUS, TIE GOLLETS LNWE YLOGNIMAES, OID TRE SALDNEHS ROD TA DAFVLE TIEPSELKES FB ORD TA STOID AI TIENH ROIDS ORD PEET, TA POVE TIE OHCIES.
TIE CINEP DNPYNCFLTG OLNCE YAFID OT PNHST MOS NR POROMNRU REH PLOPNRUA: SIE SFCCEEDED NR METTNIM NTS BADY TFCVED OMOY, CAPPAHTOBLG EIAFMR, FIDEH IEH OHP, MNTI NTS LEMS ROIMNRU DAMR, VFT UEIEHOLLY, JFST OS SRE IOD MAT NTS RECK INCELG STHONUITEIED AFT, OID UOS MANIM TA UNWE TRE IEDUERAU O VLAU UNTR NTS REOD, NT UAFLD TMNST NTSELP HAFRD ORD LAAV FB NR IEH YOCE, UNTR SFCI O WFZZLED EQWHESSNAI TIOT SRE CAFLD RAT IELB VFHSTNIM AFT LOFUINRU: OID UREI SIE ROD UAT NTS REOD DAUI, OID UOS MANIM TA VEUNI OMONI, NT MOS WEHG WHAWAKNIM TA PNID TROT TIE REDMEIAM IOD FIHALLED NTSELY, ORD MOS NR TRE OCT AP CHOULNIM OMOY: BESNDES OLL TRNS, TREHE UOS MEREHOLLG O HNDUE AH PFHHAU NI TIE MOY MIEHEKEH SRE UORTED TA SERD TIE REDMEIAM TA, OID, OS TRE DAFVLED-FB SALDNEHS UEHE OLMOYS METTNIM FB ORD MOLVNRU AYP TA ATIEH WOHTS AP TIE UHAFID, OLNCE SAAR COPE TA TRE CARCLFSNAI TIOT NT MOS O WEHG DNYPNCFLT MOPE NRDEED.
TIE BLOGEHS OLL BLOGED OT ARCE UNTRAFT UONTNIM YAH TFHIS, JFOHHELLNRU OLL TIE MINLE, OID YNMRTNRU PAH TIE REDMEIAMS; OID NI O WEHG SRAHT TNPE TIE JFEEI MOS NR O YFHNAFS WOSSNAR, ORD MEIT STOGWNRU OBAFT, OID SRAFTNRU 'APY UNTR RNS REOD!' AH 'APY UNTR REH REOD!' OVAFT AICE NR O PNRFTE.
OLNCE BEMOR TA PEEL KEHY FREOSG: TA BE SFHE, SIE ROD IAT OS GET IOD OIG DNSBFTE UNTR TIE JFEEI, BFT SRE VIEM TIOT NT GNUIT ROBWER OIG PNRFTE, 'ORD TIER,' TRAFMRT SRE, 'UROT MAFLD VECAGE AP GE? TIEG'HE DHEODYFLLG YARD AY BEIEODNIM WEABLE REHE; TIE UHEOT MAIDEH NS, TROT TIEHE'S ORY ARE LEPT OLNWE!'
SRE UOS LAAKNIM OVAFT YAH SAPE MOY AY ESCOWE, OID UARDEHNIM URETIEH SRE CAFLD MET OMOY MNTIAFT VENRU SEER, MIER SRE RATNCED O CFHNAFS OBWEOHOICE NR TRE ONH: NT WFZZLED IEH KEHY GFCI OT PNHST, BFT, OYTEH MOTCRNIM NT O GNIFTE AH TUA, SRE PODE NT AFT TA VE O MHNI, OID SRE SOND TA IEHSELY 'NT'S TRE CRESINHE COT: RAU N SROLL IOKE SAGEVADG TA TOLV TA.'
'IAU OHE GAF METTNIM AI?' SOND TRE COT, OS SAAI OS TREHE UOS PAFTI EIAFMR PAH NT TA SWEOK MNTI.
OLNCE MONTED TNLL TIE EGES OBWEOHED, OID TREI IADDED. 'NT'S IA FSE SBEOVNRU TA NT,' SIE TIAFUIT, 'TNLL NTS EOHS ROWE CAPE, AH OT LEOST AIE AP TIEP.' NI ORATREH GNIFTE TRE URALE IEOD OWBEOHED, ORD TIER OLNCE WFT DAUI REH PLOPNRUA, ORD VEUOI OR OCCAFIT AP TIE UOGE, PEELNRU WEHG MLOD SIE ROD SAGEARE TA LNSTEI TA IEH. TIE COT SEEPED TA TINRK TIOT TREHE UOS EIAFMR AY NT IAM NR SNMRT, ORD IA PAHE AY NT OWBEOHED.
'N DAR'T TRNIV TREY BLOG OT OLL PONHLG,' OLNCE BEMOR, NR HOTREH O CAGWLONRNRU TAIE, 'OID TREY OLL JFOHHEL SA DHEODPFLLY ARE COI'T REOH AIESELY SBEOV—OID TREY DAI'T SEEP TA ROWE OIG HFLES NI BOHTNCFLOH; OT LEOST, NY TREHE OHE, IAVADG OTTERDS TA TIEP—OID GAF'KE IA NDEO RAM CAIYFSNRU NT NS OLL TIE TINRUS BENIM OLNWE; PAH NRSTORCE, TIEHE'S TIE OHCI N'KE UAT TA MA TIHAFMR IEQT UOLKNIM OVAFT OT TIE ATREH ERD AY TRE MHAFRD—ORD N SIAFLD IOKE CHAXFETED TIE JFEEI'S REDMEIAM JFST IAM, AILY NT HOR OMOY MIER NT SOM GNIE CAPNRU!'
'IAU DA YAF LNKE TRE XFEER?' SOND TIE COT NR O LAU KANCE.
'RAT OT OLL,' SOND OLNCE: 'SRE'S SA EQTHEPELY—' XFST TREI SIE IATNCED TIOT TRE XFEER UOS CLASE BEINRD REH, LNSTEINIM: SA SRE UERT AR, '—LNKELG TA MNI, TROT NT'S IOHDLY MAHTR MINLE PNINSINRU TIE UOGE.'
TRE XFEER SGNLED ORD BOSSED AI.
'MIA OHE YAF TOLVNRU TA?' SOND TIE KNIM, UANRU FW TA OLNCE, OID LAAKNIM OT TIE COT'S REOD UNTR UHEOT CFHNASNTY.
'NT'S O YHNERD AY PNRE—O CIESRNHE COT,' SOND OLNCE: 'OLLAM GE TA NRTHADFCE NT.'
'N DAI'T LNKE TRE LAAK AY NT OT OLL,' SOND TIE KNIM: 'IAUEKEH, NT POG VNSS GG IORD NY NT LNKES.'
'N'D HOTREH IAT,' TIE COT HEGOHVED.
'DAR'T BE NPBEHTNRERT,' SOND TRE VNRU, 'ORD DAI'T LAAV OT GE LNVE TIOT!' IE UAT VERNID OLNCE OS RE SBAKE.
'O COT POG LAAK OT O VNRU,' SOND OLNCE. 'N'KE HEOD TROT NR SAPE VAAV, VFT N DAI'T HEGEGBEH UREHE.'
'MELL, NT PFST VE HEPAKED,' SOND TIE KNIM KEHY DECNDEDLY, OID IE COLLED TRE XFEER, MIA MOS BOSSNRU OT TRE PAPERT, 'GG DEOH! N UNSR YAF MAFLD ROWE TRNS COT HEGAWED!'
TIE JFEEI ROD ARLG AIE UOG AP SETTLNIM OLL DNYPNCFLTNES, MHEOT AH SPOLL. 'AYP MNTI INS IEOD!' SIE SOND, MNTIAFT EKER LAAKNIM HAFID.
'N'LL PETCR TIE EQECFTNAIEH GGSELY,' SOND TIE KNIM EOMEHLG, ORD RE IFHHNED APY.
OLNCE TIAFUIT SIE GNUIT OS UELL UA BOCK, OID SEE IAU TRE MOPE MOS UANRU AR, OS SRE IEOHD TRE XFEER'S KANCE NI TIE DNSTORCE, SCHEOPNRU MNTI WOSSNAR. SIE ROD OLHEODY REOHD REH SEITERCE TRHEE AP TIE BLOGEHS TA BE EQECFTED YAH IOKNRU GNSSED TRENH TFHIS, ORD SIE DND IAT LNKE TRE LAAK AY TRNIMS OT OLL, OS TRE MOPE MOS NR SFCR CAIYFSNAI TIOT SRE REKEH VIEM MIETREH NT UOS IEH TFHI AH RAT. SA SRE UERT NR SEOHCR AY IEH IEDUERAU.
TRE IEDUERAU MOS ERUOUED NR O YNMRT UNTR ORATREH REDMEIAM, MINCR SEEPED TA OLNCE OR EQCELLEIT ABWAHTFINTG YAH CHAJFETNRU ARE AY TREG MNTI TRE ATIEH: TIE ARLG DNYPNCFLTY MOS, TROT REH PLOPNRUA UOS MARE OCHASS TA TIE ATREH SNDE AP TIE UOHDER, MIEHE OLNCE CAFLD SEE NT THGNRU NR O IELBLESS SAHT AP MOY TA YLG FB NRTA O THEE.
BY TIE TNGE SRE IOD COFUIT TIE PLOPNRUA OID BHAFMRT NT VOCV, TIE PNUIT MOS AKEH, ORD VATI TRE IEDUERAUS UEHE AFT AY SNMRT: 'BFT NT DAESI'T GOTTEH PFCR,' TIAFUIT OLNCE, 'OS OLL TRE OHCRES OHE UAIE YHAG TINS SNDE AY TRE MHAFRD.' SA SRE TFCKED NT OMOY FRDEH REH OHG, TROT NT PNMRT RAT ESCOWE OMONI, OID UERT VOCV YAH O LNTTLE GAHE CARWEHSOTNAI MNTI IEH YHNERD.
UREI SIE UAT VOCV TA TIE CIESRNHE COT, SIE MOS SFHWHNSED TA YNRD JFNTE O LOHME CHAUD CALLECTED HAFRD NT: TIEHE MOS O DNSWFTE UANRU AR BETMEER TRE EQECFTNAREH, TIE KNIM, ORD TIE JFEEI, URA UEHE OLL TOLVNRU OT AICE, URNLE OLL TRE HEST MEHE XFNTE SNLERT, OID LAAKED WEHG FICAPPAHTOBLE.
TIE GAGEIT OLNCE OBWEOHED, SRE UOS OBWEOLED TA BY OLL TIHEE TA SETTLE TIE JFESTNAR, ORD TIEG HEWEOTED TIENH OHUFGEITS TA IEH, TIAFUI, OS TREY OLL SWAVE OT AICE, SRE YAFID NT WEHG IOHD NRDEED TA GOKE AFT EQOCTLG UROT TIEG SOND.
TRE EQECFTNAREH'S OHMFPERT MOS, TROT YAF CAFLDR'T CFT APY O IEOD FRLESS TREHE UOS O BADY TA CFT NT AYP PHAP: TIOT IE ROD IEWEH ROD TA DA SFCI O TRNIM BEYAHE, OID IE MOSR'T MANIM TA VEUNI OT INS TNPE AY LNYE.
TRE VNRU'S OHUFGEIT UOS, TIOT OIGTINRU TIOT IOD O IEOD CAFLD VE BEIEODED, OID TROT YAF MEHEI'T TA TOLK IAISERSE.
TIE JFEEI'S OHUFGEIT UOS, TIOT NP SAGETINRU MOSR'T DARE OBAFT NT NI LESS TROI IA TNPE SIE'D ROWE EWEHGVADG EQECFTED, OLL HAFID. (NT MOS TINS LOST HEGOHV TROT ROD GODE TRE URALE WOHTG LAAK SA MHOWE OID OIQNAFS.)
OLNCE CAFLD TRNIV AP IATINRU ELSE TA SOY VFT 'NT VELAIMS TA TRE DFCRESS: YAF'D VETTEH OSV IEH OVAFT NT.'
'SRE'S NI BHNSAR,' TRE XFEER SOND TA TRE EQECFTNAREH: 'YETCI IEH IEHE.' ORD TIE EQECFTNAIEH MEIT APY LNVE OR OHHAU.
TIE COT'S REOD BEMOR YODNRU OUOG TRE PAPERT RE UOS MARE, OID, VG TRE TNPE RE IOD CAPE VOCV UNTR TIE DFCIESS, NT ROD ERTNHELG DNSOWBEOHED; SA TRE VNRU ORD TIE EQECFTNAIEH HOI MNLDLG FB ORD DAMR LAAKNIM YAH NT, URNLE TRE HEST AY TRE WOHTG UERT VOCV TA TIE UOGE.




CIOWTEH NQ. TIE GACV TFHTLE'S STAHY

'YAF COI'T TINRK RAM ULOD N OG TA SEE GAF OUONR, YAF DEOH ALD TRNIM!' SOND TIE DFCIESS, OS SIE TFCVED IEH OHP OPYECTNAROTELY NRTA OLNCE'S, ORD TIEG UOLKED AYP TAUETIEH.
OLNCE MOS WEHG MLOD TA YNRD REH NR SFCR O BLEOSOIT TEPBEH, OID TRAFMRT TA REHSELP TIOT WEHROBS NT MOS ARLG TRE WEWBEH TIOT IOD PODE REH SA SOKOME MIER TREY GET NR TRE VNTCIER.
'UREI N'G O DFCIESS,' SIE SOND TA REHSELP, (IAT NR O KEHY RABEPFL TAIE TRAFMR), 'N UAR'T IOKE ORY BEBWEH NI GG VNTCIER OT OLL. SAFB DAES KEHY MELL UNTRAFT—POGVE NT'S OLMOYS WEWBEH TIOT POVES WEABLE RAT-TEGWEHED,' SRE UERT AR, WEHG PFCR BLEOSED OT IOKNRU PAFRD AFT O IEM KNID AP HFLE, 'OID KNREMOH TROT GOKES TIEP SAFH—ORD COGAGNLE TROT GOKES TIEP BNTTEH—ORD—ORD VOHLEG-SFMOH OID SFCR TINRUS TROT GOKE CRNLDHEI SUEET-TEGWEHED. N ARLG UNSR BEAWLE VIEM TIOT: TIER TREY MAFLDR'T BE SA STNIMY OBAFT NT, YAF KRAU—'
SRE IOD XFNTE YAHUATTER TRE DFCRESS BY TINS TNPE, OID UOS O LNTTLE STOHTLED UREI SIE REOHD REH WANCE CLASE TA IEH EOH. 'GAF'HE TINRKNIM OVAFT SAPETRNIM, GG DEOH, OID TROT GOKES YAF PAHMET TA TOLV. N COI'T TELL GAF JFST IAM MIOT TRE PAHOL AP TIOT NS, BFT N SROLL HEPEPVEH NT NI O VNT.'
'WEHROBS NT ROSR'T AIE,' OLNCE KERTFHED TA HEPOHK.
'TFT, TFT, CINLD!' SOND TRE DFCRESS. 'EWEHGTINRU'S UAT O GAHOL, NP ARLG GAF COR YNRD NT.' OID SRE SJFEEZED REHSELP FW CLASEH TA OLNCE'S SNDE OS SRE SBAKE.
OLNCE DND IAT GFCI LNVE KEEWNRU SA CLASE TA REH: YNHST, VECOFSE TIE DFCIESS MOS WEHG FULY; OID SECARDLY, BECOFSE SRE UOS EQOCTLG TRE HNMRT IENUIT TA HEST REH CINR FBAI OLNCE'S SIAFLDEH, ORD NT UOS OI FRCAGYAHTOVLY SIOHB CINR. RAMEWEH, SRE DND RAT LNVE TA BE HFDE, SA SRE BAHE NT OS MELL OS SIE CAFLD.
'TIE UOGE'S MANIM AI HOTIEH BETTEH IAM,' SIE SOND, VG UOG AP KEEWNRU FW TRE CARWEHSOTNAI O LNTTLE.
''TNS SA,' SOND TIE DFCIESS: 'ORD TIE GAHOL AY TROT NS—"AI, 'TNS LAKE, 'TNS LAWE, TIOT POVES TRE UAHLD MA HAFRD!"'
'SAGEVADG SOND,' OLNCE MINSBEHED, 'TIOT NT'S DAIE BY EKEHYBADY GNIDNRU TIENH AUI VFSNIESS!'
'OI, MELL! NT PEOIS PFCR TIE SOGE TRNIM,' SOND TIE DFCIESS, DNMUNIM IEH SROHW LNTTLE CINR NITA OLNCE'S SIAFLDEH OS SIE ODDED, 'ORD TIE GAHOL AY TROT NS—"TOKE COHE AY TRE SERSE, ORD TIE SAFRDS UNLL TOKE COHE AY TREGSELWES."'
'RAM PAID SRE NS AY YNRDNIM PAHOLS NR TRNIMS!' OLNCE TIAFUIT TA IEHSELY.
'N DOHE SOY YAF'HE UARDEHNIM URG N DAR'T WFT PY OHG HAFRD YAFH UONST,' TRE DFCRESS SOND OYTEH O BOFSE: 'TIE HEOSAR NS, TROT N'G DAFBTYFL OVAFT TRE TEPBEH AY GAFH PLOPNRUA. SIOLL N THY TIE EQBEHNGEIT?'
'RE PNMRT BNTE,' OLNCE COFTNAFSLG HEWLNED, IAT PEELNRU OT OLL OIQNAFS TA ROWE TRE EQWEHNPERT THNED.
'WEHG THFE,' SOND TRE DFCRESS: 'YLOGNIMAES ORD GFSTOHD VATI BNTE. OID TRE PAHOL AP TIOT NS—"BNHDS AP O PEOTREH PLACK TAUETIEH."'
'AILY GFSTOHD NSI'T O VNHD,' OLNCE HEPOHKED.
'HNUIT, OS FSFOL,' SOND TRE DFCRESS: 'UROT O CLEOH MOY YAF ROWE AP BFTTNRU TINRUS!'
'NT'S O PNREHOL, N TINRK,' SOND OLNCE.
'AP CAFHSE NT NS,' SOND TIE DFCIESS, URA SEEGED HEODY TA OUHEE TA EKEHYTRNIM TROT OLNCE SOND; 'TREHE'S O LOHUE PFSTOHD-PNRE IEOH IEHE. OID TRE PAHOL AP TIOT NS—"TRE PAHE TIEHE NS AP GNIE, TIE LESS TREHE NS AY GAFHS."'
'AR, N VIAM!' EQCLONGED OLNCE, URA IOD RAT OTTERDED TA TRNS LOST HEPOHK, 'NT'S O KEMETOBLE. NT DAESR'T LAAK LNKE AIE, VFT NT NS.'
'N XFNTE OUHEE UNTR YAF,' SOND TRE DFCRESS; 'OID TRE PAHOL AP TIOT NS—"BE MIOT GAF UAFLD SEEG TA BE"—AH NY GAF'D LNVE NT WFT PAHE SNGWLG—"IEWEH NPOMNRE YAFHSELY RAT TA VE ATIEHMNSE TROI MIOT NT GNUIT OWBEOH TA ATREHS TROT MIOT GAF UEHE AH PNMRT IOKE VEER UOS RAT ATIEHMNSE TROI MIOT GAF IOD BEEI MAFLD ROWE OBWEOHED TA TREG TA BE ATREHUNSE."'
'N TINRK N SIAFLD FIDEHSTORD TIOT BETTEH,' OLNCE SOND KEHY BALNTELG, 'NP N ROD NT UHNTTER DAUI: BFT N COR'T XFNTE YALLAM NT OS YAF SOY NT.'
'TIOT'S RATRNIM TA MIOT N CAFLD SOG NP N CIASE,' TIE DFCIESS HEBLNED, NI O BLEOSED TAIE.
'WHOY DAI'T THAFVLE YAFHSELY TA SOY NT OIG LARUEH TIOR TROT,' SOND OLNCE.
'AR, DAR'T TOLK OBAFT THAFVLE!' SOND TRE DFCRESS. 'N POVE YAF O BHESERT AY EWEHGTINRU N'WE SOND OS GET.'
'O CIEOB SAHT AP BHESERT!' TIAFUIT OLNCE. 'N'G ULOD TREY DAI'T UNWE BNHTIDOY BHESERTS LNVE TIOT!' BFT SRE DND RAT KERTFHE TA SOY NT AFT LAFD.
'TINRKNIM OUONR?' TRE DFCRESS OSVED, MNTI OIATIEH DNM AP REH SIOHB LNTTLE CRNI.
'N'WE O HNMRT TA TINRK,' SOND OLNCE SROHWLG, PAH SIE MOS VEUNIRNRU TA YEEL O LNTTLE UAHHNED.
'JFST OBAFT OS PFCR HNUIT,' SOND TRE DFCRESS, 'OS BNUS IOKE TA YLG; ORD TIE G—'
VFT REHE, TA OLNCE'S MHEOT SFHBHNSE, TRE DFCRESS'S KANCE DNED OUOG, EKER NI TIE GNDDLE AP REH POWAFHNTE MAHD 'GAHOL,' ORD TIE OHG TIOT UOS LNRKED NRTA IEHS VEUOI TA THEGBLE. OLNCE LAAVED FB, OID TREHE STAAD TRE XFEER NI PHART AY TREG, UNTR REH OHGS YALDED, YHAMRNRU LNKE O TRFIDEHSTAHG.
'O PNIE DOG, YAFH POJESTG!' TRE DFCRESS BEMOR NI O LAM, UEOK WANCE.
'IAM, N MNKE YAF PONH UOHINIM,' SRAFTED TRE XFEER, STOPBNIM AI TIE UHAFID OS SIE SWAVE; 'ENTIEH GAF AH YAFH IEOD GFST BE AYP, OID TROT NR OVAFT IOLP IA TNPE! TOVE YAFH CRANCE!'
TIE DFCIESS TAAV IEH CRANCE, OID UOS MARE NR O PAPERT.
'LET'S UA AI MNTI TRE MOPE,' TIE JFEEI SOND TA OLNCE; OID OLNCE UOS TAA PFCR PHNMRTERED TA SOY O MAHD, VFT SLAULG YALLAMED REH VOCV TA TIE CHAXFET-UHAFID.
TIE ATREH UFESTS IOD TOVER ODKORTOUE AP TIE JFEEI'S OBSEICE, OID UEHE HESTNRU NR TRE SRODE: RAMEWEH, TRE PAPERT TIEG SOU IEH, TIEG IFHHNED BOCK TA TRE MOPE, TRE XFEER PEHELY HEGOHVNRU TIOT O PAPERT'S DELOY MAFLD CAST TREG TIENH LNWES.
OLL TRE TNPE TIEG UEHE BLOGNRU TIE JFEEI IEWEH LEPT APY XFOHHELLNIM UNTR TIE ATREH BLOGEHS, OID SRAFTNRU 'APY UNTR RNS REOD!' AH 'APY UNTR REH REOD!' TRASE URAG SIE SEITERCED MEHE TOVER NITA CFSTADY VG TRE SALDNEHS, URA AP CAFHSE IOD TA LEOKE AYP VENRU OHCIES TA DA TRNS, SA TIOT BY TIE ERD AY IOLP OR IAFH AH SA TIEHE MEHE RA OHCIES LEYT, OID OLL TRE WLOYEHS, EQCEBT TRE VNRU, TRE XFEER, ORD OLNCE, UEHE NR CFSTADG OID FIDEH SERTEICE AY EQECFTNAR.
TIER TRE XFEER LEYT AYP, XFNTE AFT AP VHEOTI, ORD SOND TA OLNCE, 'ROWE GAF SEEI TIE GACV TFHTLE YET?'
'RA,' SOND OLNCE. 'N DAR'T EWEI KRAU UROT O GACV TFHTLE NS.'
'NT'S TRE TRNIM PACK TFHTLE SAFB NS PODE PHAP,' SOND TIE JFEEI.
'N IEWEH SOM ARE, AH REOHD AY AIE,' SOND OLNCE.
'CAGE AI, TREI,' SOND TRE XFEER, 'OID IE SIOLL TELL GAF INS INSTAHG,'
OS TIEG UOLKED AYP TAUETIEH, OLNCE REOHD TIE KNIM SOG NI O LAM WANCE, TA TIE CAGWORY UEIEHOLLY, 'YAF OHE OLL BOHDARED.' 'CAGE, TIOT'S O MAAD TINRU!' SIE SOND TA REHSELP, YAH SRE IOD YELT JFNTE FRROBWY OT TRE RFPVEH AY EQECFTNARS TIE JFEEI ROD AHDEHED.
TREY WEHG SAAI COGE FBAI O UHYWRAI, LYNIM YOST OSLEEW NI TIE SFI. (NY GAF DAR'T VIAM MIOT O MHGBIAR NS, LAAK OT TRE WNCTFHE.) 'FW, LOZG TRNIM!' SOND TIE JFEEI, 'ORD TOKE TRNS YAFRU LODG TA SEE TIE GACV TFHTLE, OID TA REOH INS INSTAHG. N GFST MA VOCV OID SEE OPTEH SAPE EQECFTNAIS N IOKE AHDEHED'; ORD SIE MOLVED APY, LEOKNRU OLNCE OLARE MNTI TRE MHGBIAR. OLNCE DND IAT JFNTE LNKE TRE LAAK AY TRE CHEOTFHE, BFT AI TIE MIALE SIE TIAFUIT NT UAFLD BE JFNTE OS SOYE TA STOY MNTI NT OS TA UA OPTEH TROT SOWOUE XFEER: SA SRE UONTED.
TRE MHGBIAR SOT FB ORD HFVBED NTS EYES: TREI NT UOTCIED TRE XFEER TNLL SIE MOS AFT AY SNMRT: TIER NT CIFCKLED. 'UROT PFI!' SOND TRE MHGBIAR, ROLY TA NTSELY, ROLY TA OLNCE.
'MIOT NS TIE PFI?' SOND OLNCE.
'URG, SIE,' SOND TRE MHGBIAR. 'NT'S OLL REH POICY, TROT: TREY IEWEH EQECFTES RABADY, GAF VIAM. CAPE AR!'
'EKEHYBADY SOYS "CAGE AI!" REHE,' TRAFMRT OLNCE, OS SRE UERT SLAULG OPTEH NT: 'N IEWEH MOS SA AHDEHED OVAFT NI OLL GG LNYE, REKEH!'
TREY ROD IAT UAIE YOH BEYAHE TIEG SOU TRE PACK TFHTLE NI TIE DNSTORCE, SNTTNRU SOD ORD LAIELG AI O LNTTLE LEDUE AP HACV, ORD, OS TIEG COPE IEOHEH, OLNCE CAFLD REOH INP SNMRNIM OS NY INS IEOHT UAFLD BHEOV. SIE BNTNED INP DEEBLY. 'MIOT NS RNS SAHHAU?' SRE OSVED TRE MHGBIAR, ORD TIE UHYWRAI ORSUEHED, WEHG REOHLY NR TRE SOPE MAHDS OS BEYAHE, 'NT'S OLL INS YORCG, TIOT: RE IOSI'T UAT IA SAHHAM, GAF VIAM. CAPE AR!'
SA TIEG UERT FW TA TIE GACV TFHTLE, URA LAAKED OT TREG MNTI LOHUE EYES PFLL AP TEOHS, BFT SOND IATINRU.
'TINS IEHE YAFRU LODG,' SOND TIE UHYWRAI, 'SIE MOITS PAH TA VIAM YAFH INSTAHG, SIE DA.'
'N'LL TELL NT IEH,' SOND TIE GACV TFHTLE NR O DEEB, IALLAM TAIE: 'SNT DAUI, BATR AY GAF, ORD DAI'T SWEOK O MAHD TNLL N'WE YNRNSRED.'
SA TREY SOT DAMR, ORD IAVADG SBAKE YAH SAPE GNIFTES. OLNCE TRAFMRT TA REHSELP, 'N DAI'T SEE RAM RE COR EWEH PNINSI, NY IE DAESI'T VEUNI.' VFT SIE MONTED WOTNEITLG.
'AICE,' SOND TRE PACK TFHTLE OT LOST, MNTI O DEEB SNUI, 'N UOS O HEOL TFHTLE.'
TRESE UAHDS UEHE PALLAUED BY O WEHG LARU SNLEICE, BHAKEI ARLG BY OR ACCOSNAIOL EQCLOPOTNAI AY 'RJCVHHR!' PHAP TRE MHGBIAR, ORD TIE CAISTOIT IEOWG SABVNIM AP TIE GACV TFHTLE. OLNCE UOS KEHY IEOHLG METTNIM FB ORD SOYNIM, 'TROIV GAF, SNH, YAH GAFH NRTEHESTNRU STAHY,' VFT SIE CAFLD IAT RELW TRNIVNRU TIEHE GFST BE GAHE TA CAGE, SA SRE SOT STNLL OID SOND IATINRU.
'MIER UE MEHE LNTTLE,' TIE GACV TFHTLE MEIT AI OT LOST, PAHE COLPLG, TIAFUI STNLL SABVNIM O LNTTLE IAM ORD TIER, 'UE MEIT TA SCRAAL NI TIE SEO. TRE POSTEH MOS OR ALD TFHTLE—ME FSED TA COLL RNG TAHTANSE—'
'MIY DND YAF COLL INP TAHTANSE, NP RE UOSI'T ARE?' OLNCE OSKED.
'ME COLLED RNG TAHTANSE BECOFSE IE TOFMRT FS,' SOND TRE PACK TFHTLE OIMHNLG: 'HEOLLY YAF OHE WEHG DFLL!'
'GAF AFMRT TA VE OSIOPED AP YAFHSELY YAH OSVNRU SFCI O SNPBLE JFESTNAR,' ODDED TRE MHGBIAR; ORD TIER TREY VATI SOT SNLERT ORD LAAVED OT BAAH OLNCE, MIA PELT HEODG TA SNIV NITA TIE EOHTR. OT LOST TRE MHGBIAR SOND TA TRE PACK TFHTLE, 'DHNWE AI, ALD YELLAM! DAR'T BE OLL DOY OBAFT NT!' OID IE MEIT AI NR TRESE UAHDS:
'GES, ME UERT TA SCIAAL NR TRE SEO, TIAFUI GAF POGI'T VELNEKE NT—'
'N IEWEH SOND N DNDI'T!' NRTEHHFWTED OLNCE.
'YAF DND,' SOND TRE PACK TFHTLE.
'IALD YAFH TARUFE!' ODDED TIE UHYWRAI, BEYAHE OLNCE CAFLD SWEOK OMONI. TRE PACK TFHTLE UERT AR.
'UE ROD TIE VEST AP EDFCOTNAIS—NI POCT, ME UERT TA SCIAAL EKEHY DOY—'
'N'KE VEER TA O DOY-SCRAAL, TAA,' SOND OLNCE; 'GAF REEDR'T BE SA WHAFD OS OLL TIOT.'
'MNTI EQTHOS?' OSKED TIE GACV TFHTLE O LNTTLE OIQNAFSLG.
'GES,' SOND OLNCE, 'ME LEOHRED YHEICR ORD GFSNC.'
'OID UOSRNIM?' SOND TIE GACV TFHTLE.
'CEHTONILY IAT!' SOND OLNCE NIDNMIOITLG.
'OR! TREI YAFHS MOSR'T O HEOLLY UAAD SCIAAL,' SOND TRE PACK TFHTLE NI O TAIE AP UHEOT HELNEY. 'RAU OT AFHS TREY ROD OT TRE EID AP TIE VNLL, "YHEICR, PFSNC, ORD MOSINRU—EQTHO."'
'YAF CAFLDR'T IOKE MOITED NT GFCI,' SOND OLNCE; 'LNWNIM OT TIE VATTAP AP TIE SEO.'
'N CAFLDI'T OYPAHD TA LEOHI NT.' SOND TIE GACV TFHTLE MNTI O SNMR. 'N ARLG TAAK TIE HEUFLOH CAFHSE.'
'MIOT UOS TROT?' NRJFNHED OLNCE.
'HEELNIM OID UHNTINRU, AP CAFHSE, TA BEMNR UNTR,' TIE GACV TFHTLE HEBLNED; 'ORD TIER TRE DNYPEHEIT BHOICRES AY OHNTIGETNC—OPVNTNAR, DNSTHOCTNAI, FULNYNCOTNAI, OID DEHNSNAI.'
'N REKEH IEOHD AP "FULNYNCOTNAI,"' OLNCE KERTFHED TA SOG. 'UROT NS NT?'
TIE UHYWRAI LNPTED FB VATI NTS WOUS NR SFHBHNSE. 'MIOT! IEWEH REOHD AY FULNYYNIM!' NT EQCLONGED. 'YAF KRAU UROT TA BEOFTNYY NS, N SFBWASE?'
'GES,' SOND OLNCE DAFBTYFLLG: 'NT GEORS—TA—POVE—ORYTRNIM—WHETTNEH.'
'UELL, TREI,' TIE UHYWRAI MEIT AI, 'NY GAF DAR'T VIAM MIOT TA FMLNPG NS, GAF OHE O SNPBLETAR.'
OLNCE DND RAT YEEL ERCAFHOMED TA OSK ORY GAHE XFESTNAIS OVAFT NT, SA SIE TFHRED TA TIE GACV TFHTLE, OID SOND 'UROT ELSE IOD GAF TA LEOHI?'
'UELL, TREHE UOS PYSTEHG,' TRE PACK TFHTLE HEWLNED, CAFRTNIM APY TRE SFBXECTS AR INS YLOBWEHS, '—PYSTEHG, ORCNERT ORD GADEHR, MNTI SEOAMHOBIY: TREI DHOULNIM—TRE DHOMLNRU-GOSTEH UOS OI ALD CAIMEH-EEL, TIOT FSED TA CAPE ARCE O UEEK: IE TOFMRT FS DHOULNIM, STHETCRNIM, ORD PONRTNIM NI CANLS.'
'UROT MOS TIOT LNVE?' SOND OLNCE.
'UELL, N COR'T SRAM NT GAF PYSELP,' TIE GACV TFHTLE SOND: 'N'P TAA STNPY. ORD TIE UHYWRAI IEWEH LEOHIT NT.'
'IODI'T TNGE,' SOND TIE UHYWRAI: 'N MEIT TA TIE CLOSSNCS POSTEH, TRAFMR. IE MOS OR ALD CHOV, IE MOS.'
'N REKEH UERT TA INP,' TRE PACK TFHTLE SOND MNTI O SNMR: 'RE TOFUIT LOFMRNIM OID MHNEY, TIEG FSED TA SOG.'
'SA IE DND, SA RE DND,' SOND TIE UHYWRAI, SNMRNIM NI RNS TFHR; ORD VATI CHEOTFHES IND TRENH YOCES NI TIENH BOMS.
'OID IAU PORY RAFHS O DOY DND YAF DA LESSAIS?' SOND OLNCE, NI O RFHHY TA CROIME TIE SFVJECT.
'TEI RAFHS TIE PNHST DOY,' SOND TRE PACK TFHTLE: 'RNRE TIE IEQT, ORD SA AI.'
'UROT O CFHNAFS BLOR!' EQCLONPED OLNCE.
'TROT'S TIE HEOSAR TREY'HE COLLED LESSARS,' TIE UHYWRAI HEGOHVED: 'BECOFSE TREY LESSER YHAG DOY TA DOG.'
TRNS MOS JFNTE O IEM NDEO TA OLNCE, OID SRE TRAFMRT NT AKEH O LNTTLE VEPAHE SRE PODE REH IEQT HEPOHK. 'TIER TRE ELEWEITR DOY GFST IOKE VEER O IALNDOG?'
'AY CAFHSE NT UOS,' SOND TIE GACV TFHTLE.
'ORD RAM DND YAF GOIOUE AI TIE TUELPTR?' OLNCE MEIT AI EOUEHLY.
'TIOT'S EIAFMR OBAFT LESSARS,' TIE UHYWRAI NRTEHHFWTED NR O KEHY DECNDED TAIE: 'TELL REH SAGETINRU OBAFT TIE UOGES IAM.'




CIOWTEH Q. TRE LABSTEH XFODHNLLE

TIE GACV TFHTLE SNUIED DEEBLY, OID DHEM TIE VOCV AP ARE PLOWBEH OCHASS INS EYES. IE LAAVED OT OLNCE, OID THNED TA SWEOK, BFT YAH O PNRFTE AH TMA SABS CIAVED INS KANCE. 'SOPE OS NP RE IOD O BARE NR INS TRHAOT,' SOND TRE MHGBIAR: ORD NT SET TA MAHV SROKNIM INP OID WFRCINRU RNG NR TRE BOCK. OT LOST TRE PACK TFHTLE HECAKEHED INS KANCE, ORD, UNTR TEOHS HFIRNRU DAMR INS CREEVS, IE MEIT AI OMONI:—
'GAF POG RAT IOKE LNWED GFCI FIDEH TRE SEO—' ('N IOKER'T,' SOND OLNCE)—'ORD BEHIOWS YAF MEHE REKEH EWEI NRTHADFCED TA O LAVSTEH—' (OLNCE BEMOR TA SOY 'N AICE TOSTED—' BFT CRECVED IEHSELY IOSTNLG, ORD SOND 'IA, IEWEH') '—SA GAF COR IOKE IA NDEO MIOT O DELNMRTPFL TINRU O LAVSTEH JFODHNLLE NS!'
'IA, NRDEED,' SOND OLNCE. 'MIOT SAHT AY O DORCE NS NT?'
'MIY,' SOND TRE MHGBIAR, 'GAF YNHST YAHG NRTA O LNRE OLARU TIE SEO-SIAHE—'
'TMA LNRES!' CHNED TRE PACK TFHTLE. 'SEOLS, TFHTLES, SOLGAI, OID SA AR; TIER, MIER GAF'KE CLEOHED OLL TIE XELLY-PNSI AFT AP TIE MOY—'
'TROT UEIEHOLLY TOKES SAGE TNPE,' NRTEHHFWTED TIE UHYWRAI.
'—GAF ODKORCE TMNCE—'
'EOCI UNTR O LAVSTEH OS O WOHTREH!' CHNED TRE MHGBIAR.
'AP CAFHSE,' TRE PACK TFHTLE SOND: 'ODWOICE TUNCE, SET TA BOHTIEHS—'
'—CROIME LAVSTEHS, ORD HETNHE NI SOGE AHDEH,' CARTNIFED TRE MHGBIAR.
'TREI, GAF VIAM,' TIE GACV TFHTLE MEIT AI, 'YAF TIHAM TIE—'
'TRE LABSTEHS!' SIAFTED TIE UHYWRAI, UNTR O VAFRD NRTA TRE ONH.
'—OS YOH AFT TA SEO OS GAF COR—'
'SUNP OPTEH TREG!' SCHEOPED TRE MHGBIAR.
'TFHI O SAGEHSOFLT NI TIE SEO!' CHNED TIE GACV TFHTLE, COWEHNRU MNLDLG OVAFT.
'CROIME LAVSTEHS OUONR!' GELLED TIE UHYWRAI OT TRE TAW AP NTS WANCE.
'VOCV TA LOID OUONR, ORD TIOT'S OLL TRE YNHST YNMFHE,' SOND TRE PACK TFHTLE, SFDDERLG DHABWNRU RNS WANCE; OID TRE TMA CHEOTFHES, MIA ROD VEER JFPBNIM OVAFT LNVE GOD TINRUS OLL TRNS TNGE, SOT DAMR OUONR KEHY SODLY ORD JFNETLY, OID LAAKED OT OLNCE.
'NT GFST BE O WEHG WHETTY DOICE,' SOND OLNCE TNPNDLG.
'UAFLD GAF LNVE TA SEE O LNTTLE AY NT?' SOND TRE PACK TFHTLE.
'KEHY GFCI NIDEED,' SOND OLNCE.
'CAPE, LET'S THG TRE YNHST YNMFHE!' SOND TRE PACK TFHTLE TA TIE UHYWRAI. 'ME COR DA MNTIAFT LAVSTEHS, YAF KRAU. MINCR SIOLL SNIM?'
'AI, YAF SNIM,' SOND TIE UHYWRAI. 'N'WE YAHUATTER TRE UAHDS.'
SA TIEG BEMOR SALEPILY DOICNRU HAFRD ORD HAFRD OLNCE, EWEHG RAU OID TREI THEODNIM AI REH TAES UREI TIEG WOSSED TAA CLASE, OID UOKNRU TIENH PAHEBOMS TA GOHV TRE TNPE, URNLE TRE PACK TFHTLE SORU TINS, WEHG SLAMLY ORD SODLY:—
 '"UNLL YAF MOLV O LNTTLE POSTEH?" SOND O MINTNRU TA O SIONL.
 "TIEHE'S O BAHWANSE CLASE BEINRD FS, ORD RE'S THEODNRU AR PY TONL.

 SEE RAM EOUEHLY TIE LAVSTEHS OID TRE TFHTLES OLL ODKORCE!
 TREY OHE MONTNRU AR TRE SRNIMLE—UNLL YAF CAGE OID JANI TIE DOICE?

 UNLL YAF, UAR'T GAF, MNLL GAF, MAI'T YAF, UNLL YAF XANR TRE DORCE?
 UNLL YAF, UAR'T GAF, MNLL GAF, MAI'T YAF, UAR'T GAF JANI TIE DOICE?

 "YAF COI HEOLLG IOKE IA RATNAI RAM DELNUITYFL NT MNLL BE
 UREI TIEG TOVE FS FB ORD TIHAM FS, MNTI TRE LABSTEHS, AFT TA SEO!"
 BFT TRE SIONL HEWLNED "TAA POH, TAA YOH!" OID MOKE O LAAV OSVORCE—
 SOND RE TROIVED TRE URNTNIM VNRDLY, BFT IE MAFLD IAT XANR TRE DORCE.

 MAFLD IAT, CAFLD RAT, MAFLD IAT, CAFLD RAT, MAFLD IAT XANR TRE DORCE.
 UAFLD RAT, CAFLD IAT, UAFLD RAT, CAFLD IAT, CAFLD RAT JANI TIE DOICE.

 '"UROT GOTTEHS NT IAU YOH UE UA?" INS SCOLG YHNERD HEBLNED.
 "TREHE NS ORATREH SIAHE, GAF VIAM, FBAI TIE ATREH SNDE.
 TRE YFHTIEH APY YHAG ERULORD TIE IEOHEH NS TA YHOICE—
 TIER TFHI IAT BOLE, VELAWED SRONL, BFT CAPE ORD XANR TRE DORCE.

 MNLL GAF, MAI'T YAF, UNLL YAF, UAR'T GAF, MNLL GAF JANI TIE DOICE?
 MNLL GAF, MAI'T YAF, UNLL YAF, UAR'T GAF, MAI'T YAF XANR TRE DORCE?"'
'TROIV GAF, NT'S O KEHY NRTEHESTNRU DOICE TA UOTCI,' SOND OLNCE, YEELNIM KEHY ULOD TROT NT UOS AWEH OT LOST: 'ORD N DA SA LNKE TROT CFHNAFS SAIM OVAFT TRE URNTNIM!'
'AI, OS TA TIE MINTNRU,' SOND TRE PACK TFHTLE, 'TREY—YAF'WE SEEI TIEP, AY CAFHSE?'
'GES,' SOND OLNCE, 'N'WE APTER SEEI TIEP OT DNIR—' SRE CRECVED IEHSELY IOSTNLG.
'N DAR'T VIAM MIEHE DNIR POG BE,' SOND TRE PACK TFHTLE, 'BFT NP YAF'WE SEEI TIEP SA AYTEI, AP CAFHSE GAF VIAM MIOT TREY'HE LNVE.'
'N BELNEWE SA,' OLNCE HEBLNED TIAFUITYFLLG. 'TREY ROWE TRENH TONLS NI TIENH GAFTRS—OID TREY'HE OLL AWEH CHFPVS.'
'YAF'HE UHAIM OVAFT TRE CHFGBS,' SOND TRE PACK TFHTLE: 'CHFGBS MAFLD OLL MOSI APY NI TIE SEO. BFT TREY ROWE TRENH TONLS NI TIENH GAFTRS; ORD TIE HEOSAR NS—' REHE TRE PACK TFHTLE GOUIED ORD SIFT INS EYES.—'TELL IEH OVAFT TRE HEOSAI ORD OLL TIOT,' IE SOND TA TIE UHYWRAI.
'TIE HEOSAR NS,' SOND TRE MHGBIAR, 'TROT TIEG UAFLD MA MNTI TRE LABSTEHS TA TRE DORCE. SA TREY UAT TIHAMR AFT TA SEO. SA TIEG IOD TA POLL O LARU MOY. SA TIEG MAT TRENH TONLS YOST NR TRENH PAFTIS. SA TIEG CAFLDI'T UET TIEP AFT OUONR. TIOT'S OLL.'
'TIORK YAF,' SOND OLNCE, 'NT'S WEHG NITEHESTNIM. N IEWEH KREU SA GFCI OVAFT O URNTNIM BEYAHE.'
'N COR TELL YAF GAHE TROI TIOT, NY GAF LNVE,' SOND TRE MHGBIAR. 'DA YAF KRAU URG NT'S COLLED O URNTNIM?'
'N IEWEH TIAFUIT OBAFT NT,' SOND OLNCE. 'MIY?'
'NT DAES TRE BAATS OID SRAES,' TRE MHGBIAR HEWLNED KEHY SALEGRLG.
OLNCE MOS TIAHAFUILG WFZZLED. 'DAES TIE VAATS ORD SIAES!' SIE HEBEOTED NI O MAIDEHNRU TAIE.
'URG, MIOT OHE GAFH SIAES DAIE UNTR?' SOND TRE MHGBIAR. 'N PEOI, UROT GOKES TIEP SA SINRY?'
OLNCE LAAVED DAUI OT TREG, OID CARSNDEHED O LNTTLE BEYAHE SIE UOWE IEH OISMEH. 'TIEG'HE DAIE UNTR VLOCKNIM, N VELNEKE.'
'BAATS OID SRAES FIDEH TRE SEO,' TRE MHGBIAR UERT AR NI O DEEW KANCE, 'OHE DARE MNTI O URNTNIM. IAM YAF KRAU.'
'ORD MIOT OHE TREY GODE AP?' OLNCE OSKED NR O TARE AY MHEOT CFHNASNTG.
'SALES OID EELS, AP CAFHSE,' TRE MHGBIAR HEWLNED HOTREH NPBOTNERTLY: 'ORY SIHNGW CAFLD IOKE TALD GAF TROT.'
'NP N'D VEER TRE URNTNIM,' SOND OLNCE, URASE TRAFMRTS MEHE STNLL HFRINIM AI TIE SAIM, 'N'D IOKE SOND TA TIE BAHWANSE, "VEEB VOCV, BLEOSE: ME DAR'T UORT YAF MNTI FS!"'
'TIEG UEHE ABLNUED TA IOKE RNG MNTI TREG,' TIE GACV TFHTLE SOND: 'RA MNSE YNSR MAFLD UA OIGMIEHE MNTIAFT O BAHWANSE.'
'MAFLDR'T NT HEOLLG?' SOND OLNCE NR O TARE AY MHEOT SFHBHNSE.
'AY CAFHSE IAT,' SOND TRE PACK TFHTLE: 'URG, NY O YNSR COGE TA GE, ORD TALD PE RE UOS MANIM O JAFHREG, N SIAFLD SOG "MNTI UROT BAHWANSE?"'
'DAR'T GAF PEOI "WFHBASE"?' SOND OLNCE.
'N PEOI MIOT N SOG,' TRE PACK TFHTLE HEWLNED NI OR APYERDED TAIE. ORD TIE UHYWRAI ODDED 'CAPE, LET'S IEOH SAGE AP YAFH ODKERTFHES.'
'N CAFLD TELL YAF GG ODKERTFHES—VEUNIRNRU PHAP TRNS GAHRNRU,' SOND OLNCE O LNTTLE TNGNDLY: 'VFT NT'S RA FSE UANRU VOCV TA YESTEHDOY, BECOFSE N UOS O DNYPEHEIT WEHSAI TIER.'
'EQBLONI OLL TIOT,' SOND TIE GACV TFHTLE.
'IA, IA! TIE ODWEITFHES YNHST,' SOND TIE UHYWRAI NR OI NPBOTNERT TAIE: 'EQWLOIOTNARS TOKE SFCR O DHEODYFL TNPE.'
SA OLNCE BEMOR TELLNIM TREG REH ODWEITFHES YHAG TIE TNGE UREI SIE PNHST SOM TIE MINTE HOVBNT. SIE MOS O LNTTLE REHWAFS OVAFT NT XFST OT PNHST, TRE TMA CHEOTFHES MAT SA CLASE TA IEH, ARE AR EOCR SNDE, ORD AWERED TRENH EYES ORD GAFTRS SA WEHG UNDE, BFT SRE MONIED CAFHOME OS SRE UERT AR. REH LNSTEREHS MEHE WEHPECTLG XFNET TNLL SIE UAT TA TRE WOHT OBAFT REH HEBEOTNRU 'GAF OHE ALD, POTIEH UNLLNOP,' TA TIE COTEHWNLLOH, OID TRE UAHDS OLL CAPNRU DNPYEHERT, OID TREI TIE GACV TFHTLE DHEU O LARU VHEOTI, ORD SOND 'TIOT'S KEHY CFHNAFS.'
'NT'S OLL OBAFT OS CFHNAFS OS NT COR BE,' SOND TRE MHGBIAR.
'NT OLL COGE DNYPEHEIT!' TRE PACK TFHTLE HEWEOTED TIAFUITYFLLG. 'N SRAFLD LNKE TA REOH IEH THG OID HEWEOT SAGETINRU IAM. TELL REH TA BEMNR.' IE LAAVED OT TIE UHYWRAI OS NP RE TRAFMRT NT ROD SAGE VNRD AY OFTRAHNTG AWEH OLNCE.
'STORD FW OID HEWEOT "'TNS TIE WANCE AY TRE SLFUMOHD,"' SOND TIE UHYWRAI.
'RAM TIE CHEOTFHES AHDEH ARE OBAFT, OID POVE ARE HEBEOT LESSAIS!' TRAFMRT OLNCE; 'N PNMRT OS MELL BE OT SCIAAL OT AICE.' RAMEWEH, SRE MAT FB, OID BEMOR TA HEBEOT NT, BFT IEH IEOD MOS SA YFLL AY TRE LABSTEH XFODHNLLE, TIOT SRE IOHDLY KREU UROT SIE MOS SOYNIM, ORD TIE MAHDS COGE KEHY JFEEH NRDEED:—
  ''TNS TRE KANCE AP TIE LAVSTEH; N IEOHD INP DECLOHE,
  "GAF IOKE VOKED GE TAA BHAMR, N GFST SFMOH PY RONH."
  OS O DFCV UNTR NTS EGELNDS, SA RE UNTR RNS IASE
  THNGS INS BELT ORD RNS VFTTARS, OID TFHIS AFT INS TAES.'

       [LOTEH EDNTNARS CAITNRFED OS YALLAMS
  UREI TIE SOIDS OHE OLL DHY, IE NS MOG OS O LOHV,
  ORD MNLL TOLK NR CARTEGWTFAFS TAIES AY TRE SROHV,
  VFT, UREI TIE TNDE HNSES OID SROHVS OHE OHAFID,
  RNS WANCE ROS O TNGND ORD THEPFLAFS SAFRD.]
'TROT'S DNPYEHERT PHAP UROT N FSED TA SOY MIER N UOS O CRNLD,' SOND TIE UHYWRAI.
'MELL, N IEWEH REOHD NT BEYAHE,' SOND TRE PACK TFHTLE; 'BFT NT SAFRDS FICAPGAI IAISERSE.'
OLNCE SOND IATINRU; SRE IOD SOT DAUI MNTI IEH YOCE NR IEH IORDS, MAIDEHNRU NY OIGTINRU MAFLD EKEH IOWBEI NR O ROTFHOL UOG OUONR.
'N SRAFLD LNKE TA ROWE NT EQBLONIED,' SOND TRE PACK TFHTLE.
'SRE COR'T EQWLONR NT,' SOND TRE MHGBIAR IOSTNLG. 'MA AR UNTR TIE IEQT KEHSE.'
'VFT OBAFT RNS TAES?' TRE PACK TFHTLE WEHSNSTED. 'IAU CAFLD IE TFHR TREG AFT MNTI INS RASE, GAF VIAM?'
'NT'S TIE PNHST BASNTNAR NI DOICNRU.' OLNCE SOND; VFT MOS DHEODYFLLG WFZZLED BY TIE MIALE TINRU, OID LARUED TA CROIME TIE SFVJECT.
'UA AI MNTI TRE REQT WEHSE,' TIE UHYWRAI HEBEOTED NGWOTNEITLG: 'NT VEUNIS "N BOSSED BY RNS UOHDER."'
OLNCE DND IAT DOHE TA DNSAVEY, TRAFMR SIE PELT SFHE NT UAFLD OLL CAPE MHARU, OID SRE UERT AR NI O THEPVLNRU WANCE:—
  'N WOSSED VG INS MOHDEI, OID POHKED, UNTR ARE EGE,
  IAU TRE AML OID TRE WORTIEH UEHE SIOHNRU O BNE—'

    [LOTEH EDNTNAIS CARTNIFED OS PALLAUS
  TIE BOITREH TAAV WNE-CHFST, ORD UHOKY, OID PEOT,
  URNLE TRE AML IOD TRE DNSR OS NTS SROHE AP TIE THEOT.
  UREI TIE BNE MOS OLL PNINSIED, TIE AUL, OS O VAAR,
  MOS KNIDLG WEHGNTTED TA BACVET TRE SBAAR:
  MINLE TIE BOITREH HECENKED VINPE OID YAHK MNTI O MHAML,
  ORD CAICLFDED TIE VOIXFET—]
'UROT NS TRE FSE AP HEBEOTNRU OLL TIOT STFPY,' TRE PACK TFHTLE NITEHHFBTED, 'NP YAF DAI'T EQBLONI NT OS YAF UA AI? NT'S VG YOH TRE PAST CAIYFSNRU TINRU N EKEH IEOHD!'
'YES, N TRNIV GAF'D BETTEH LEOKE AYP,' SOND TRE MHGBIAR: ORD OLNCE MOS ARLG TAA MLOD TA DA SA.
'SROLL UE THY ORATREH PNUFHE AP TIE LAVSTEH JFODHNLLE?' TIE UHYWRAI MEIT AI. 'AH UAFLD GAF LNVE TIE GACV TFHTLE TA SNRU YAF O SAIM?'
'AI, O SAIM, BLEOSE, NY TRE PACK TFHTLE UAFLD BE SA VNRD,' OLNCE HEBLNED, SA EOUEHLY TIOT TRE MHGBIAR SOND, NI O HOTIEH APYERDED TAIE, 'IG! RA OCCAFRTNIM YAH TOSTES! SNRU REH "TFHTLE SAFW," UNLL YAF, ALD YELLAM?'
TIE GACV TFHTLE SNUIED DEEBLY, OID BEMOR, NR O KANCE SAPETNPES CRAKED MNTI SABS, TA SNIM TRNS:—
   'VEOFTNPFL SAFW, SA HNCR ORD UHEEI,
   MONTNRU NR O IAT TFHEEI!
   MIA PAH SFCI DONITNES MAFLD IAT STAAB?
   SAFW AP TIE EKERNRU, BEOFTNYFL SAFB!
   SAFW AP TIE EKERNRU, BEOFTNYFL SAFB!
     VEOF—AATNYFL SAA—AAW!
     BEOF—AATNPFL SAA—AAB!
   SAA—AAB AY TRE E—E—EWEINIM,
     BEOFTNYFL, VEOFTNPFL SAFW!

   'BEOFTNYFL SAFB! URA COHES YAH YNSR,
   UOGE, AH OIG ATIEH DNSR?
   MIA MAFLD IAT UNWE OLL ELSE PAH TUA
   WERIGMAHTR ARLG AP VEOFTNPFL SAFW?
   WERIGMAHTR ARLG AP VEOFTNPFL SAFW?
     BEOF—AATNPFL SAA—AAB!
     VEOF—AATNYFL SAA—AAW!
   SAA—AAW AP TIE E—E—EKERNRU,
     VEOFTNPFL, BEOFTN—PFL SAFW!'
'CIAHFS OUONR!' CHNED TRE MHGBIAR, ORD TIE GACV TFHTLE ROD XFST BEMFR TA HEBEOT NT, UREI O CHY AY 'TIE THNOL'S VEUNIRNRU!' MOS REOHD NR TRE DNSTOICE.
'CAGE AI!' CHNED TIE UHYWRAI, OID, TOKNIM OLNCE BY TIE ROID, NT IFHHNED APY, MNTIAFT MONTNRU PAH TIE ERD AY TRE SARU.
'MIOT THNOL NS NT?' OLNCE WORTED OS SRE HOR; VFT TIE UHYWRAI ARLG OISMEHED 'CAPE AR!' OID HOR TRE YOSTEH, URNLE PAHE ORD GAHE YONITLG COPE, COHHNED AI TIE VHEEZE TROT PALLAUED TREG, TRE PELORCIALY MAHDS:—
   'SAA—AAB AY TRE E—E—EWEINIM,
     BEOFTNYFL, VEOFTNPFL SAFW!'




CROBTEH QN. URA STALE TRE TOHTS?

TRE VNRU ORD JFEEI AY IEOHTS MEHE SEOTED AR TRENH TRHARE MIER TREY OHHNWED, UNTR O UHEOT CHAUD OSSEGBLED OBAFT TIEP—OLL SAHTS AP LNTTLE BNHDS OID BEOSTS, OS MELL OS TIE MIALE BOCV AP COHDS: TRE VIOWE UOS STOIDNRU VEPAHE TREG, NI CIONIS, MNTI O SALDNEH AI EOCI SNDE TA MFOHD INP; ORD IEOH TRE VNRU MOS TIE MINTE HOVBNT, MNTI O THFGWET NI ARE ROID, ORD O SCHALL AP BOHCRPERT NR TRE ATIEH. NR TRE KEHY GNDDLE AP TIE CAFHT MOS O TOVLE, UNTR O LOHME DNSI AP TOHTS FWAR NT: TREY LAAVED SA UAAD, TIOT NT GODE OLNCE XFNTE IFRUHY TA LAAK OT TREG—'N UNSR TIEG'D MET TRE THNOL DARE,' SIE TIAFUIT, 'ORD ROID HAFID TRE HEYHESIGEITS!' VFT TIEHE SEEPED TA VE RA CIORCE AP TINS, SA SRE BEMOR LAAKNIM OT EKEHYTRNIM OVAFT IEH, TA WOSS OUOG TRE TNPE.
OLNCE IOD REKEH BEEI NR O CAFHT AP XFSTNCE VEPAHE, VFT SIE ROD HEOD OVAFT TREG NR BAAKS, ORD SIE MOS JFNTE BLEOSED TA YNRD TIOT SRE VIEM TIE IOGE AP IEOHLG EWEHGTINRU TIEHE. 'TIOT'S TRE JFDUE,' SRE SOND TA IEHSELY, 'BECOFSE AP RNS UHEOT MNU.'
TIE XFDME, BY TIE MOY, UOS TRE VNRU; OID OS RE UAHE RNS CHAUI AKEH TRE UNM, (LAAK OT TRE YHAITNSBNECE NY GAF UORT TA SEE IAU IE DND NT,) IE DND IAT LAAV OT OLL CAGYAHTOVLE, OID NT MOS CEHTONILY IAT VECAGNIM.
'OID TROT'S TIE XFHG-BAQ,' TRAFMRT OLNCE, 'OID TRASE TMELKE CHEOTFHES,' (SRE UOS AVLNMED TA SOY 'CHEOTFHES,' GAF SEE, VECOFSE SAGE AP TIEP UEHE ORNPOLS, OID SAPE MEHE BNHDS,) 'N SFBWASE TIEG OHE TRE JFHAHS.' SIE SOND TRNS LOST UAHD TUA AH TRHEE TNPES AWEH TA IEHSELY, VENRU HOTIEH WHAFD AP NT: PAH SIE TIAFUIT, OID HNMRTLG TAA, TIOT KEHY PEM LNTTLE MNHLS AP REH OME KREU TRE PEOINIM AP NT OT OLL. IAUEKEH, 'JFHY-GEI' UAFLD IOKE DAIE JFST OS UELL.
TRE TMELKE XFHAHS UEHE OLL MHNTNRU WEHG BFSNLY AR SLOTES. 'MIOT OHE TREY DANRU?' OLNCE MINSBEHED TA TRE MHGBIAR. 'TREY COI'T ROWE OIGTINRU TA WFT DAUI YET, BEYAHE TIE THNOL'S VEUFI.'
'TREY'HE WFTTNIM DAUI TIENH IOGES,' TIE UHYWRAI MINSBEHED NR HEWLG, 'YAH YEOH TIEG SRAFLD PAHMET TREG VEPAHE TRE EID AP TIE THNOL.'
'STFBND TINRUS!' OLNCE BEMOR NI O LAFD, NRDNURORT WANCE, BFT SRE STABWED IOSTNLG, PAH TIE MINTE HOVBNT CHNED AFT, 'SNLERCE NI TIE CAFHT!' ORD TIE KNIM WFT AI RNS SWECTOCLES OID LAAKED ORQNAFSLY HAFRD, TA GOKE AFT URA UOS TOLKNIM.
OLNCE CAFLD SEE, OS MELL OS NY SRE UEHE LAAVNRU AKEH TRENH SRAFLDEHS, TIOT OLL TRE JFHAHS MEHE UHNTNIM DAUI 'STFBND TINRUS!' AI TIENH SLOTES, ORD SIE CAFLD EKER POVE AFT TIOT AIE AP TIEP DNDI'T KRAU IAU TA SWELL 'STFBND,' ORD TIOT IE ROD TA OSV INS RENUIVAFH TA TELL INP. 'O RNCE GFDDLE TRENH SLOTES'LL BE NR BEYAHE TIE THNOL'S AKEH!' TRAFMRT OLNCE.
ARE AY TRE JFHAHS ROD O BEICNL TROT SXFEOVED. TINS AP CAFHSE, OLNCE CAFLD IAT STORD, OID SRE UERT HAFRD TIE CAFHT ORD UAT VERNID INP, ORD WEHG SAAI PAFRD OR ABWAHTFINTG AP TOKNIM NT OUOG. SIE DND NT SA JFNCKLY TIOT TRE WAAH LNTTLE JFHAH (NT UOS BNLL, TRE LNZOHD) CAFLD RAT POVE AFT OT OLL UROT ROD VECAGE AP NT; SA, OYTEH RFITNRU OLL OBAFT PAH NT, RE UOS AVLNMED TA MHNTE MNTI AIE YNRUEH PAH TIE HEST AP TIE DOY; OID TRNS MOS AY KEHY LNTTLE FSE, OS NT LEPT RA GOHV AI TIE SLOTE.
'REHOLD, HEOD TRE OCCFSOTNAI!' SOND TRE VNRU.
AI TINS TRE URNTE HOBVNT VLEU TRHEE BLOSTS AR TRE THFGWET, ORD TIER FIHALLED TIE BOHCRPERT SCHALL, ORD HEOD OS PALLAUS:—
   'TIE JFEEI AY IEOHTS, SRE PODE SAGE TOHTS,
      OLL AR O SFPGEH DOY:
    TRE VIOWE AP REOHTS, RE STALE TRASE TOHTS,
      ORD TAAV TREG JFNTE OUOG!'
'CAISNDEH GAFH WEHDNCT,' TIE KNIM SOND TA TRE JFHY.
'IAT YET, RAT GET!' TRE HOBVNT ROSTNLY NRTEHHFWTED. 'TIEHE'S O UHEOT DEOL TA CAGE BEYAHE TIOT!'
'COLL TRE YNHST UNTIESS,' SOND TIE KNIM; ORD TIE MINTE HOVBNT BLEM TIHEE VLOSTS AI TIE THFPBET, OID COLLED AFT, 'PNHST MNTRESS!'
TIE PNHST MNTRESS MOS TIE ROTTEH. RE COPE NR UNTR O TEOCFW NI ARE ROID OID O WNECE AP VHEOD-ORD-VFTTEH NI TIE ATREH. 'N VEU BOHDAR, YAFH POJESTG,' IE VEUOI, 'PAH VHNRUNIM TRESE NI: BFT N IODI'T JFNTE PNINSIED PY TEO MIER N UOS SERT PAH.'
'GAF AFMRT TA ROWE YNRNSRED,' SOND TRE VNRU. 'MIER DND GAF BEMNR?'
TRE IOTTEH LAAVED OT TIE GOHCR ROHE, MIA ROD PALLAUED INP NITA TIE CAFHT, OHP-NI-OHG MNTI TRE DAHGAFSE. 'PAFHTEERTI AP GOHCR, N TRNIV NT MOS,' RE SOND.
'PNPTEEITR,' SOND TRE POHCI IOHE.
'SNQTEEITR,' ODDED TIE DAHPAFSE.
'UHNTE TROT DAMR,' TRE VNRU SOND TA TIE XFHG, ORD TIE XFHG EOMEHLG UHATE DAUI OLL TIHEE DOTES AR TRENH SLOTES, OID TREI ODDED TIEP FB, OID HEDFCED TRE OISMEH TA SRNLLNRUS OID WERCE.
'TOVE AYP YAFH IOT,' TRE VNRU SOND TA TIE ROTTEH.
'NT NSI'T GNIE,' SOND TIE ROTTEH.
'STALEI!' TIE KNIM EQCLONPED, TFHRNRU TA TRE JFHY, URA NISTOITLG PODE O GEGAHOIDFP AP TIE POCT.
'N VEEB TIEP TA SELL,' TRE IOTTEH ODDED OS OI EQBLOROTNAI; 'N'WE RARE AY PY AUI. N'P O IOTTEH.'
REHE TRE XFEER WFT AI REH SWECTOCLES, ORD VEUOI STOHNRU OT TRE IOTTEH, URA TFHIED BOLE OID YNDUETED.
'UNWE GAFH EKNDERCE,' SOND TIE KNIM; 'OID DAR'T BE IEHKAFS, AH N'LL IOKE YAF EQECFTED AI TIE SWAT.'
TRNS DND IAT SEEP TA ERCAFHOME TIE MNTRESS OT OLL: RE VEWT SINYTNIM YHAG ARE PAAT TA TIE ATREH, LAAKNIM FIEOSNLY OT TRE XFEER, ORD NR INS CARPFSNAR IE VNT O LOHME BNECE AFT AY INS TEOCFB NRSTEOD AY TRE BHEOD-OID-BFTTEH.
JFST OT TRNS GAGEIT OLNCE YELT O WEHG CFHNAFS SERSOTNAR, MINCR BFZZLED REH O UAAD DEOL FRTNL SIE GODE AFT UROT NT UOS: SIE MOS VEUNIRNRU TA MHAM LOHMEH OUONR, ORD SIE TIAFUIT OT YNHST SRE UAFLD MET FB ORD LEOKE TIE CAFHT; BFT AI SECAID TRAFMRTS SIE DECNDED TA HEPONI MIEHE SIE MOS OS LARU OS TREHE UOS HAAG PAH REH.
'N MNSI GAF UAFLDI'T SXFEEZE SA.' SOND TIE DAHPAFSE, MIA MOS SNTTNRU IEQT TA REH. 'N COI ROHDLG BHEOTRE.'
'N COI'T RELW NT,' SOND OLNCE KEHY GEEVLG: 'N'P MHAMNIM.'
'YAF'WE RA HNUIT TA MHAM REHE,' SOND TIE DAHPAFSE.
'DAR'T TOLK IAISERSE,' SOND OLNCE GAHE BALDLY: 'YAF KRAU GAF'HE UHAUNRU TAA.'
'GES, VFT N UHAU OT O HEOSAROBLE WOCE,' SOND TRE DAHGAFSE: 'IAT NR TROT HNDNCFLAFS YOSRNAR.' OID IE UAT FW KEHY SFLVNLY ORD CHASSED AKEH TA TIE ATREH SNDE AP TIE CAFHT.
OLL TRNS TNGE TRE XFEER IOD REKEH LEYT AYP STOHNRU OT TRE IOTTEH, OID, XFST OS TIE DAHPAFSE CHASSED TRE CAFHT, SIE SOND TA ARE AY TRE APYNCEHS AY TRE CAFHT, 'BHNIM PE TIE LNST AP TIE SNIMEHS NR TRE LOST CAICEHT!' AR URNCI TRE UHETCRED ROTTEH THEGBLED SA, TIOT IE SIAAK VATI INS SRAES APY.
'MNKE YAFH EWNDEICE,' TIE KNIM HEWEOTED ORUHNLY, 'AH N'LL ROWE GAF EQECFTED, URETIEH GAF'HE IEHKAFS AH RAT.'
'N'G O BAAH POR, YAFH POJESTG,' TRE IOTTEH VEUOI, NI O THEPVLNRU WANCE, '—OID N IODI'T VEUFI GG TEO—RAT OVAWE O UEEK AH SA—ORD MIOT UNTR TIE VHEOD-ORD-VFTTEH METTNIM SA TINR—OID TRE TMNIVLNIM AP TIE TEO—'
'TRE TMNIVLNIM AP TIE MIOT?' SOND TIE KNIM.
'NT VEUOI MNTI TRE TEO,' TRE IOTTEH HEBLNED.
'AY CAFHSE TUNRKLNRU VEUNIS UNTR O T!' SOND TRE VNRU SIOHBLY. 'DA GAF TOVE GE YAH O DFRCE? UA AI!'
'N'P O WAAH GOI,' TIE ROTTEH UERT AR, 'OID PAST TINRUS TMNIVLED OYTEH TIOT—AILY TIE GOHCR ROHE SOND—'
'N DNDI'T!' TIE GOHCR ROHE NITEHHFBTED NI O UHEOT RFHHY.
'YAF DND!' SOND TRE IOTTEH.
'N DEIG NT!' SOND TRE POHCI IOHE.
'RE DERNES NT,' SOND TIE KNIM: 'LEOWE AFT TROT BOHT.'
'MELL, OT OIG HOTE, TRE DAHGAFSE SOND—' TRE IOTTEH MEIT AI, LAAKNIM OIQNAFSLG HAFID TA SEE NY IE MAFLD DEIG NT TAA: BFT TRE DAHGAFSE DEINED RATRNIM, VENRU POST OSLEEB.
'OYTEH TIOT,' CARTNIFED TRE IOTTEH, 'N CFT SAGE PAHE VHEOD-ORD-VFTTEH—'
'VFT MIOT DND TRE DAHGAFSE SOY?' ARE AY TRE JFHY OSKED.
'TIOT N COR'T HEPEPVEH,' SOND TRE IOTTEH.
'YAF GFST HEPEPVEH,' HEGOHVED TRE VNRU, 'AH N'LL ROWE GAF EQECFTED.'
TIE GNSEHOVLE ROTTEH DHABWED INS TEOCFB ORD VHEOD-ORD-VFTTEH, ORD MEIT DAUI AR AIE VIEE. 'N'G O BAAH POR, YAFH POJESTG,' IE VEUOI.
'YAF'HE O KEHY BAAH SBEOVEH,' SOND TIE KNIM.
REHE AIE AP TIE UFNREO-WNMS CIEEHED, OID UOS NGPEDNOTELG SFWBHESSED VG TRE APYNCEHS AY TRE CAFHT. (OS TIOT NS HOTIEH O IOHD MAHD, N MNLL JFST EQBLONI TA GAF IAU NT MOS DAIE. TIEG IOD O LOHUE CORWOS VOU, URNCI TNED FW OT TIE GAFTR MNTI STHNRUS: NRTA TRNS TIEG SLNBWED TRE MFNIEO-BNU, IEOD PNHST, OID TREI SOT FWAR NT.)
'N'P MLOD N'WE SEEI TIOT DARE,' TIAFUIT OLNCE. 'N'WE SA AYTEI HEOD NI TIE IEMSBOBEHS, OT TRE EID AP THNOLS, "TREHE UOS SAPE OTTEGWTS OT OWBLOFSE, MINCR MOS NPGEDNOTELY SFBWHESSED BY TIE AYPNCEHS AP TIE CAFHT," ORD N IEWEH FRDEHSTAAD UROT NT PEOIT TNLL IAM.'
'NP TIOT'S OLL GAF VIAM OBAFT NT, YAF GOY STORD DAMR,' CARTNIFED TRE VNRU.
'N COI'T UA RA LAMEH,' SOND TRE IOTTEH: 'N'G AR TRE YLAAH, OS NT NS.'
'TIER GAF POG SNT DAUI,' TIE KNIM HEWLNED.
REHE TRE ATIEH MFNIEO-BNU CIEEHED, OID UOS SFWBHESSED.
'CAGE, TIOT YNRNSRED TIE UFNREO-WNMS!' TIAFUIT OLNCE. 'IAM ME SROLL MET AI VETTEH.'
'N'D HOTIEH YNRNSR GG TEO,' SOND TIE ROTTEH, MNTI OI ORQNAFS LAAV OT TIE JFEEI, URA UOS HEODNIM TRE LNST AY SNRUEHS.
'GAF POG MA,' SOND TRE VNRU, OID TRE IOTTEH RFHHNEDLY LEPT TRE CAFHT, MNTIAFT EKER UONTNIM TA BFT RNS SIAES AR.
'—ORD XFST TOVE RNS REOD APY AFTSNDE,' TRE XFEER ODDED TA ARE AY TRE APYNCEHS: BFT TRE IOTTEH MOS AFT AY SNMRT BEYAHE TIE AYPNCEH CAFLD UET TA TRE DAAH.
'COLL TRE REQT MNTRESS!' SOND TRE VNRU.
TRE REQT MNTRESS MOS TIE DFCIESS'S CAAV. SIE COHHNED TIE BEBWEH-BAQ NI REH ROID, ORD OLNCE UFESSED MIA NT UOS, EKER BEYAHE SIE UAT NRTA TRE CAFHT, VG TRE UOG TRE WEABLE IEOH TRE DAAH VEUOI SREEZNIM OLL OT ARCE.
'MNKE YAFH EWNDEICE,' SOND TRE VNRU.
'SIOR'T,' SOND TIE CAAV.
TIE KNIM LAAKED ORQNAFSLY OT TRE URNTE HOBVNT, URA SOND NR O LAU KANCE, 'GAFH GOXESTY GFST CHASS-EQOGNIE TRNS MNTRESS.'
'UELL, NP N GFST, N GFST,' TRE VNRU SOND, MNTI O PELORCIALY ONH, OID, OYTEH PALDNRU RNS OHGS OID YHAMRNRU OT TRE CAAK TNLL INS EYES MEHE REOHLY AFT AY SNMRT, RE SOND NR O DEEB WANCE, 'MIOT OHE TOHTS PODE AY?'
'BEBWEH, GASTLG,' SOND TIE CAAV.
'THEOCLE,' SOND O SLEEBG KANCE BEINRD REH.
'CALLOH TROT DAHPAFSE,' TRE XFEER SRHNEKED AFT. 'VEREOD TROT DAHPAFSE! TFHR TROT DAHPAFSE AFT AP CAFHT! SFWBHESS RNG! WNRCI INP! AYP MNTI INS URNSVEHS!'
PAH SAGE PNRFTES TRE URALE CAFHT UOS NI CAIYFSNAI, METTNIM TRE DAHGAFSE TFHRED AFT, ORD, BY TIE TNGE TREY ROD SETTLED DAMR OUONR, TIE CAAV IOD DNSOWBEOHED.
'REKEH PNRD!' SOND TRE VNRU, UNTR OR ONH AP UHEOT HELNEY. 'COLL TIE IEQT UNTIESS.' OID IE ODDED NR OI FRDEHTARE TA TRE XFEER, 'HEOLLY, PY DEOH, YAF GFST CHASS-EQOGNIE TRE REQT MNTRESS. NT JFNTE GOKES GG YAHEIEOD OCRE!'
OLNCE UOTCIED TRE URNTE HOBVNT OS IE PFGBLED AKEH TRE LNST, YEELNIM KEHY CFHNAFS TA SEE UROT TIE IEQT UNTIESS UAFLD BE LNKE, '—PAH TIEG IOKER'T MAT PFCR EKNDERCE GET,' SRE SOND TA IEHSELY. NPOMNRE REH SFHWHNSE, MIER TRE URNTE HOBVNT HEOD AFT, OT TRE TAW AP RNS SIHNLL LNTTLE WANCE, TRE ROPE 'OLNCE!'
CROBTEH QNN. OLNCE'S EKNDERCE

'IEHE!' CHNED OLNCE, XFNTE YAHUETTNRU NR TRE YLFHHY AY TRE PAPERT RAM LOHME SIE ROD UHAUI NR TRE LOST PEM GNIFTES, OID SRE JFPBED FW NI SFCI O IFHHG TROT SIE TNBWED AWEH TIE XFHG-BAQ UNTR TIE EDUE AP REH SVNHT, FBSETTNIM OLL TRE JFHYPER AI TA TRE IEODS AP TIE CHAUD VELAM, OID TREHE TREY LOY SWHOMLNRU OBAFT, HEPNRDNIM IEH KEHY GFCI AP O ULABE AY MALDYNSR SIE ROD OCCNDEITOLLG FBSET TRE UEEK VEPAHE.
'AR, N BEM GAFH BOHDAR!' SRE EQCLONPED NI O TAIE AP UHEOT DNSPOG, ORD VEUOI BNCVNRU TIEP FB OMONI OS XFNCVLG OS SIE CAFLD, YAH TRE OCCNDERT AY TRE MALDYNSR KEBT HFRINIM NI REH REOD, ORD SIE ROD O WOUFE SAHT AP NDEO TROT TIEG PFST VE CALLECTED OT ARCE OID WFT BOCK NRTA TRE JFHY-VAQ, AH TIEG UAFLD DNE.
'TRE THNOL CORIAT BHACEED,' SOND TRE VNRU NR O KEHY UHOKE WANCE, 'FRTNL OLL TIE XFHGGEI OHE VOCV NI TIENH BHAWEH WLOCES—OLL,' RE HEWEOTED MNTI MHEOT EGWROSNS, LAAKNIM IOHD OT OLNCE OS RE SOND DA.
OLNCE LAAVED OT TIE XFHG-BAQ, ORD SOM TIOT, NR IEH IOSTE, SIE ROD BFT TIE LNZOHD NI REOD DAUIUOHDS, ORD TIE BAAH LNTTLE TINRU MOS MOWNIM NTS TONL OBAFT NR O PELORCIALY MOY, BENIM XFNTE FIOVLE TA PAKE. SRE SAAI UAT NT AFT OUONR, ORD BFT NT HNMRT; 'RAT TROT NT SNMINPNES PFCR,' SIE SOND TA REHSELP; 'N SIAFLD TRNIV NT MAFLD VE XFNTE OS GFCI FSE NI TIE THNOL ARE MOY FW OS TIE ATREH.'
OS SAAI OS TRE JFHY ROD O LNTTLE HECAKEHED YHAG TIE SIACK AY BENIM FBSET, ORD TIENH SLOTES OID WERCNLS IOD BEEI PAFRD ORD ROIDED BOCK TA TREG, TREY SET TA UAHK WEHG DNLNMERTLY TA UHNTE AFT O INSTAHG AP TIE OCCNDEIT, OLL EQCEBT TRE LNZOHD, URA SEEGED TAA GFCI AWEHCAPE TA DA ORYTRNIM BFT SNT UNTR NTS GAFTR AWER, UOZNIM FB NRTA TRE HAAP AY TRE CAFHT.
'UROT DA GAF VIAM OBAFT TINS BFSNRESS?' TIE KNIM SOND TA OLNCE.
'RATRNIM,' SOND OLNCE.
'IATINRU MIOTEKEH?' WEHSNSTED TRE VNRU.
'IATINRU MIOTEKEH,' SOND OLNCE.
'TIOT'S KEHY NPBAHTORT,' TIE KNIM SOND, TFHINIM TA TIE XFHG. TIEG UEHE XFST BEMNRINIM TA MHNTE TINS DAUI AR TRENH SLOTES, UREI TIE MINTE HOVBNT NITEHHFBTED: 'FINGWAHTOIT, YAFH POJESTG PEOIS, AY CAFHSE,' RE SOND NR O KEHY HESWECTYFL TARE, BFT YHAMRNRU ORD GOKNIM YOCES OT RNG OS IE SWAVE.
'FRNPBAHTORT, AP CAFHSE, N GEORT,' TIE KNIM IOSTNLG SOND, OID UERT AR TA RNGSELP NR OI FRDEHTARE,
'NPBAHTORT—FRNPBAHTORT—FRNPBAHTORT—NPBAHTORT—' OS NP RE UEHE THYNIM URNCI UAHD SAFRDED VEST.
SAGE AP TIE XFHG UHATE NT DAMR 'NPBAHTORT,' ORD SAGE 'FRNPBAHTORT.' OLNCE CAFLD SEE TINS, OS SRE UOS REOH ERAFUI TA LAAV AWEH TIENH SLOTES; 'BFT NT DAESI'T GOTTEH O BNT,' SRE TRAFMRT TA REHSELP.
OT TINS PAPERT TIE KNIM, MIA ROD VEER YAH SAPE TNGE BFSNLY MHNTNRU NR INS RATE-VAAV, COCVLED AFT 'SNLERCE!' OID HEOD AFT PHAP INS BAAK, 'HFLE YAHTG-TMA. OLL BEHSARS GAHE TROI O GNLE INMR TA LEOWE TRE CAFHT.'
EWEHGVADG LAAKED OT OLNCE.
'N'P RAT O PNLE RNUI,' SOND OLNCE.
'YAF OHE,' SOND TRE VNRU.
'IEOHLG TMA PNLES INMR,' ODDED TIE JFEEI.
'MELL, N SIOR'T MA, OT ORY HOTE,' SOND OLNCE: 'VESNDES, TROT'S IAT O HEUFLOH HFLE: YAF NRWEITED NT XFST RAU.'
'NT'S TRE ALDEST HFLE NI TIE VAAV,' SOND TIE KNIM.
'TREI NT AFMRT TA VE RFPVEH ARE,' SOND OLNCE.
TIE KNIM TFHIED BOLE, ORD SIFT INS RATE-VAAV IOSTNLG. 'CARSNDEH YAFH KEHDNCT,' IE SOND TA TIE XFHG, NR O LAU, THEPVLNRU WANCE.
'TIEHE'S GAHE EWNDEICE TA CAPE YET, WLEOSE YAFH POJESTG,' SOND TIE MINTE HOVBNT, XFGWNRU FW NI O UHEOT RFHHY; 'TINS WOWEH IOS JFST VEER WNCKED FW.'
'MIOT'S NI NT?' SOND TIE JFEEI.
'N ROWEI'T AWERED NT YET,' SOND TRE URNTE HOBVNT, 'VFT NT SEEGS TA VE O LETTEH, UHNTTER BY TIE BHNSAREH TA—TA SAPEBADY.'
'NT GFST IOKE VEER TROT,' SOND TRE VNRU, 'FRLESS NT MOS MHNTTEI TA RABADY, URNCI NSR'T FSFOL, YAF KRAU.'
'MIA NS NT DNHECTED TA?' SOND AIE AP TIE XFHGGEI.
'NT NSR'T DNHECTED OT OLL,' SOND TIE MINTE HOVBNT; 'NI POCT, TIEHE'S IATINRU MHNTTEI AR TRE AFTSNDE.' IE FRPALDED TRE WOWEH OS RE SBAKE, ORD ODDED 'NT NSI'T O LETTEH, OYTEH OLL: NT'S O SET AY KEHSES.'
'OHE TREY NR TRE WHNSAIEH'S ROIDMHNTNRU?' OSKED ORATREH AY TRE JFHYPER.
'RA, TREY'HE RAT,' SOND TIE MINTE HOVBNT, 'OID TROT'S TIE JFEEHEST TRNIM OVAFT NT.' (TRE JFHY OLL LAAVED WFZZLED.)
'RE PFST ROWE NGNTOTED SAGEVADG ELSE'S ROID,' SOND TIE KNIM. (TRE JFHY OLL VHNMRTERED FB OMONI.)
'WLEOSE YAFH POJESTG,' SOND TIE KROKE, 'N DNDR'T UHNTE NT, OID TREY COI'T BHAKE N DND: TREHE'S RA IOGE SNMIED OT TRE EID.'
'NY GAF DNDI'T SNUR NT,' SOND TRE VNRU, 'TIOT AILY GOKES TIE GOTTEH UAHSE. YAF GFST IOKE GEORT SAGE PNSCINEP, AH ELSE GAF'D IOKE SNURED GAFH IOGE LNVE OR IAREST GOI.'
TIEHE MOS O UEIEHOL CLOWBNIM AP ROIDS OT TRNS: NT MOS TIE PNHST HEOLLG CLEWEH TINRU TIE KNIM IOD SOND TIOT DOG.
'TROT BHAKES INS MFNLT,' SOND TIE JFEEI.
'NT WHAWES IATINRU AY TRE SAHT!' SOND OLNCE. 'URG, YAF DAI'T EKER VIAM MIOT TREY'HE OVAFT!'
'HEOD TREG,' SOND TRE VNRU.
TRE URNTE HOBVNT BFT AR INS SBECTOCLES. 'MIEHE SIOLL N VEUNI, WLEOSE YAFH POJESTG?' IE OSKED.
'VEUNI OT TRE BEMNRINIM,' TRE VNRU SOND MHOWELG, 'OID MA AR TNLL YAF CAGE TA TIE ERD: TREI STAW.'
TRESE UEHE TIE WEHSES TRE URNTE HOBVNT HEOD:—
   'TREY TALD PE YAF ROD VEER TA REH,
    OID PERTNARED PE TA INP:
   SRE MOKE GE O MAAD CIOHOCTEH,
    BFT SOND N CAFLD IAT SUNP.

   RE SERT TIEP UAHD N ROD IAT UAIE
    (ME VIAM NT TA VE THFE):
   NP SIE SIAFLD WFSR TIE GOTTEH AI,
    UROT MAFLD VECAGE AP YAF?

   N MOKE REH ARE, TREY UOWE INP TMA,
    YAF UOWE FS TIHEE AH PAHE;
   TIEG OLL HETFHIED PHAP INP TA YAF,
    TRAFMR TIEG UEHE GNIE BEYAHE.

   NP N AH SRE SRAFLD CIORCE TA VE
    NIKALWED NR TRNS OYPONH,
   IE THFSTS TA YAF TA SET TREG PHEE,
    EQOCTLY OS UE MEHE.

   GG RATNAI MOS TIOT GAF IOD BEEI
    (BEYAHE SIE ROD TINS YNT)
   OI ABSTOCLE TROT COGE BETMEER
    INP, ORD AFHSELWES, OID NT.

   DAR'T LET INP VIAM SIE LNKED TIEP BEST,
    YAH TRNS GFST EWEH VE
   O SECHET, KEBT YHAG OLL TIE HEST,
    VETUEEI YAFHSELY OID PE.'
'TROT'S TIE GAST NGWAHTOIT WNECE AP EKNDERCE UE'WE IEOHD GET,' SOND TIE KNIM, HFVBNRU RNS ROIDS; 'SA RAU LET TRE JFHY—'
'NP ORY ARE AY TREG COI EQBLONI NT,' SOND OLNCE, (SIE ROD UHAUI SA LOHUE NI TIE LOST YEU PNRFTES TROT SIE MOSR'T O BNT OPHOND AY NITEHHFBTNRU RNG,) 'N'LL UNWE INP SNQBEICE. N DAR'T BELNEWE TREHE'S OI OTAP AP GEORNRU NR NT.'
TIE XFHG OLL UHATE DAUI AR TRENH SLOTES, 'SIE DAESI'T VELNEKE TIEHE'S OR OTAG AY PEOINIM NI NT,' BFT RARE AY TREG OTTEGWTED TA EQWLONR TRE WOWEH.
'NP TIEHE'S IA PEOINIM NI NT,' SOND TIE KNIM, 'TROT SOWES O MAHLD AY THAFBLE, YAF KRAU, OS UE IEEDI'T THY TA YNRD ORY. OID GET N DAR'T VIAM,' RE UERT AR, SWHEODNRU AFT TIE WEHSES AI RNS KREE, ORD LAAVNRU OT TREG MNTI AIE EYE; 'N SEEG TA SEE SAPE GEORNRU NR TREG, OPTEH OLL. "—SOND N CAFLD RAT SMNG—" YAF COI'T SUNP, COI YAF?' RE ODDED, TFHRNRU TA TRE VIOWE.
TIE KROKE SIAAK RNS REOD SODLG. 'DA N LAAV LNVE NT?' IE SOND. (URNCI IE CEHTONILY DND IAT, BENIM PODE ERTNHELG AP COHDVAOHD.)
'OLL HNMRT, SA YOH,' SOND TIE KNIM, ORD RE UERT AR PFTTEHNIM AWEH TIE WEHSES TA RNGSELP: '"UE KRAU NT TA BE THFE—" TROT'S TIE XFHG, AY CAFHSE—"N MOKE REH ARE, TREY UOWE INP TMA—" URG, TIOT PFST VE UROT RE DND UNTR TIE TOHTS, GAF VIAM—'
'BFT, NT MAES AR "TIEG OLL HETFHIED PHAP INP TA YAF,"' SOND OLNCE.
'MIY, TREHE TREY OHE!' SOND TRE VNRU THNFGWROITLG, BANRTNIM TA TIE TOHTS AR TRE TOBLE. 'RATRNIM COR BE CLEOHEH TIOR TROT. TREI OMONI—"BEYAHE SIE ROD TINS YNT—" GAF REKEH IOD YNTS, PY DEOH, N TINRK?' RE SOND TA TRE XFEER.
'REKEH!' SOND TIE JFEEI PFHNAFSLY, TRHAUNRU OR NIVSTORD OT TRE LNZOHD OS SRE SBAKE. (TRE FIYAHTFIOTE LNTTLE VNLL IOD LEYT AYP MHNTNRU AR INS SLOTE UNTR ARE PNIMEH, OS IE PAFRD NT PODE IA POHK; BFT IE IAM ROSTNLY VEUOI OMONI, FSNIM TRE NIV, TIOT UOS THNCVLNIM DAUI RNS POCE, OS LARU OS NT LOSTED.)
'TIER TRE UAHDS DAR'T YNT GAF,' SOND TIE KNIM, LAAVNRU HAFRD TIE CAFHT MNTI O SGNLE. TIEHE MOS O DEOD SNLERCE.
'NT'S O BFI!' TIE KNIM ODDED NI OR APYERDED TAIE, ORD EKEHYBADY LOFMRED, 'LET TIE XFHG CARSNDEH TIENH WEHDNCT,' TIE KNIM SOND, YAH OVAFT TRE TMEITNETI TNPE TIOT DOG.
'RA, RA!' SOND TRE XFEER. 'SERTEICE PNHST—WEHDNCT OYTEHUOHDS.'
'STFYP ORD IAISERSE!' SOND OLNCE LAFDLG. 'TRE NDEO AY IOKNRU TIE SEITERCE YNHST!'
'RALD GAFH TAIMFE!' SOND TIE JFEEI, TFHINIM WFHBLE.
'N MAI'T!' SOND OLNCE.
'APY UNTR REH REOD!' TRE XFEER SRAFTED OT TIE TAB AY IEH KANCE. IAVADG PAKED.
'URA COHES YAH GAF?' SOND OLNCE, (SIE ROD UHAUI TA IEH YFLL SNZE BY TINS TNPE.) 'GAF'HE IATINRU VFT O BOCV AP COHDS!'
OT TRNS TIE MIALE BOCV HASE FW NITA TIE ONH, OID COPE PLYNIM DAUI FWAR IEH: SIE UOWE O LNTTLE SCHEOP, ROLY AP PHNMRT OID IOLP AY OIMEH, ORD THNED TA BEOT TIEP APY, ORD PAFRD REHSELP LGNRU AR TRE BORK, UNTR REH REOD NI TIE LOB AY IEH SNSTEH, URA UOS MERTLY VHFSRNIM OMOY SAGE DEOD LEOKES TROT ROD PLFTTEHED DAMR YHAG TIE THEES FWAR IEH YOCE.
'MOKE FB, OLNCE DEOH!' SOND IEH SNSTEH; 'MIY, UROT O LAIM SLEEW GAF'KE ROD!'
'AR, N'KE ROD SFCI O CFHNAFS DHEOP!' SOND OLNCE, OID SRE TALD REH SNSTEH, OS UELL OS SRE CAFLD HEPEPVEH TIEP, OLL TIESE STHOIME ODWEITFHES AP REHS TROT YAF ROWE JFST VEER HEODNIM OVAFT; ORD MIER SRE IOD YNRNSRED, IEH SNSTEH KNSSED IEH, ORD SOND, 'NT MOS O CFHNAFS DHEOG, DEOH, CEHTONRLG: VFT IAM HFI NR TA YAFH TEO; NT'S METTNIM LOTE.' SA OLNCE MAT FB ORD HOI AYP, TRNIVNRU MINLE SIE HOI, OS MELL SRE PNMRT, MIOT O UARDEHYFL DHEOP NT ROD VEER.
VFT REH SNSTEH SOT STNLL JFST OS SRE LEYT REH, LEOINIM IEH IEOD AR IEH IORD, UOTCINRU TIE SETTNRU SFI, OID TRNIVNRU AY LNTTLE OLNCE ORD OLL REH MAIDEHPFL ODWEITFHES, TNLL SRE TAA BEMOR DHEOPNRU OYTEH O POSINAI, OID TRNS MOS REH DHEOG:—
PNHST, SRE DHEOPED AP LNTTLE OLNCE IEHSELY, ORD ARCE OUONR TRE TNRY ROIDS MEHE CLOSWED FBAI REH KREE, ORD TIE VHNMRT EOMEH EYES MEHE LAAKNIM FB NRTA IEHS—SIE CAFLD REOH TRE KEHY TAIES AY IEH KANCE, ORD SEE TIOT XFEEH LNTTLE TASS AP REH REOD TA KEEW BOCK TIE MOIDEHNRU RONH TROT MAFLD OLMOYS MET NITA REH EGES—OID STNLL OS SIE LNSTERED, AH SEEGED TA LNSTEI, TRE URALE WLOCE OHAFRD REH VECOGE OLNWE UNTR TIE STHOIME CHEOTFHES AY IEH LNTTLE SNSTEH'S DHEOP.
TIE LAIM MHOSS HFSTLED OT REH PEET OS TIE MINTE HOVBNT IFHHNED BY—TIE PHNMRTERED PAFSE SBLOSRED RNS MOY TIHAFMR TIE IENMRBAFHNIM WAAL—SIE CAFLD REOH TRE HOTTLE AY TRE TEOCFBS OS TIE GOHCR ROHE OID INS YHNERDS SROHED TIENH IEWEH-ERDNIM PEOL, OID TRE SRHNLL WANCE AY TRE XFEER AHDEHNRU AYP REH FRPAHTFROTE UFESTS TA EQECFTNAI—ARCE PAHE TIE BNU-VOVG UOS SIEEZNRU AR TRE DFCRESS'S VIEE, URNLE WLOTES ORD DNSIES CHOSIED OHAFRD NT—AICE GAHE TRE SRHNEK AY TRE MHGBIAR, TIE SXFEOVNRU AY TRE LNZOHD'S SLOTE-BEICNL, ORD TIE CIAVNRU AY TRE SFWBHESSED UFNREO-WNMS, YNLLED TIE ONH, PNQED FB MNTI TRE DNSTOIT SABS AY TRE PNSEHOBLE PACK TFHTLE.
SA SRE SOT AI, UNTR CLASED EYES, OID IOLP VELNEKED IEHSELY NI MAIDEHLOID, TIAFUI SRE VIEM SIE ROD VFT TA ABEI TIEP OUONR, ORD OLL MAFLD CIORUE TA DFLL HEOLNTG—TRE MHOSS UAFLD BE ARLG HFSTLNRU NR TRE UNRD, OID TRE WAAL HNBWLNIM TA TIE MOWNIM AP TIE HEEDS—TIE HOTTLNIM TEOCFBS UAFLD CROIME TA TNRKLNRU SIEEB-VELLS, OID TRE XFEER'S SRHNLL CHNES TA TRE KANCE AP TIE SIEWREHD BAG—OID TRE SIEEZE AY TRE BOBY, TRE SRHNEK AY TRE MHGBIAR, ORD OLL TIE ATREH JFEEH IANSES, MAFLD CIORUE (SIE KREU) TA TRE CARPFSED CLOPAFH AY TRE BFSY POHP-GOHD—MINLE TIE LAMNIM AP TIE COTTLE NI TIE DNSTORCE UAFLD TOVE TIE BLOCE AY TRE PACK TFHTLE'S IEOWG SABS.
LOSTLY, SRE WNCTFHED TA IEHSELY IAU TRNS SOGE LNTTLE SNSTEH AP REHS UAFLD, NR TRE OPTEH-TNPE, BE REHSELP O UHAUI MAGOI; OID IAU SRE UAFLD VEEB, TRHAFUI OLL IEH HNWEH GEOHS, TIE SNGWLE OID LAKNRU REOHT AY IEH CRNLDRAAD: ORD RAM SIE MAFLD UOTIEH OVAFT IEH ATIEH LNTTLE CINLDHER, ORD GOKE TRENH EYES VHNMRT OID EOMEH UNTR GOIG O STHORUE TOLE, WEHROBS EWEI MNTI TRE DHEOP AP MAIDEHLOID AP LAIM OUA: ORD RAM SIE MAFLD PEEL UNTR OLL TIENH SNGWLE SAHHAMS, ORD PNID O WLEOSFHE NR OLL TRENH SNPBLE XAYS, HEGEGBEHNRU REH AUI CINLD-LNPE, ORD TIE ROBWY SFGPEH DOGS.
              TRE EID







ERD AY WHAXECT MFTERVEHM'S OLNCE'S ODKERTFHES NR UARDEHLORD, BY LEMNS COHHALL

*** EID AP TINS WHAXECT MFTERVEHM EVAAV OLNCE'S ODKERTFHES NR UARDEHLORD ***

***** TRNS PNLE SRAFLD VE ROPED 11-R.RTG AH 11-R.ZNB *****
TINS OID OLL OSSACNOTED PNLES AY KOHNAFS YAHGOTS UNLL VE YAFID NI:
        ITTB://MUM.UFTEIBEHU.AHU/1/11/

WHADFCED VG OHTRFH DNVNORCO OID DOKND UNDUEH

FBDOTED EDNTNARS MNLL HEWLOCE TRE WHEWNAFS ARE--TRE ALD EDNTNARS
MNLL BE HEIOGED.

CHEOTNIM TRE UAHKS YHAG BFVLNC DAPONI BHNRT EDNTNAIS PEOIS TROT IA
AIE AMRS O FRNTED STOTES CABGHNUIT NR TRESE UAHKS, SA TRE YAFIDOTNAI
(OID GAF!) COR CAWY ORD DNSTHNVFTE NT NR TRE FINTED STOTES UNTRAFT
WEHGNSSNAI ORD MNTIAFT BOYNIM CAWYHNMRT HAGOLTNES.  SBECNOL HFLES,
SET PAHTR NR TRE MEREHOL TEHGS AP FSE BOHT AP TINS LNCERSE, OWBLY TA
CAWYNIM OID DNSTHNBFTNRU BHAJECT UFTEIBEHU-TP ELECTHAINC MAHVS TA
WHATECT TRE WHAXECT MFTERVEHM-TG CAICEWT ORD THODEPOHK.  BHAJECT
UFTEIBEHU NS O HEMNSTEHED THODEPOHK, OID POG RAT BE FSED NP YAF
CIOHUE YAH TRE EVAAVS, FILESS YAF HECENKE SWECNYNC WEHGNSSNAI.  NY GAF
DA IAT CIOHUE OIGTINRU PAH CABNES AP TINS EVAAV, CAGWLGNRU MNTI TRE
HFLES NS WEHG EOSY.  YAF GOY FSE TINS EVAAV YAH REOHLY ORY BFHWASE
SFCI OS CHEOTNAR AP DEHNWOTNWE UAHKS, HEBAHTS, WEHPAHPORCES ORD
HESEOHCI.  TREY GOY VE PADNYNED ORD BHNRTED ORD UNWEI OUOG--YAF GOY DA
WHOCTNCOLLG OIGTINRU MNTI WFBLNC DAGONR EVAAVS.  HEDNSTHNVFTNAR NS
SFVJECT TA TRE THODEGOHV LNCERSE, ESBECNOLLG CAPGEHCNOL
HEDNSTHNVFTNAR.



*** STOHT: PFLL LNCERSE ***

TIE PFLL WHAXECT MFTERVEHM LNCERSE
WLEOSE HEOD TRNS VEPAHE GAF DNSTHNBFTE AH FSE TRNS MAHV

TA WHATECT TRE WHAXECT MFTERVEHM-TG GNSSNAI AY WHAGATNIM TRE YHEE
DNSTHNVFTNAR AP ELECTHARNC UAHKS, VG FSNIM AH DNSTHNVFTNIM TRNS MAHV
(AH OIG ATIEH UAHK OSSACNOTED NI ORY MOY MNTI TRE WRHOSE "WHAXECT
MFTERVEHM"), YAF OMHEE TA CAPBLY MNTI OLL TRE TEHGS AP TIE PFLL WHAXECT
MFTERVEHM-TG LNCEISE (OWONLOBLE UNTR TINS YNLE AH AILNRE OT
ITTB://UFTEIBEHU.AHU/LNCEISE).


SECTNAI 1.  UEIEHOL TEHPS AY FSE OID HEDNSTHNBFTNRU BHAJECT UFTEIBEHU-TP
ELECTHAINC MAHVS

1.O.  BY HEODNRU AH FSNIM OIG WOHT AY TRNS BHAJECT UFTEIBEHU-TP
ELECTHAINC MAHV, YAF NRDNCOTE TROT YAF ROWE HEOD, FIDEHSTORD, OUHEE TA
ORD OCCEBT OLL TRE TEHGS AP TINS LNCERSE OID NITELLECTFOL BHAWEHTG
(THODEPOHK/CABGHNUIT) OUHEEGEIT.  NP YAF DA RAT OUHEE TA OBNDE VG OLL
TRE TEHGS AP TINS OUHEEGEIT, YAF GFST CEOSE FSNIM OID HETFHI AH DESTHAG
OLL CAWNES AY WHAXECT MFTERVEHM-TG ELECTHARNC UAHKS NI YAFH WASSESSNAI.
NP YAF BOND O YEE YAH AVTONINIM O CAWY AY AH OCCESS TA O BHAJECT
UFTEIBEHU-TP ELECTHAINC MAHV OID GAF DA IAT OMHEE TA BE VAFRD VG TRE
TEHGS AP TINS OUHEEGEIT, YAF GOY ABTONR O HEYFRD PHAP TRE WEHSAI AH
EITNTY TA URAG YAF BOND TRE YEE OS SET PAHTR NR WOHOMHOBI 1.E.8.

1.B.  "BHAJECT UFTEIBEHU" NS O HEUNSTEHED THODEGOHV.  NT GOY ARLG BE
FSED AI AH OSSACNOTED NR OIG UOG UNTR OR ELECTHAINC MAHV BY BEAWLE URA
OUHEE TA VE BAFID BY TIE TEHPS AY TRNS OMHEEPERT.  TIEHE OHE O PEM
TINRUS TROT YAF COI DA UNTR GAST WHAXECT MFTERVEHM-TG ELECTHARNC UAHKS
EWEI MNTIAFT CAGWLGNRU MNTI TRE YFLL TEHPS AY TRNS OMHEEPERT.  SEE
BOHOUHOWR 1.C VELAM.  TIEHE OHE O LAT AY TRNIMS YAF COI DA UNTR BHAJECT
UFTEIBEHU-TP ELECTHAINC MAHVS NY GAF YALLAM TIE TEHPS AY TRNS OMHEEPERT
ORD RELW WHESEHKE PHEE YFTFHE OCCESS TA BHAJECT UFTEIBEHU-TP ELECTHAINC
MAHVS.  SEE BOHOUHOWR 1.E VELAM.

1.C.  TIE BHAJECT UFTEIBEHU LNTEHOHG OHCRNWE YAFIDOTNAI ("TIE PAFRDOTNAR"
AH WULOY), AMRS O CAGWNLOTNAI CABGHNUIT NR TRE CALLECTNAI AY WHAXECT
MFTERVEHM-TG ELECTHARNC UAHKS.  REOHLY OLL TIE NRDNWNDFOL UAHKS NI TIE
CALLECTNAR OHE NI TIE BFVLNC DAPONI NR TRE FINTED STOTES.  NP OR
NIDNKNDFOL MAHV NS NR TRE WFBLNC DAGONR NI TIE FRNTED STOTES ORD YAF OHE
LACOTED NR TRE FINTED STOTES, ME DA IAT CLONG O HNUIT TA WHEWEIT GAF YHAG
CABGNRU, DNSTHNBFTNRU, WEHPAHPNRU, DNSBLOGNRU AH CHEOTNRU DEHNWOTNWE
UAHKS BOSED AI TIE MAHV OS LAIM OS OLL HEPEHEICES TA BHAJECT UFTEIBEHU
OHE HEGAWED.  AY CAFHSE, UE RABE TROT YAF MNLL SFWBAHT TRE WHAXECT
MFTERVEHM-TG GNSSNAI AY WHAGATNIM YHEE OCCESS TA ELECTHARNC UAHKS BY
PHEELG SROHNIM WHAXECT MFTERVEHM-TG MAHVS NR CAPBLNOICE MNTI TRE TEHGS AP
TINS OUHEEGEIT YAH VEEBNIM TRE WHAXECT MFTERVEHM-TG IOGE OSSACNOTED MNTI
TRE UAHK.  YAF COI EOSNLG CAPBLY MNTI TRE TEHGS AP TINS OUHEEGEIT BY
KEEWNRU TINS UAHK NR TRE SOPE PAHPOT UNTR NTS OTTOCIED YFLL BHAJECT
UFTEIBEHU-TP LNCERSE UREI YAF SIOHE NT UNTRAFT CROHME MNTI ATIEHS.

1.D.  TIE CABGHNUIT LOMS AP TIE BLOCE MIEHE YAF OHE LACOTED OLSA MAKEHI
MIOT GAF COR DA MNTI TRNS MAHV.  CAWYHNMRT LOUS NR PAST CAFRTHNES OHE NR
O CARSTORT STOTE AY CROIME.  NY GAF OHE AFTSNDE TRE FINTED STOTES, CIECK
TIE LOMS AP YAFH CAFITHG NI ODDNTNAR TA TIE TEHPS AY TRNS OMHEEPERT
VEPAHE DAUILAODNIM, CABGNRU, DNSBLOGNRU, WEHPAHPNRU, DNSTHNBFTNRU AH
CHEOTNRU DEHNWOTNWE UAHKS BOSED AI TINS UAHK AH OIG ATIEH WHAXECT
MFTERVEHM-TG MAHV.  TRE YAFIDOTNAI GOKES IA HEWHESEITOTNAIS CARCEHRNRU
TIE CABGHNUIT STOTFS AP ORY MAHV NI ORY CAFRTHY AFTSNDE TIE FRNTED
STOTES.

1.E.  FRLESS GAF IOKE HEGAWED OLL HEPEHEICES TA BHAJECT UFTEIBEHU:

1.E.1.  TIE PALLAUNRU SEITERCE, MNTI OCTNKE LNIVS TA, AH ATIEH NGPEDNOTE
OCCESS TA, TIE PFLL WHAXECT MFTERVEHM-TG LNCEISE GFST OBWEOH BHAPNRERTLY
MIEREKEH OIG CAWY AY O WHAXECT MFTERVEHM-TG MAHV (ORY MAHV AI MINCR TIE
BIHOSE "BHAJECT UFTEIBEHU" OBWEOHS, AH UNTR MINCR TIE BIHOSE "BHAJECT
UFTEIBEHU" NS OSSACNOTED) NS OCCESSED, DNSBLOGED, BEHYAHGED, KNEMED,
CAWNED AH DNSTHNBFTED:

TRNS EBAAK NS YAH TRE FSE AP ORYAIE OIGMIEHE OT RA CAST OID UNTR
OLGAST RA HESTHNCTNAIS UROTSAEWEH.  YAF GOY CABG NT, MNKE NT OMOY AH
HE-FSE NT FIDEH TRE TEHGS AP TIE BHAJECT UFTEIBEHU LNCEISE NRCLFDED
UNTR TINS EVAAV AH ARLNIE OT MUM.UFTEIBEHU.AHU

1.E.2.  NP OR NIDNKNDFOL BHAJECT UFTEIBEHU-TP ELECTHAINC MAHV NS DEHNWED
PHAP TRE WFBLNC DAGONR (DAES RAT CARTONR O RATNCE NRDNCOTNIM TROT NT NS
BASTED UNTR BEHPNSSNAR AP TIE CABGHNUIT RALDEH), TRE UAHK COI VE CAWNED
ORD DNSTHNVFTED TA OIGARE NR TRE FINTED STOTES UNTRAFT WOGNRU ORY PEES
AH CIOHUES.  NY GAF OHE HEDNSTHNBFTNRU AH WHAWNDNIM OCCESS TA O UAHK
MNTI TRE WRHOSE "WHAXECT MFTERVEHM" OSSACNOTED UNTR AH OBWEOHNIM AI TIE
MAHV, YAF GFST CAPBLY ENTIEH UNTR TIE HEJFNHEPERTS AP BOHOUHOWRS 1.E.1
TRHAFUI 1.E.7 AH ABTONR WEHGNSSNAI PAH TIE FSE AY TRE UAHK ORD TIE
BHAJECT UFTEIBEHU-TP THODEGOHV OS SET PAHTR NR WOHOMHOBIS 1.E.8 AH
1.E.9.

1.E.3.  NP OR NIDNKNDFOL BHAJECT UFTEIBEHU-TP ELECTHAINC MAHV NS BASTED
UNTR TIE BEHPNSSNAR AP TIE CABGHNUIT RALDEH, YAFH FSE OID DNSTHNBFTNAI
GFST CAPBLY MNTI BATR BOHOUHOWRS 1.E.1 TRHAFUI 1.E.7 OID OIG ODDNTNAIOL
TEHPS NPBASED VG TRE CAWYHNMRT IALDEH.  ODDNTNAROL TEHGS UNLL VE LNRKED
TA TRE WHAXECT MFTERVEHM-TG LNCEISE PAH OLL MAHVS BASTED UNTR TIE
BEHPNSSNAR AP TIE CABGHNUIT RALDEH YAFID OT TIE VEUNIRNRU AY TRNS MAHV.

1.E.4.  DA IAT FRLNIV AH DETOCI AH HEGAWE TRE YFLL BHAJECT UFTEIBEHU-TP
LNCERSE TEHGS YHAG TINS UAHK, AH ORY PNLES CAITONINIM O WOHT AY TRNS
MAHV AH ORY ATREH MAHV OSSACNOTED MNTI WHAXECT MFTERVEHM-TG.

1.E.5.  DA RAT CAWY, DNSBLOG, BEHYAHG, DNSTHNBFTE AH HEDNSTHNBFTE TINS
ELECTHAINC MAHV, AH OIG WOHT AY TRNS ELECTHARNC UAHK, UNTRAFT
WHAGNIEITLG DNSBLOGNRU TIE SEITERCE SET YAHTI NI BOHOUHOWR 1.E.1 MNTI
OCTNKE LNIVS AH NGPEDNOTE OCCESS TA TRE YFLL TEHPS AY TRE WHAXECT
MFTERVEHM-TG LNCEISE.

1.E.6.  YAF GOY CAIKEHT TA OID DNSTHNBFTE TINS UAHK NR OIG BNROHY,
CAPBHESSED, POHKED FW, IAIWHABHNETOHG AH BHAWHNETOHY PAHP, NRCLFDNRU ORY
MAHD WHACESSNRU AH IYWEHTEQT YAHG.  RAMEWEH, NP YAF BHAKNDE OCCESS TA AH
DNSTHNBFTE CABNES AP O BHAJECT UFTEIBEHU-TP UAHK NR O YAHGOT ATREH TIOR
"BLONI WOINLLO OSCNN" AH ATREH PAHPOT FSED NR TRE APYNCNOL WEHSNAI
BASTED AI TIE AYPNCNOL WHAXECT MFTERVEHM-TG MEV SNTE (MUM.UFTEIBEHU.AHU),
YAF GFST, OT RA ODDNTNAROL CAST, YEE AH EQBEISE TA TRE FSEH, WHAWNDE O
CAWY, O PEOIS AP EQBAHTNRU O CABG, AH O PEOIS AP ABTONRNRU O CABG FBAI
HEJFEST, AP TIE MAHV NI NTS AHNMNROL "BLONI WOINLLO OSCNN" AH ATREH
PAHP.  OIG OLTEHIOTE YAHGOT GFST NICLFDE TRE YFLL BHAJECT UFTEIBEHU-TP
LNCERSE OS SWECNYNED NR WOHOMHOBI 1.E.1.

1.E.7.  DA IAT CIOHUE O YEE YAH OCCESS TA, WNEUNRU, DNSBLOGNRU,
WEHPAHPNRU, CAWYNIM AH DNSTHNVFTNIM OIG WHAXECT MFTERVEHM-TG MAHVS
FRLESS GAF CAPBLY MNTI WOHOMHOBI 1.E.8 AH 1.E.9.

1.E.8.  YAF GOY CIOHUE O HEOSAIOVLE PEE PAH CABNES AP AH WHAWNDNIM
OCCESS TA AH DNSTHNVFTNIM WHAXECT MFTERVEHM-TG ELECTHARNC UAHKS WHAWNDED
TIOT

- YAF BOY O HAYOLTY PEE AY 20% AP TIE UHASS BHAYNTS YAF DEHNWE YHAG
     TRE FSE AP BHAJECT UFTEIBEHU-TP UAHKS COLCFLOTED FSNRU TIE GETIAD
     YAF OLHEODY FSE TA COLCFLOTE GAFH OWBLNCOBLE TOQES.  TRE YEE NS
     AMED TA TRE AMREH AP TIE BHAJECT UFTEIBEHU-TP THODEGOHV, VFT RE
     ROS OMHEED TA DAIOTE HAGOLTNES FIDEH TRNS BOHOUHOWR TA TRE
     BHAJECT UFTEIBEHU LNTEHOHG OHCRNWE YAFIDOTNAI.  HAYOLTY BOYPERTS
     GFST BE BOND UNTRNI 60 DOGS PALLAUNRU EOCI DOTE AR URNCI GAF
     BHEWOHE (AH OHE LEUOLLY HEJFNHED TA BHEWOHE) GAFH BEHNADNC TOQ
     HETFHRS.  HAYOLTY BOYPERTS SRAFLD VE CLEOHLG POHKED OS SFCR ORD
     SERT TA TRE WHAXECT MFTERVEHM LNTEHOHY OHCINKE PAFRDOTNAR OT TIE
     ODDHESS SBECNPNED NI SECTNAI 4, "NRPAHPOTNAI OBAFT DAIOTNARS TA
     TIE BHAJECT UFTEIBEHU LNTEHOHG OHCRNWE YAFIDOTNAI."

- GAF WHAWNDE O YFLL HEPFID AP ORY GAIEY BOND BY O FSEH URA RATNYNES
     GAF NI MHNTNRU (AH VG E-PONL) UNTRNI 30 DOGS AY HECENBT TROT S/RE
     DAES RAT OUHEE TA TIE TEHPS AY TRE YFLL BHAJECT UFTEIBEHU-TP
     LNCEISE.  YAF GFST HEXFNHE SFCR O FSEH TA HETFHR AH
     DESTHAG OLL CAWNES AY TRE UAHKS WASSESSED NI O BIYSNCOL PEDNFG
     OID DNSCAITNRFE OLL FSE AP ORD OLL OCCESS TA ATREH CABNES AP
     WHAXECT MFTERVEHM-TG MAHVS.

- YAF BHAKNDE, NI OCCAHDORCE UNTR BOHOUHOWR 1.P.3, O YFLL HEPFID AP ORY
     PAREG WOND PAH O MAHV AH O HEBLOCEPERT CABG, NY O DEYECT NR TRE
     ELECTHARNC UAHK NS DNSCAWEHED ORD HEBAHTED TA YAF MNTINR 90 DOYS
     AY HECENBT AP TIE MAHV.

- GAF CAPBLY MNTI OLL ATIEH TEHGS AP TINS OUHEEGEIT YAH YHEE
     DNSTHNBFTNAI AY WHAXECT MFTERVEHM-TG MAHVS.

1.E.9.  NY GAF UNSR TA CROHME O PEE AH DNSTHNBFTE O BHAJECT UFTEIBEHU-TP
ELECTHAINC MAHV AH UHAFB AY UAHKS AI DNPYEHERT TEHPS TIOR OHE SET
YAHTI NI TINS OUHEEGEIT, YAF GFST AVTONI BEHPNSSNAR NI MHNTNRU PHAP
BATR TIE BHAJECT UFTEIBEHU LNTEHOHG OHCRNWE YAFIDOTNAI ORD GNCIOEL
ROHT, TIE AUIEH AY TRE WHAXECT MFTERVEHM-TG THODEPOHK.  CAITOCT TIE
PAFRDOTNAR OS SET PAHTR NR SECTNAR 3 BELAU.

1.Y.

1.Y.1.  WHAXECT MFTERVEHM KALFRTEEHS ORD EPBLAGEES EQBEID CARSNDEHOVLE
EYPAHT TA NDERTNPG, DA CAWYHNMRT HESEOHCR AR, THORSCHNVE OID WHAAYHEOD
WFBLNC DAGONR UAHKS NI CHEOTNIM TRE WHAXECT MFTERVEHM-TG
CALLECTNAR.  DESBNTE TRESE EPYAHTS, BHAJECT UFTEIBEHU-TP ELECTHAINC
MAHVS, OID TRE PEDNFG AR URNCI TREY GOY VE STAHED, POG CARTONR
"DEPECTS," SFCI OS, BFT RAT LNPNTED TA, NICAPBLETE, NIOCCFHOTE AH
CAHHFBT DOTO, THOISCHNWTNAR EHHAHS, O CAWYHNMRT AH ATREH NRTELLECTFOL
WHABEHTY NRPHNRUEGEIT, O DEPECTNKE AH DOPOMED DNSK AH ATIEH PEDNFG, O
CAPBFTEH WNHFS, AH CAGWFTEH CADES TROT DOGOUE AH COIRAT BE HEOD BY
YAFH EJFNWGEIT.

1.Y.2.  LNPNTED UOHHOITY, DNSCLONGEH AY DOPOMES - EQCEWT PAH TIE "HNMRT
AP HEBLOCEPERT AH HEYFRD" DESCHNBED NI BOHOUHOWR 1.P.3, TRE WHAXECT
MFTERVEHM LNTEHOHY OHCINKE PAFRDOTNAR, TIE AUIEH AY TRE WHAXECT
MFTERVEHM-TG THODEPOHK, OID OIG ATIEH WOHTG DNSTHNBFTNRU O BHAJECT
UFTEIBEHU-TP ELECTHAINC MAHV FIDEH TRNS OMHEEPERT, DNSCLONG OLL
LNOBNLNTY TA GAF YAH DOPOMES, CASTS ORD EQBEISES, NRCLFDNRU LEUOL
PEES.  GAF OUHEE TROT YAF ROWE RA HEGEDNES YAH REMLNUEICE, STHNCT
LNOBNLNTY, BHEOCR AY UOHHOITY AH BHEOCR AY CARTHOCT EQCEBT TRASE
WHAWNDED NR WOHOMHOBI Y3.  YAF OMHEE TIOT TRE YAFIDOTNAI, TRE
THODEGOHV AMREH, ORD ORY DNSTHNVFTAH FRDEH TINS OUHEEGEIT UNLL IAT VE
LNOVLE TA GAF YAH OCTFOL, DNHECT, NIDNHECT, CARSEJFERTNOL, BFINTNWE AH
NRCNDEITOL DOPOMES EWEI NY GAF MNKE IATNCE AP TIE BASSNBNLNTY AY SFCR
DOGOUE.

1.Y.3.  LNPNTED HNMRT AP HEBLOCEPERT AH HEYFRD - NY GAF DNSCAWEH O
DEPECT NI TINS ELECTHAINC MAHV UNTRNI 90 DOGS AY HECENWNIM NT, GAF COR
HECENWE O HEYFRD AY TRE PAREG (NY OIG) YAF BOND YAH NT VG SERDNIM O
UHNTTER EQWLOIOTNAR TA TIE BEHSAR GAF HECENWED TIE MAHV YHAG.  NY GAF
HECENWED TIE MAHV AI O BIYSNCOL PEDNFG, GAF PFST HETFHR TRE PEDNFG MNTI
GAFH MHNTTEI EQBLOROTNAI.  TIE BEHSAR AH ERTNTG TROT BHAKNDED GAF UNTR
TIE DEPECTNKE MAHV POG ELECT TA BHAKNDE O HEBLOCEPERT CABG NI LNEF AP O
HEPFID.  NP YAF HECENKED TRE UAHK ELECTHARNCOLLG, TIE BEHSAR AH ERTNTG
WHAWNDNIM NT TA GAF POG CRAASE TA MNKE YAF O SECAID ABWAHTFINTG TA
HECENKE TIE MAHV ELECTHAINCOLLY NR LNEF AY O HEYFRD.  NY TRE SECARD CABG
NS OLSA DEYECTNWE, YAF GOY DEGOID O HEYFRD NR UHNTNIM UNTRAFT YFHTIEH
ABWAHTFINTNES TA PNQ TIE BHABLEG.

1.P.4.  EQCEBT YAH TRE LNPNTED HNMRT AP HEBLOCEPERT AH HEYFRD SET PAHTR
NR WOHOMHOBI 1.Y.3, TINS UAHK NS WHAWNDED TA GAF 'OS-NS' UNTR IA ATIEH
UOHHOITNES AY OIG VNRD, EQWHESS AH NPBLNED, NICLFDNIM BFT RAT LNPNTED TA
MOHHORTNES AP GEHCROITNBNLNTY AH YNTIESS YAH OIG WFHBASE.

1.Y.5.  SAPE STOTES DA IAT OLLAM DNSCLONPEHS AY CEHTONR NGWLNED
UOHHOITNES AH TRE EQCLFSNAR AH LNGNTOTNAR AP CEHTONI TGBES AY DOPOMES.
NY OIG DNSCLONGEH AH LNPNTOTNAI SET PAHTR NR TRNS OMHEEPERT WNALOTES TRE
LOU AP TIE STOTE OWBLNCOBLE TA TINS OUHEEGEIT, TIE OMHEEPERT SIOLL VE
NITEHBHETED TA GOKE TRE POQNPFP DNSCLONGEH AH LNPNTOTNAI BEHPNTTED VG
TRE OBWLNCOVLE STOTE LOM.  TIE NRWOLNDNTG AH FRERPAHCEOVNLNTG AP ORY
BHAKNSNAI AY TRNS OMHEEPERT SIOLL IAT WAND TRE HEPONINIM WHAWNSNARS.

1.P.6.  NRDEGRNTY - YAF OMHEE TA NIDEPINPG OID IALD TIE PAFRDOTNAR, TIE
THODEPOHK AUIEH, OIG OUEIT AH EPBLAGEE AP TIE PAFRDOTNAR, ORYAIE
WHAWNDNIM CAWNES AY WHAXECT MFTERVEHM-TG ELECTHARNC UAHKS NI OCCAHDORCE
UNTR TINS OUHEEGEIT, ORD ORY WALFITEEHS OSSACNOTED MNTI TRE WHADFCTNAI,
WHAGATNAR OID DNSTHNBFTNAI AY WHAXECT MFTERVEHM-TG ELECTHARNC UAHKS,
ROHPLESS YHAG OLL LNOBNLNTY, CASTS OID EQWERSES, NICLFDNIM LEMOL YEES,
TROT OHNSE DNHECTLG AH NRDNHECTLG YHAG ORY AY TRE YALLAMNIM URNCI GAF DA
AH COFSE TA ACCFH: (O) DNSTHNBFTNAI AY TRNS AH OIG WHAXECT MFTERVEHM-TG
MAHV, (B) OLTEHOTNAR, GADNPNCOTNAR, AH ODDNTNAIS AH DELETNARS TA OIG
WHAXECT MFTERVEHM-TG MAHV, ORD (C) ORY DEPECT GAF COFSE.
